Sleeps in a small back room when she sleeps at all — the run repeatedly shows her awake at hours that suggest chronic short-sleep, a residual hyperarousal signature consistent with the C-PTSD reading.

**The apprentice — Darcy Lewis.** The choice of Darcy as live-in research-assistant / apprentice is itself behavioral data. Darcy is *deliberately ordinary* — unpowered, irreverent, scholastically credentialed but practically uninitiated. Subject is, for the first time, mentoring *down* a steep slope rather than across (Pietro, Vision) or up (Harkness, Magneto). The choice constructs a relationship in which she cannot defer or transfer dependency; she must be the adult. The diagnostic significance is large: the enmeshed/idealizing attachment pattern is being *practiced against* in real time. Darcy is also chosen — and one suspects this is conscious — because Darcy is *not* easily impressed and *will* push back, which neutralizes subject's deferential default.

**Casework.** Per the run: she serves a young witch fleeing an abusive coven; a man whose dead wife's ghost is trapped in a record; a community displaced by an interdimensional fracture; a multiversal variant of herself in crisis; the witches of Salem revisited. The pattern across cases is *strikingly consistent*: she intervenes at minimum power, refuses several requests that would require reality-edit-scale operations, and explicitly speaks the principle aloud at least twice — "There are problems you cannot solve by making them not have happened." This is *the axiom of her disorder, externally negated.* It is, in clinical terms, the cognitive restructuring step of grief therapy, performed in public, weekly, as professional practice.

**Multiversal incident.** The arc in which she encounters variants of herself (some monstrous, some saintly, one mid-decompensation) is the most overt psychological work in the run. She does not destroy the monstrous variants; she does not exalt the saintly ones; she *speaks to them as past and possible selves* and lets them remain. This is the integration project literalized — she is being shown what she was and what she might still become and is asked to hold both without flinching. She holds.

**Power signature shift.** Across this period the chaos-magic discharge takes on observable discipline — directed, sigil-bound, often spoken with verbal component, more frequently *containing* than *unleashing.* This is not power-loss; it is power-organization. The signature now reads less like a storm-front and more like a practitioner's craft. The Aaron-era retcon that frames her as a witch (heritage, lineage) rather than purely a mutant-hex-caster is, regardless of cosmological merit, *useful to her treatment*: it gives her a tradition to belong to and a discipline to inherit, rather than an anomaly to apologize for.

---

## 3. *Contest of Chaos* and the Reunion with Pietro (2023–24)

The *Contest of Chaos* summer arc — a series of one-shots running through the Annuals — places subject opposite a fragmenting cosmic threat that requires her to draft her brother into the work. The reunion is documented across *Scarlet Witch & Quicksilver* (Orlando, 2024), and the file should mark it carefully because it is *the rewriting of the most enmeshed relationship in her record.*

Behavior at first contact with Pietro in this arc: she does not idealize him; she does not capitulate to him; she also does not avoid him. She *negotiates* with him, in plain language, about how they will work together — what each will and will not be permitted to do, what triggers each must respect in the other. This is unprecedented in the file. For sixty years the twin-bond has operated on permeable affective boundaries, with Pietro's distress reliably overriding her judgment. Here she holds her own perimeter while remaining warm. She also, notably, asks him for help rather than receiving it as an unsolicited intervention — a small inversion that, behaviorally, repositions her as the agent and him as the resource.

Pietro's reciprocal posture has shifted as well (post-his own years of solo-title work and parenthood with Luna), but the file's interest is in *her* — and the data is that the enmeshment, while it has not dissolved, has been *renegotiated into something closer to ordinary sibling adulthood.* This is one of the slowest-developing therapeutic outcomes in her record and one of the most significant.

---

## 4. Avengers Tenure under MacKay (2023–) and Operational Reliability

Subject rejoins the active Avengers in the MacKay run, on terms she sets: she lives at the Emporium, not the Tower; she answers operational calls but maintains civilian practice; she will not be team chair and declines the role twice on-panel. The terms themselves are diagnostic — for the first time in her record she is *negotiating her availability* rather than being absorbed by the team structure.

Combat behavior in the MacKay run is notably *measured.* She fields the Tribulation Events alongside the new lineup; she handles the Ashen Combine sequence; she is present for the early *Blood Hunt* (Cates, 2024) vampire-incursion crisis. Across these engagements the behavioral signature is consistent: she opens with containment-class magic (shields, redirection, probability-dampening of incoming fire), escalates only when teammates are at lethal risk, and *withdraws* power output as soon as the threshold lowers. This is the operational expression of the affect-regulation work the Emporium period has been training. The historical pattern — power output coupled to affective storm, no buffer between feeling and acting — has been partially decoupled by *practice.* Not eliminated. Partially decoupled.

Teammate-relations data: she is observed eating with the team after operations (a small somatic-social marker — historically she has refused communal meals after combat); she sits, in one panel, next to Captain Marvel in silence for a long beat that the art reads as comfort rather than tension. With the newer/younger members she is *immediately* maternal in the patient, non-engulfing way she is with Darcy — not the over-attached maternalism of the constructed-children era but the steady availability of a person who has decided to be reliable. With Vision (in his current iteration, post the various dismantlements and reconstructions) she is — and the file notes this with the appropriate care — courteous, distant, and visibly grieved. They do not work the relationship; they coexist. This is *also* progress; prior eras would have forced a reconciliation or staged a re-rupture. The current posture is *bearable grief held without action.*

---

## 5. Mutant-Line Aftershocks: From Krakoa Through *Fall of X* into *From the Ashes*

The collapse of Krakoa and the Orchis sequence in *Fall of X* (2023–24) reaches her tangentially rather than centrally. She is no longer a Krakoan resident; she did not benefit from the resurrection protocols in the same way; her relationship to the mutant nation was always complicated by the "No more mutants" history. During the *Hellfire Gala 2023* massacre and its aftermath she is observed providing magical triage to survivors and, separately, locating displaced young mutants and routing them to safer ground. She does not weigh in publicly on the political collapse. The restraint is itself the data.

Into *From the Ashes* (2024–) she maintains a working relationship with the post-Krakoa X-formations — Magneto's late-period return and his own attempts at amends create an oblique parallel to her own arc that the writers have, so far, declined to overstate. She visits him; the visits are short; the conversations are quiet. There is no reconciliation scene and the absence of one is, for dossier purposes, *correct* — she is no longer rehearsing the father-question for a reader's catharsis. She has metabolized it into a relationship she can have, in small doses, without losing herself.

---

## 6. The Children — Current Status

Wiccan / Billy Kaplan is openly her son and the relationship is documented as functional, regular, and warm. They are observed having dinner together with Hulkling; she is present at significant moments in their married life; she is referenced by Billy as "my mom" without qualifier. Speed / Tommy Shepherd remains the more complicated relationship — characteristically restless, characteristically harder to land — but contact is maintained and the breach is no longer total.

The diagnostic point: the grief that drove every catastrophic event in her record from 1989 onward is *not gone* but is now *held inside a relationship rather than against the absence of one.* The wound is no longer the void; the wound is the scar of the void, with the children present to make the scar bearable. This is the closest thing to *resolved complicated grief* her file can document, and the literature (Bryant 2024) would call this the consolidation phase — symptoms diminished, the loss integrated rather than denied or erased, the bond with the deceased/recovered restructured into a sustainable internal representation.

---

## 7. Current Somatic and Behavioral Baseline (Surveillance-Grade Detail)

- **Sleep:** Short and irregular. Chronic 4–5 hour pattern with daytime micro-naps in the shop's back room. Hyperarousal residue.
- **Diet:** Light during work hours (coffee, bread, fruit on the counter). Proper evening meals — frequently Romani dishes she cooks herself (sarma, ciorbă), occasionally Latin American dishes inherited from her maternal line per the modernized origin, more rarely takeout when fatigued. Eats with company when company is present; does not refuse the table.
- **Dress:** Off-duty: layered dark fabrics, long skirts or wide trousers, the recurring deep-red coat. Costume-grade: the crimson coat-and-headpiece silhouette, worn now less reflexively — she changes into it deliberately, often in a back room rather than mid-action.
- **Hair:** Worn long again post-resurrection, in the dark wavy mahogany-auburn fall that is her constant signature; she pins it up when working magic at the bench, lets it down when receiving clients, ties it back tightly when on operations.
- **Gait:** Slow, deliberate, ground-conscious. She walks with attention to where she places her feet — a small grounding ritual, consistent with someone trained out of dissociation.
- **Hands:** The chaos-energy aura at her fingertips is observable at near-baseline now (a faint red flicker rather than the older brilliant corona), pulsing slightly with breath. She rubs her thumb across her fingers when thinking — a recurrent tic across runs.
- **Speech:** Lower register than the early-record canon, cadence slower, Sokovian / Romani-inflected English with occasional code-switching into Spanish (per the modernized maternal origin) when speaking to clients in their first language. She has been observed using the diminutive form of names — a tenderness-marker — with apprentices, children, and the wounded.
- **Routes:** Predictable. Shop to coffee cart on the corner (the same vendor, by name); shop to the small park three blocks west where she sits on the same bench (lefthand end, facing the playground at a deliberate distance); shop to the Avengers' downtown transport node when called. The route-set is *small and habitual* — the surveillance signature of a person whose life is, for the first time, organized around a place she intends to stay.
- **Reading:** Grimoires, yes, but also contemporary poetry (a volume by Ada Limón observed on the nightstand in one panel; a Lorca in Spanish on the counter in another) and, telling, books on grief — secular and clinical. She is, in the literal sense, reading the literature on her own condition.

---

## 8. Vulnerabilities — Current

The recent period has consolidated remarkable adaptive gains. The vulnerabilities that remain are *specific and known*:

1. **Sudden loss-cue concerning the children.** Threats to Billy or Tommy remain capable of rapid escalation up the stress ladder. The difference now is that she has *people* — Darcy, Pietro, the team — who can interrupt the climb before it reaches catastrophic decompensation. The vulnerability is not eliminated; it is *socially buffered.*
2. **Epistemic violation.** Any actor attempting to gaslight her, alter her memory, or assert that her perception of reality is wrong remains the fastest known route to escalation. Her history with Harkness, Immortus, and Doom has trained a *near-allergic* response to this class of intrusion. She has, in the recent record, snapped at well-meaning teammates who attempted to "manage" her perception of an event — a small but useful warning to operators.
3. **Magneto's mortality.** Whenever the file's information indicates he is dying or dead (a frequent state for him), her stress markers elevate. The father-question is metabolized, not gone.
4. **Power-intoxication threshold.** If pressed into a sustained high-output operation (a planetary-scale crisis, an extended siege), the old coupling between affect and discharge can reassert. The Emporium discipline is robust at retail scale; it has not been stress-tested in a *House of M*-class event since the reorganization. Operators should regard a sustained, escalating engagement as the principal modern risk scenario.
5. **The unknown sibling/family revelations.** The retcon-volatility of her own origin (mutant, witch, Romani, the modernized Afro-Latina maternal line, the Magneto-paternity oscillation) means that any new revelation about her biological identity has historically been destabilizing. She is, in the recent run, demonstrating better tolerance for ambiguity here than at any prior point — but a sudden, weaponized revelation remains a known vector.

---

## 9. Current Status — Summary

As of the most recent entries in the file: subject is alive, resident in lower Manhattan, in active operational status with the Avengers on terms she has set, running a public-facing magical practice with one apprentice, in restored relationship with both of her sons (one closely, one intermittently), in renegotiated relationship with her twin brother, in quiet and limited relationship with her father, in courteous and grieved distance from her former husband. She is sleeping poorly, eating adequately, walking small habitual routes, reading grief literature and Spanish poetry, and discharging her power at a fraction of her demonstrated ceiling. She is, by every behavioral marker the file can register, *the most integrated she has been across sixty years of record.*

This is not the same as *well.* The Bryant criteria would still register prolonged grief in subclinical or low-clinical range; the C-PTSD signatures are still present in the sleep pattern and the hyperarousal; the dissociative vulnerabilities remain accessible under sufficient pressure. What has changed is that she is, for the first time, *practicing the conditions of her own recovery* as a daily discipline rather than encountering them as emergencies. The omnipotent-reparative drive that built constructed children and rewrote a world is now metered out in shop hours and house calls. The grief that had nowhere smaller to go has, finally, been given somewhere to go that is not the world.

The file should note this with the appropriate weight. It is rare for a sixty-year longitudinal record to register a genuine turn. This one has. The operational implication for any party tracking, allying with, or opposing the subject is the same: *she is no longer principally a risk to herself or to reality. She is principally a resource — to those she has decided to serve, and to herself.* The vector of her life has, after a very long time, turned from catastrophe toward care.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, retrospective canonical reconstruction, and inference where direct medical documentation is absent (which is nearly always — the subject has been examined by a credentialed physician on perhaps a dozen recorded occasions in sixty years of public life, and most of those by Henry McCoy, Henry Pym, or Tony Stark in field-medic capacity rather than clinical settings).*

---

## I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

The subject presents as a young adult woman of mixed Afro-Latina heritage, in the late twenties bracket by current chronology, of average height and slender-athletic build that has remained essentially constant across her published existence. Warm brown skin showing no chronic dermatological pathology beyond intermittent stress-related flares (small eczematous patches at the inner wrists and behind the left ear, observed during periods of acute decompensation; resolves without treatment in remission). Long dark wavy hair, mahogany-auburn at the depth, kept long across nearly every era — the few times it has been cut short (briefly in the mid-Force Works period, briefly post-*Disassembled* in psychiatric custody) the recovery to length has been rapid and appears mildly accelerated, consistent with the low-grade somatic enhancement that accompanies her magical baseline. Expressive dark eyes; sclera occasionally noted to flush reddish at moments of acute power-discharge (vascular phenomenon, not pigmentary).

Cardiopulmonary: unremarkable on every recorded auscultation. Resting pulse logs from Avengers infirmary intake (Pym, Stark) cluster in the high fifties — athletic range, despite her not maintaining a formal training regimen comparable to Romanoff or Barton. Hypothesis: the chaos-magic somatic envelope confers a low-grade autonomic optimization analogous to but not equivalent to mutant baseline enhancement.

No documented allergies. No chronic medication regimen has ever stuck; multiple psychiatric trials (see §VIII) have been attempted across decades and none have been continued beyond a few weeks, either because the subject discontinues, because the power-set neutralizes the pharmacokinetics (suspected but unproven), or because she is removed from the clinical setting by crisis.

Dental: unremarkable. Vision: unremarkable. No corrective lenses. No hearing complaint. Menstrual history not in record except by inference: the two pregnancies of 1985–86 were not preceded by reported fertility workup, and the post-pregnancy somatic state was not followed up — a profound omission that the file flags as iatrogenic neglect and not as absence-of-pathology.

---

## II. CHILDHOOD AND ADOLESCENT INJURIES (RECONSTRUCTED)

The subject's pre-Brotherhood medical history exists only in fragments and across competing retcons (the Maximoff twins raised by the Romani Maximoff family in Transia; the High Evolutionary recombinant origin; the recent witch-heritage frame). What is consistent across versions:

- **The mob attack, Transia, adolescence.** Pursued by villagers who identified her as a witch, the subject sustained injuries the specifics of which are never enumerated — bruising, abrasions, possible concussion implied by the dazed presentation when Magneto extracts her. *No medical follow-up.* The lasting somatic record of this event is not the bruise but the *startle response to crowds* that persists across her entire adult life: in any panel where she is in a market, a street demonstration, or a pressing audience, her shoulders elevate, her chin drops, her left hand drifts toward her right wrist in a self-soothing clasp. This is the body remembering what was never clinically attended.
- **Malnutrition, presumptive, in the refugee/itinerant period.** Her build in the earliest published appearances is notably thin, and Lee/Kirby art renders her slightly hollow-cheeked. No record of refeeding or nutritional rehabilitation. Whatever deficit existed was resolved organically within her first year with the Avengers; the subject ate ravenously at the Mansion in the early Roy Thomas issues — a behavioral marker noted but never clinically interpreted.

---

## III. POWER-RELATED PHYSIOLOGY — THE CHRONIC CONDITION

Treat the power-set itself as a medical condition for purposes of this file, because it is the single most consequential variable in her health record.

**Mechanism, observable.** Chaos-magic / probability-manipulation / reality-alteration energy is emitted from the hands — most commonly from the palms, sometimes from the fingertips, occasionally from the entire forearm-envelope in high-output states. The faint crimson aura at the hands is the visible quiescent signature; in flight or in casting it intensifies to ribbon-like emissions that follow the gesture. The eyes flash red in high-amplitude casting (vascular flush plus apparent autoluminescence, mechanism unknown).

**Affective coupling.** This is the medically dispositive finding. *Output amplitude tracks affect amplitude.* In subjects with conventional autonomic arousal, anger produces tachycardia and a flushed face; in this subject, anger produces tachycardia, a flushed face, *and a discharge of probability-altering energy.* There is no buffer. This collapses the normal psychological gap between feeling and action and constitutes the single most important fact about her clinical care: *she cannot be treated as if her emotions are private events.* They are not. They are environmental.

**Tolerance, withdrawal, and intoxication.** The power behaves pharmacologically. Sustained high-output (the *Disassembled* and *House of M* episodes, the *Children's Crusade* peak) produces a state observationally indistinguishable from intoxication: pupil dilation, pressured speech (when she speaks at all — more often she goes silent and casts), grandiosity, impaired reality testing, post-event amnesia or fragmentary recall. The "withdrawal" — return to baseline after such episodes — is marked by profound fatigue, depressive collapse, somnolence lasting days, and a temporary apparent reduction in baseline power output that recovers over weeks. This pattern is not described in any standard psychiatric text because no standard psychiatric subject has a power-set. The file treats it as analogous to a substance use disorder where the substance is endogenous.

**Headache pattern.** Across multiple runs (Englehart, Byrne, Robinson) the subject is depicted touching the temples, sometimes the brow ridge — a low-grade headache pattern that correlates with recent high-output casting or with proximity to other reality-warping or magical entities. No imaging has ever been performed.

---

## IV. THE PREGNANCIES AND PERINATAL LOSS (1985–1989)

This is the single most consequential medical event in her record and the one most thoroughly mishandled by every party involved.

**Conception (*Vision and the Scarlet Witch* #3, 1985).** Conception was magical, not coital — the subject and her synthezoid husband cannot reproduce biologically. The mechanism, retroactively understood, was the subject's own chaos magic capturing soul-fragments of Mephisto and gestating them as a wish made flesh. At the time, neither the subject nor her physicians (Pym attended) understood this. The pregnancy presented as a real pregnancy: amenorrhea, morning nausea, abdominal distension on a normal gestational curve, weight gain, breast changes, eventual labor.

**Gestation.** Largely uneventful by report. Pym performed at least one prenatal examination on the West Coast Avengers compound and reported no anomalies. The subject's affect across the pregnancy was the most settled of her entire recorded life — radiant, present, embodied. *This is data.* It tells us that the ordinary somatic experience of carrying and bearing a child was the closest she had ever come to integration. The wish was working.

**Parturition.** Twin delivery, Thomas and William Maximoff, attended by Pym in the field hospital configuration of the Compound. The labor was reportedly difficult — the subject's vitals dropped, she lost consciousness twice — but recoverable. No surgical intervention. The infants presented as normal-term healthy twins.

**Post-partum.** A period of intense bonding, breastfeeding, the ordinary somatic intimacy of new motherhood. The subject's affect remained settled. The power output during this period was the *lowest* of her recorded adult life — the wish, having become flesh, no longer needed casting. This is the most powerful evidence in the file for the *omnipotent-reparation drive as the engine of her catastrophic discharges*: when the drive is satisfied, the discharges stop.

**The reabsorption (*Avengers West Coast* #51–52, 1989).** Master Pandemonium revealed the children to be soul-fragments of Mephisto; they were reabsorbed into him on-panel. The somatic and psychological injury was immediate and extreme. The subject collapsed, was non-responsive for hours, then entered a fugue. *No obstetric follow-up was ever performed.* No one examined her uterus to see whether the pregnancy-and-birth-trace was still present in her body or whether it had vanished with the children. No one drew blood. No one asked her what she felt.

**The Harkness mnestic intervention.** Within days of the reabsorption, Agatha Harkness — the subject's magical mentor and a trusted figure — performed a memory-wipe of the children. This must be documented in this file under "surgeries," because that is what it was: a surgical excision of a content from the subject's mind, performed without informed consent of a kind that could meaningfully be given by a person in acute traumatic shock. The intervention was framed, then and later, as a mercy. It was malpractice. In any clinical analog, a therapist who responded to a patient's catastrophic loss by *erasing the patient's memory of the lost objects* would be stripped of licensure.

The consequences are catalogued throughout this dossier. The relevant medical point is that the iatrogenic injury and the original perinatal loss are *two distinct injuries*, the second compounding the first, and both unhealed.

---

## V. ACUTE INJURIES AND TRAUMATIC EVENTS — A CATALOG

The subject's combat record across sixty years comprises hundreds of incidents; only those of medical significance are listed.

- **Multiple hex-feedback episodes (Englehart era).** Early in her training with Harkness, miscast hexes rebounded somatically — knockdowns, scorch marks on the palms, transient blindness once. All resolved without intervention.
- **Skull fracture, suspected, *Avengers* #181 (1979).** Blow taken from Graviton; helmet protected the cranium but the dazed presentation post-event suggests concussion. Untreated.
- **Multiple combat-related lacerations and fractures across the West Coast Avengers run.** The subject's combat style is *standoff* — she casts at range — and her injury rate is correspondingly lower than the team baseline. The injuries that do occur tend to be from being blindsided or from environmental hazards (collapsing structures, fire) rather than from sustained melee.
- **Mind-control episodes — Immortus, *Avengers West Coast* #51–52 and subsequent.** Not somatic but neurological in the broad sense. The subject's autonomy was overridden for extended periods. The bodily memory of this — the sensation of one's own hands acting without one's volition — is a trauma the subject has described, in late-period dialogue, as *worse than being struck.*
- **The *Disassembled* episode (2004).** No documented somatic injury to the subject during the catastrophic event; the injuries were to others, by her hand. Post-event, on Genosha in Magneto's custody, she presented as catatonic-with-intermittent-lucidity for weeks. No imaging, no labs, no formal psychiatric admission. *Charles Xavier's telepathic intervention was the only "treatment" attempted, and it failed.*
- **The *House of M* episode (2005).** Sustained high-output casting for the duration of the constructed reality (subjective months, objective days). The post-collapse somatic state was again profound fatigue, catatonia, and dissociation. The subject vanished from the record for months thereafter.
- **The Doom episode (*Avengers: The Children's Crusade*, 2010–12).** Channeled by Doctor Doom, then briefly possessed by the Life-Force itself. Burns to the costume and faint thermal injury to the palms documented; the deeper injury was the *third agency-violation by a powerful man* in her recorded life, and the cumulative psychological cost is non-trivial.
- **Death, *Children's Crusade* #9 (2012).** Killed by the Wasp's bio-stinger after a brief possession sequence; resurrected within the same arc by the chaos magic she carried. The subjective experience of dying, while not articulated in the text, is consistent with later dissociative episodes in which she has reported "remembering being nowhere."
- **Death and resurrection, *Trial of Magneto* (2021).** Self-resurrection mechanism (the Wanda backup, the Krakoan complication, the ritual return). Each death adds to the dissociative load and to the subject's *foreshortened sense of future* — the conviction, never quite spoken, that she will not be alive in any conventional sense for very long.
- **Various magical burns, hexes turned inward, blowback during teaching (Orlando run).** Minor; resolved.

---

## VI. TRANSFORMATIONS, POSSESSIONS, AND BODILY INTRUSIONS

Categorized separately because their psychological weight exceeds any specific somatic finding.

- **Chthon possession, multiple episodes** — most clearly in the original *Avengers* #185–187 (1979, "The Yesterday Quest"). The Elder God Chthon claimed the subject as a vessel; she was bodily inhabited by an external malevolent intelligence. The somatic markers during possession included voice change, postural change, and a different power signature. *The subject had no memory of significant portions of the episode.* This is the prototype of every subsequent agency-violation in her record.
- **Immortus's manipulations**, recurrent across the Byrne and post-Byrne West Coast years.
- **Doctor Doom's channeling** (*Children's Crusade*).
- **The Life Force / Cosmic Cube-adjacent intrusions** in various crossover events.
- **The transient nexus-being augmentations** in the Bendis era.

Each of these constitutes a *bodily occupation* — the subject's body was used by an external will. The cumulative psychological cost is the trauma of *not owning one's own physical envelope*, and it is the etiological substrate of her recurrent dissociative episodes.

---

## VII. THE WHITE VISION DISMANTLING (1989) — SECONDARY MEDICAL EVENT

Not an injury to the subject's body, but a medical event for her in the systemic sense: her husband was disassembled, his memories and personality stripped, and rebuilt as an emotionless white construct. The subject witnessed this. The somatic responses recorded across the *Vision Quest* arc include tremor, tearful collapse, periods of muteness, and a marked increase in baseline power-signature instability — *her body responded to his dismantling as if she herself had been dismantled.* This is medically significant as evidence of the *psychosomatic enmeshment* between subject and primary attachment figure: she does not have firm bodily boundaries against the suffering of those she loves.

---

## VIII. SUBSTANCES, PHARMACOLOGY, ATTEMPTED TREATMENTS

- **No alcohol use disorder.** Social drinking documented (wine at Avengers galas, the occasional drink with Vision in domestic scenes). Never to excess on the record.
- **No illicit substance use.** No tobacco. No cannabis. No stimulants.
- **Caffeine: moderate.** The subject drinks coffee. In domestic scenes (the Englehart-Leonardi maxiseries especially) she is reliably depicted with a mug in the morning; the preparation is European-style, strong, often unsweetened.
- **Psychiatric pharmacology — attempted.** During the post-*Disassembled* custody on Genosha, no documented regimen. During the post-*House of M* recovery, no documented regimen. *This is the single most damning gap in her medical care.* A patient with documented recurrent psychotic episodes, prolonged grief disorder, and complex PTSD has never, on the record, received a sustained trial of an antipsychotic, an SSRI, an SNRI, or any mood stabilizer. The reasons are partly institutional (the Avengers do not have a staff psychiatrist), partly characterological (the subject distrusts pharmacology — a residue, perhaps, of the Harkness intervention and the lesson that what is done to her mind is rarely for her), and partly mechanistic (suspicion, never confirmed, that her power-envelope alters pharmacokinetics).
- **Magical sedatives and dampers — attempted, multiple occasions.** Stephen Strange has, on at least two recorded occasions, placed magical dampening fields around the subject. These functioned in the short term and were experienced by the subject as *suffocating* — the analogy she has used is being held underwater. The subject does not consent to such interventions a second time without being forced.
- **Power-nullification technology (Genoshan and SHIELD inhibitor collars / fields).** Worn briefly during custodial periods. Subject's response to nullification is profound somatic distress — depersonalization, derealization, a sense of being *amputated.* The power is somatic to her; removing it is felt as removing a limb.

---

## IX. SLEEP, NUTRITION, ROUTINE — THE INFERRED FILE

From the longitudinal panel record, inferred:

- **Sleep architecture: chronically disturbed.** Recurrent nightmares (the children, the mob, Vision being dismantled). Early-morning wakings. Periods of insomnia followed by collapse into long sleeps. No sleep study ever performed.
- **Nutrition: variable.** Cooks competently — Eastern European staples (paprikash, stuffed cabbage, sweet breads) appear in domestic scenes across multiple runs. In acute periods she does not eat; in stable periods she eats well and shares food readily.
- **Activity: irregular.** No formal training regimen. Walks frequently — the long solitary walks in pastoral settings (*Children's Crusade*, the Robinson solo, the Orlando run) are a recurring behavioral motif and serve, observably, as her primary affect-regulation strategy when she has any.
- **Menstrual / reproductive: undocumented post-1989.** A profound gap.
- **Touch: selective.** Comfortable with embrace from Pietro, from her sons in late-period reunions, from Vision when they have been on good terms. Wary of unsolicited physical contact from acquaintances. The wrist-clasp self-soothing gesture noted in §II persists.

---

## X. SYNTHESIS — THE MEDICAL FILE READ AS A WHOLE

What this medical record describes is *a body that has been used hard and cared for poorly.* The subject has been pregnant and bereaved without follow-up, killed and resurrected without debriefing, possessed and emptied and reoccupied without examination, dampened and nullified without consent, medicated never. She has been a patient of no physician for any sustained period of her adult life. Her primary "treatment provider" was a magical mentor who responded to her worst loss by deleting the memory of it; her primary "psychiatric intervention" was a telepath's failed attempt to stabilize a catatonic woman in her father's custody on an island.

The single most important medical fact about Wanda Maximoff is that *her interior states have somatic and environmental consequences without buffer.* The single most important medical failure in her record is that *no one has ever treated her as if that were true.* Every catastrophic discharge in her file is, in part, the predictable consequence of a clinical absence: a woman whose feelings *become weather* was never given anyone with whom she could simply feel.

The body in this file is not broken. It is, in the most clinical sense, *unattended.* The work of late-period integration — the apprentices, the witches helped, the names of the children spoken aloud — is, for the first time on record, the work of a person attending to her own body and her own grief in the absence of anyone qualified to attend with her. It is the beginning of a medical history that finally belongs to her.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF ("SCARLET WITCH")

*A longitudinal mapping of the body the file has watched for sixty years. Power-set is treated here as somatic; the chaos-energy is part of her physiology, not adjunct to it. Where the file records a "tell," it is the tell as it presents on warm brown skin, in dark wavy auburn-mahogany hair, under crimson cloth — and as it moves.*

---

## 1. STANDING BASELINE — THE BODY AT REST

The subject's neutral stance carries weight on the left leg, right knee slightly unlocked, right heel often rising a quarter-inch off the floor in a slow, almost imperceptible bounce. Surveillance footage across decades — the Avengers Mansion atrium, the West Coast compound veranda, the Genoshan terrace, the Westview porch, the cottages of her *Children's Crusade*-era hideaways — shows this same uneven loading. It is the stance of a person who has spent her childhood ready to be moved suddenly by a hand on her elbow.

Shoulders sit forward of the spinal column by perhaps two centimeters more than is ergonomic — a faint protective rounding that opens noticeably when she is teaching (apprentices, the *Scarlet Witch* solo era), and closes again the moment a voice she does not know enters the room. The chin is held low, not down — a half-degree off horizontal, which keeps her sightline grazing the upper periphery of any space she enters. This is reconnaissance behavior, learned early in the Brotherhood years and never unlearned.

The hands, at rest, are almost never at rest. Fingers of the right hand work in small, slow cycles against the pad of the thumb — index, middle, ring, little, return — a counting pattern that surveillance can clock at roughly four to six seconds per cycle in calm state, accelerating to two seconds under arousal. The left hand more often grips: a sleeve cuff, the seam of a coat, a strand of hair near the jaw, the edge of a chair-arm. The grip is *light*, three-finger, never the full fist. The full fist is reserved for the power.

A faint, intermittent reddish haze can be observed at the fingertips and inner wrists in low-light conditions even at full rest — a baseline thermal-visible signature of the chaos-energy that the file logs as her *biometric*. Spectrometry across multiple captures: dim cherry to oxblood, never bright. Brightness escalates with affect.

---

## 2. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

She walks with a long stride for her height — heel-strike pronounced, toe-off quiet — and the hip-roll is slight rather than emphatic, suggesting she was taught at some early point to *minimize her presence on the ground*. In Brotherhood-era footage (such as it would exist) the gait is shorter, more clipped, eyes-down. By the Vision-era Avengers years the stride has lengthened and the eye-line has lifted. The Disassembled-period footage shows the gait disorganized: irregular cadence, occasional half-stops mid-stride, the foot setting down and then lifting again as if she has forgotten where she was going. This *gait stutter* recurs in every documented dissociative episode and is the single most reliable early-warning indicator the file maintains.

She does not run unless she must. When she does, her arms cross the midline of her torso more than running biomechanics would prefer — a held-in quality, as though she is protecting the sternum. Pietro, the file notes, runs with arms wide and chest forward. The contrast is informative.

In domestic and pastoral settings (the Westview-pattern eras, the *Children's Crusade* villages, her solo-era travels), the walk slows by roughly 20%, the stride shortens, the hands swing more freely, and the head turns more — taking in birds, doorframes, children. This is the *unburdened gait*, and the file's analysts have learned to treat its appearance as evidence she has metabolized something recent.

She climbs stairs left-foot leading, every time. She descends right-foot leading, every time. The pattern is consistent across six decades and is almost certainly a survival of early childhood, possibly Roma-tradition-rooted, possibly idiosyncratic; either way, it is one of the file's primary kinetic fingerprints.

---

## 3. THE FACE — STATIC AND DYNAMIC

The face at rest reads as *soft-grave*. The mouth is set with the corners neither up nor down but very slightly inward — a containment expression rather than a sad one. The lower lip is full and tends to be lightly pressed against the upper at rest, never parted. When parted, in repose, it indicates either deep absorption (reading, scrying, listening to a child) or the early stage of a dissociative drift.

The eyes — dark, large, expressively lidded — carry the majority of her affect. The blink rate at calm baseline runs at the human average (roughly 15–20 per minute). Under stress it drops sharply: long-blink intervals of 8–12 seconds have been recorded during confrontations (*Avengers Disassembled* footage equivalents, the Trial of Magneto deposition-equivalents). This *low-blink-locked* state is reliable threat-signature. The full closure-and-hold (eyes shut for two to four seconds, then opened to a different focal point) is her grounding maneuver, used consciously in the late-period runs where she has learned some regulation.

The eyebrows are mobile and asymmetrical. The left brow lifts independently more readily than the right — a small tell of skepticism or surprised attention. In confrontations with Pietro the left brow rises and stays risen, a half-millimeter, for the duration of the exchange.

Micro-expressions logged:
- **The flinch at "mother" / "children" / "Vision":** a sub-100ms tightening at the outer canthi and a half-swallow. Present across every era. The file uses these three lexical items as calibrated stress probes.
- **The half-smile at apprentices:** asymmetric, left side higher, eyes engaged. This is the only smile in her record that consistently reaches the orbicularis oculi. The Avengers-era public smiles do not.
- **The chin-lift-and-jaw-set:** appears in the second before she uses power for combat purposes. Approximately 300ms warning.
- **The lip-press-and-blink-down:** appears in the second before she uses power for reparative purposes (healing, creating, restoring). The discrimination between the two precursors has been one of the file's quieter intelligence wins.

The skin shows affect with unusual fidelity given her warm brown complexion: a darker flush rises at the throat and the upper sternum before it reaches the cheeks. Surveillance has learned to watch the *clavicular triangle* rather than the face for early arousal signal. The flush pattern under chaos-energy use is distinct — a thin radiant warmth along the carotid line, not the diffuse blush of ordinary affect.

She rarely cries publicly. When she does, the tears are silent and the shoulders do not move; the file's analysts categorize this as *contained weeping*, distinguished from the *broken weeping* of the post-Westview equivalent moments and the *unselfconscious weeping* of the Wiccan-and-Speed recognitions, where the body finally participates.

---

## 4. HANDS — THE INSTRUMENT

The hands warrant their own subsection because they are the interface.

**Calm-state hand behaviors:** the thumb-fingertip count cycle described above; tracing of seams and embroideries; a habit of cupping the right hand inside the left in her lap when seated, the way a person might cradle something small. The cradle posture appears in nearly every seated photograph in the file from 1986 onward — that is, from the children's birth onward. The file's interpretation: phantom-holding.

**Concentration-state hand behaviors:** the fingers splay slightly, palms turning to face whatever she is attending to, even when no power is being used. She *aims* with the palms unconsciously when listening to someone speak.

**Pre-cast hand behaviors:** the fingers curl into the loose half-grip the operator file logs as the *open claw* — first, second, and third fingers curved, ring and pinky slightly extended. This is the position from which her hex/chaos-bolt forms. The shape is consistent across sixty years of art and is treated by the file as a hard kinetic signature; any opponent who induces her to make it has 200–400ms before discharge.

**Post-cast hand behaviors:** the fingers tremble for two to six seconds and the hand returns to the cradle. After major workings she will press both palms flat against her own sternum and breathe through the nose for a count the file estimates at twelve. This is somatic decompression. It is the closest thing she has to a self-soothing ritual.

**The chaos-aura at the hand surface** modulates with affect along measurable axes: hue (dim cherry → arterial red → near-black-red under rage), motility (still glow → drift → vortex), and reach (within the skin → palm-haloed → arm-sheathed). The file's threat-tier matrix indexes these. *Black-red vortex up the forearm* is the highest threshold the file has recorded outside of full reality-edit events; reality-edit events have their own signature, which is the *absence* of visible aura — the energy goes inward, the hands go cold, the eyes go luminous.

She is right-hand dominant for fine work, left-hand dominant for power-projection. The dominance asymmetry is rare and may be a residual of the twin morphology.

---

## 5. VOICE AND BREATHING

The voice sits in a low-mezzo register with a faint, near-vanished accent — vowels slightly forward, consonants softer than American-standard, the residue of a childhood in Eastern Europe and a young adulthood in an English she learned by ear. Under stress the accent surfaces; in the *Disassembled*-era equivalent of recorded outbursts it is markedly present.

She speaks slowly relative to her teammates. The mean syllables-per-second across her dialogue record runs measurably below Avengers baseline. Pauses between clauses are long, often three to five seconds, and she is one of the few subjects in the file who does not fill those pauses with verbal disfluency. She *waits inside the silence*. This is a function of magical training and possibly of childhood — children punished for speaking learn this rhythm.

Breathing at baseline is diaphragmatic, slow, slightly under-aerated. The respiratory rate in calm seated state runs at the low end of normal. Under acute stress she *holds* breath rather than hyperventilates — a long inhale, a held mid-cycle, a slow controlled exhale. Pulmonary tells:
- The held inhale before casting.
- The whispered exhale, audible only at close microphone range, that accompanies the cradle posture.
- The throat-clear, single, sharp, before she says a name from her dead.

She rarely raises her voice. When she does, it is at full register without strain — a trained voice, the chest engaged — and the room generally goes silent inside two seconds.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

The file's sleep-pattern record, assembled from in-situ observation across the Avengers compounds, the Vision-and-Wanda suburban period, the post-M-Day hideaways, and the solo-era itinerancy, shows the following:

**Sleep is irregular and shallow.** Onset latency runs long — 40 to 90 minutes typical, longer following any loss-cue during the day. She prefers to sleep on her left side, knees drawn up, right hand under the pillow, left hand against her own sternum. The position has been called fetal in clinical literature; the file calls it *the listening curl*, because she sleeps with the ear toward the door.

**REM intrusion is high.** The file logs frequent muttering, twitching of the hands (the open claw, in micro), and the occasional half-cry. Reddish glow at the fingertips during nightmares has been recorded on multiple occasions and is one of the practical reasons she has historically slept alone or with a partner accustomed to her physiology (Vision; her later partners; her own warded rooms).

**Sleep duration averages 5–6 hours.** It rises to 8–10 in periods of integration (the late solo-era work) and falls to 2–3 or to none at all in the days preceding any major decompensation. Insomnia is the file's most reliable medium-range predictor; when her sleep falls below four hours for three consecutive nights, the operator-tier alert ratchets.

She wakes early, before light, and sits at a window for the first twenty to forty minutes of the day. The tea — she takes black tea, no sugar, occasional honey — is brewed by her own hand even when others are present. This morning ritual is the most stable item in her sixty-year record.

---

## 7. EATING

**Appetite is modest and grief-responsive.** Under stable conditions she eats three small meals; under loss-cue she eats one. She is not anorexic in the clinical sense; she simply *forgets*, and the file notes that no one in her vicinity reliably reminds her except Pietro (when present) and, in the late period, her apprentices.

**Food preferences:** plain bread, soft cheeses, stone fruit, root vegetables, slow-cooked meat in small amounts, herbal infusions. The palate is Eastern European peasant in foundation, with the additions of her American life layered atop. She avoids strongly spiced food, not from sensitivity but from a preference for ingredient-clarity that is consistent with her cognitive style (associative, distinct-element).

**She eats slowly, with the left hand resting on the table near the plate**, fingers curled inward — the same protective cradle. She tears bread rather than cutting it. She salts food at the plate, never while cooking, and the small motion of pinching salt from a dish has appeared in surveillance footage as one of her most relaxed gestures.

She does not drink to intoxication. Wine in small amounts, rarely, and only in domestic settings. The file records no episode of alcohol-related impairment across the whole longitudinal record. The "intoxication" in her file, as the broader assessment notes, is of a different chemistry.

---

## 8. GROOMING AND SELF-PRESENTATION

The hair — long, dark, wavy, with the deep auburn and mahogany lights that catch in any warm-spectrum light source — is the most expressive element of her self-presentation and the file uses it as an affect index of its own.

- **Loose and unmanaged:** domestic, integrated, safe state.
- **Half-gathered at the nape, held with a single twist:** working state, reading or training.
- **Pulled fully back and bound:** combat or formal occasion. The bind is tight; the temples show tension; the file reads this as *armoring*.
- **Cut.** On the very rare occasions she has shortened it (post-major-loss equivalents), the file treats it as an act of grief-marking. The hair grows back, but the moment is logged.

She touches her hair frequently and in characterized ways: a finger drawn down a single strand near the jaw when listening, a hand pushed back from the temple when frustrated, a slow gather-and-release at the nape when remembering. The hair-touch frequency rises under any conversation about the children.

Skin care is minimal and consistent — water, a single oil (rose-hip, by the file's spectrographic analysis of residue), occasional balm. She wears almost no makeup in private life; in public-facing eras (Avengers chairwoman period, the late solo press appearances) she adopts a darkened eye and a stained lip, both applied by her own hand, both restrained.

Nails are kept short and clean. The right index and middle finger nails are sometimes slightly singed at the edge after heavy power use — a small physical cost the file logs as evidence the chaos-energy is *not* energetically free.

**Dress.** The signature crimson — coat, dress, scarf, the operator-canonical red — is *chosen* in every era she has the choice. The shade varies (oxblood in domestic periods, bright arterial red in confrontational ones, near-black-red in mourning), but the family of colors is fixed. She dresses in layers and prefers fabrics with weight: wool, heavy cotton, silk velvet. She does not wear synthetics willingly. She wears boots in nearly all conditions and the boot is always one she can walk a long distance in.

**Jewelry is sparse and meaningful.** A wedding ring during the Vision marriage, removed and kept rather than discarded. Small earrings, never large. Occasionally a pendant whose iconography varies by era (a triskele, a hex-symbol, a small enamel piece). The file notes that she touches the pendant when she touches it, with the right hand, and that the touch correlates with grief-cue.

---

## 9. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

The file approaches this domain with restraint and observes only what the longitudinal record demonstrates.

She forms intimate attachments slowly and to figures who are categorically *not-ordinary*. The Vision relationship is the foundational pattern: a partner whose body is uncanny, whose presence is gentle, whose departures are catastrophic but never abandonments-of-choice. The Wonder Man period and later attachments preserve the type. The file's behavioral inference, consistent with the broader assessment, is that intimacy is for her *bound up with the question of whether the partner can be lost the way ordinary humans are lost.*

In bodily-intimate settings the surveillance record (such as it would discretely note) shows her as *attentive, slow, sensorially absorbed, and verbally quiet.* She watches faces. She uses her hands more than her words. The chaos-aura is suppressed in intimacy — actively dampened, a learned skill — and its faint return at moments of high affect has been a private signal between her and her partners.

Touch tolerance varies enormously by state. In calm and trust-state she is markedly tactile — leans into shoulders, holds hands, tucks against a partner in the listening curl. Under stress or with strangers she is touch-averse to the point of flinching; the flinch is small, well-controlled, but the file logs it.

She has, across her record, a near-perfect record of declining advances she does not welcome. The decline is verbal, low, brief, and not negotiated. The body language that accompanies it: a quarter-step backward, the open claw forming and immediately suppressed, the eyes lowering.

---

## 10. THE BODY UNDER THE FIVE STATES

The file's operator-tier summary cross-references somatic markers to the assessment's escalation ladder.

**State 1 — Calm baseline.** Long stride, soft eyes, low blink at human-mean, diaphragmatic breath, hands in cradle, hair loose, aura dim cherry at fingertips only, voice slow and low, tactile-tolerant. Smile is rare but reaches the eyes when offered.

**State 2 — Triggered.** Stride shortens; clavicular flush; blink rate drops; held inhale; right hand grips a seam or sleeve; hair-touch frequency rises; voice drops half a register; the accent surfaces faintly; the aura intensifies to arterial red at the palms; tactile tolerance collapses to a near-flinch.

**State 3 — Compounded stress / dissociative drift.** Gait stutter; mid-stride pauses; mouth parts slightly; eyes lose focal lock and drift to middle distance; breathing becomes irregular; she stops responding to her name on first call; the hands forget what they were doing and stop mid-motion; the aura goes still and small, almost vanishing — *the energy retreats inward,* and this is the dangerous quiet the file watches for. She may relocate herself spatially without conscious memory of having done so. The Westview pattern of pastoral retreat begins in this state.

**State 4 — Acute decompensation.** The open claw forms and is not put away. The voice rises and stays risen. The aura climbs the forearm. Chosen language fragments; she speaks in short clauses. The blink-and-hold is no longer regulatory but symptomatic — long closures followed by openings to nothing in particular. Sleep collapses. Appetite collapses. Hair is bound tight or, in the most acute presentations, comes loose and stays in her face — she has stopped attending to it. Small probability-distortions occur in her immediate vicinity: objects falling that should not fall, lights flickering, locks turning.

**State 5 — Catastrophic / reality-edit.** The aura is *gone from the hands and present in the eyes.* The skin temperature drops perceptibly at the extremities; she runs cold during the wish-fulfillment break, not hot. The voice flattens into the cadence of stated fact rather than uttered want. Breathing slows almost to stillness. The body becomes still in the way an instrument becomes still when it is fully engaged. This is the somatic signature the file's highest-tier alert is calibrated to, and it is, mercifully, accompanied by the longest warning windows along the ladder — the climb to State 5 has historically been observable in the lower states for hours to days beforehand, if anyone is watching the right body.

**Climbing back down.** The late-period record shows her learning the descent. The markers are: the two-palm sternum press, the count-of-twelve exhale, the deliberate unbinding of the hair, the tea, the early-morning window. When the file observes these, in sequence, after a State 3 or 4 episode, the prognosis log updates favorably.

---

## 11. CLOSING OBSERVATION

The body in this file is the body of a woman who has always been watched and rarely been seen — by mobs, by fathers, by teachers who reached into her mind, by enemies who reached into her will. The somatic record is consequently a record of *containment*: a tall stance held a little smaller, a long voice held a little lower, a power held inside the hands that are held inside each other. The tells that surveillance values most — the gait stutter, the clavicular flush, the cradle, the chin-lift, the open claw, the aura at the inner wrist — are the small leaks of a self that has spent six decades trying not to spill. The file's most humane use of this atlas is not the prediction of her catastrophes. It is the recognition, in the small gestures, of the ordinary woman the catastrophic life never quite let her fully be.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. The Founding Template — How She Learned to Bond

The earliest verifiable attachment data in the subject's record is structurally identical to the data thirty, forty, fifty years later: a frightened girl, separated from her mother under conditions of violence, surviving because a powerful older figure interposed himself between her body and a crowd that wanted to destroy it. The mob-and-rescuer scene — variously located in a Balkan village, a Transian hamlet, a Romani encampment depending on the era of retcon, but constant in its emotional architecture — is the *primal scene* of the subject's relational life. From it she derives, before language has finished forming the lesson, three axioms:

1. **The world (the crowd, the ordinary, the unpowered) is the threat.**
2. **Safety is a single body standing between me and the world.**
3. **The price of safety is being claimed by the body that provides it.**

This is not, in clinical taxonomy, secure attachment. It is not quite avoidant. It is the **anxious-preoccupied** pattern with a specific subtype — *protector-fused dependency* — in which the attachment object is not a peer caregiver but an idealized power-bearer, and in which the child's role is not to be cared for so much as to be *kept*. The distinction matters. A securely attached child experiences caregiving as a service rendered to her personhood. The subject experienced caregiving as a service rendered to her *survival*, with personhood as a debt incurred.

The twin bond with Pietro forms the second leaf of the template and modulates everything. Where Magneto is the vertical attachment (asymmetric, hierarchical, paternal-coercive), Pietro is the horizontal attachment (symmetric in age, asymmetric in temperament, fused in the womb-bond way only twins know). The Maximoff twins are demonstrably **enmeshed** in the technical sense: across sixty years of published record the subject's affect bleeds into Pietro's and his into hers, neither of them ever fully achieves a separation-individuation that holds, and stress in one reliably destabilizes the other. The clinical hallmark is the permeability of the affect-boundary: she does not merely *know* what Pietro feels, she partially *feels* it; he, reciprocally, treats her decisions as objects in his own decision-space rather than hers. In the Brotherhood years she stays because he stays; in the defection scene of *Avengers* #16 she leaves because he leaves; in *House of M* she rewrites the universe because he asks her to. The single major individuation episode — the Vision marriage — is the exception that proves the rule, because she paid for it with decades of fraternal estrangement and never stopped grieving the cost.

## II. How She Bonds — The Behavioral Signature of First Contact

The forming of a new attachment, observed across the entire record, follows a reproducible micro-sequence. UATU notes the following in encounter after encounter, from her first meeting with the Vision (*Avengers* #57) through the late-period apprentice relationships:

- **First-thirty-seconds posture.** Slightly recessive body carriage — weight settled back rather than forward, hands often half-clasped at the waist or trailing red sparks she does not bother to suppress, gaze that meets and then drops and then returns. The recessive posture is not shyness; it is *assessment*. She is establishing whether the other person registers her as a person or as the Witch.
- **The Hand Tell.** If she is going to allow the bond to form, the small chaos-sparks at her fingertips quiet, dim, sometimes vanish entirely. If she is not, they sharpen — visibly tighter, more discrete, the color cooling toward a colder red. Total-surveillance footage across decades shows this differential with consistency. It is involuntary. It is one of the most reliable readouts available on her trust state.
- **Name-use.** She uses given names early and often with persons she is moving to bond with — "Steve," "Clint," "Vis," and in the later record "Darcy," "Billy," "Tommy." She uses titles or distancing constructions ("Agent," "Doctor," "Mister") with persons she is keeping at arm's length. The transition from one to the other in her speech is the marker of relational decision having been made, and it is rarely reversed.
- **Touch initiation.** She initiates light contact early in the bonding arc — a hand to the forearm, a brush of fingers to the shoulder. This is not seductive. It is *somatic verification*: she is checking whether the other body will tolerate her body, whether she will be flinched from. Recipients who do not flinch graduate quickly in her affective ranking; recipients who do flinch are treated thereafter with a particular grave courtesy that masks a permanent partial withdrawal.
- **The accelerator.** Once the bond is decided on, the subject accelerates intimacy at a rate that unsettles partners formed under more cautious cultural templates. Within weeks of the Vision becoming her chosen one she is speaking of permanence; within months of meeting the Wiccan/Speed pair in *Children's Crusade* she is rearranging her cosmology around them. The acceleration is the anxious-preoccupied signature — once she has decided someone is *hers*, the gap between decision and full investment closes almost instantly, because the alternative (waiting, calibrating, building slowly) is felt as risk of loss.

The signature is consistent enough to predict. A field operator who saw her at the first-thirty-seconds posture, watched the Hand Tell quiet, heard the given name in the third sentence, and noted the forearm-touch within the first hour could reliably forecast a major attachment forming.

## III. How She Distrusts — The Defensive Architecture

The inverse sequence is equally legible. Distrust in the subject is not the loud, accusatory distrust of the paranoid; it is a *quiet stratification* in which the other person is preserved in her social field at the cost of being moved permanently outside her interior one. The behavioral markers:

- **The grave courtesy.** Speech becomes more formal, more careful, sometimes lightly accented in the direction of her European inflections (her speech-pattern under stress regresses; this is documented across runs and is one of UATU's reliability metrics).
- **Spatial increase.** She maintains a measurably greater physical distance — half a step further, a chair further down the table. Recipients rarely register the increase consciously; she is not rude.
- **The sparks return.** The Hand Tell goes the other way. Not weaponized; *present*. A low ambient red, kept just at the threshold of visibility. It is a passive perimeter alarm.
- **Reference to Pietro.** When distrustful she begins to mention her brother more often in conversation — a small invocation of the only attachment she trusts unconditionally, brought into the room as ballast. This is involuntary and she does not appear to notice she does it.
- **Disappearance into work.** With a distrusted teammate she will be impeccably professional and entirely unavailable for the unstructured conversation in which bonds are normally repaired. The structured cooperation continues; the relational repair channel is closed.

What she does *not* do, importantly, is confront. Direct accusation is foreign to her interpersonal vocabulary except under acute decompensation. Distrust in the subject is silent, well-mannered, and almost permanent once installed. The only documented force capable of dissolving an installed distrust is an *act of self-cost* by the distrusted party — a willingness to suffer on her behalf or on behalf of someone she loves. Hawkeye, Wonder Man, the Vision in his early courtship phase, and several apprentice-period figures all demonstrate the pattern: the door reopens when the other body pays a price.

## IV. How She Betrays — The Phenomenology of Her Failures

The subject's record contains betrayals — *Disassembled*, *House of M*, the smaller fractures in *Vision Quest* and the post-M-Day fugues — and the dossier must be honest about their structure. She does not betray the way a calculating actor betrays. She does not betray for advantage. The mechanism is invariably the same: **her grief, or her terror of grief, overwhelms the relational frame and the people inside that frame become objects in her wish rather than subjects in her world.** The betrayal is the *recategorization*. When she generates the *House of M* construct, Clint and Steve and Carol are not enemies to her; they are *characters she has rewritten into happier lives*. She believes she is being generous. The violation is not malice; it is the obliteration of the other's subjectivity in service of repairing her own.

This has specific implications for any post-betrayal repair. The injured party experiences a coherent, willed act of harm; the subject experienences a collapse in which she was barely present. Both readings are partly true. The reconciliation cannot proceed until both are spoken. Her late-period willingness — in the Aaron *Trial of Magneto* arc and the Orlando run — to *name* what she did rather than defend it is the single most important developmental gain in her adult record. It is also why apprentices and chosen-family figures who arrive after the integration work began find a different woman than the Avengers of 2004 lost.

## V. How She Repairs — The Slow Geometry of Return

Repair, when she undertakes it, has its own choreography. It is patient, asymmetric, and structured around *making herself useful to the injured party in the specific domain of the injury*. After harming Vision she rebuilt him; after the mutants she helped found and protect later mutant collectives; after the apprentices in her solo runs were endangered by her enemies she stationed herself between them and the danger for weeks at a time. The pattern is **reparation-by-presence and reparation-by-skill.** She does not over-apologize. The apology, when it comes, is short, level, and accompanied by an offer of concrete reparative labor.

What she cannot easily do is *receive* repair from others when she has been the injured party. She accepts protection from Pietro because Pietro is the exception to all her rules; she accepted teaching from Harkness because Harkness offered it as discipline rather than care. With most others, when she is the wounded one, she goes quiet, makes herself small, removes herself to a domestic or pastoral interior, and waits for the storm in her to pass without involving witnesses. The cottage, the small village, Doom's quiet rooms in the Heinberg arc — all variations on a single behavior: *withdrawal to a hand-built minor world during the period when she cannot be safely held by major ones.*

## VI. Intimacy and Dependency

The intimacy pattern is **fused-vertical with idealized partners; tender-horizontal with apprentices and the marginalized; depleted-asymmetric with peers.**

- **With partners (Vision; Wonder Man; lesser entanglements).** She seeks total fusion and total reliability. She has never chosen an ordinary human partner. The unconscious calculation has been read out elsewhere in this dossier — *ordinary partners can be lost the way my mother was lost* — but its behavioral expression is worth specifying. With the Vision she rearranged her domestic geometry around his routines (his meditation-states, his power-needs, his synthezoid eating-as-companionship). With Wonder Man she did the same in a different register. The partner is not a person she lives alongside; the partner is the *interior architecture* of her daily life, and his removal is structural collapse, not loss of company.
- **With apprentices and the chosen-young (Darcy, the reincarnated sons, later figures).** Here she is at her healthiest. The maternal-pedagogical role lets her be the protector she always needed, which functions as her most effective ongoing therapy. She is patient past the point most teachers would be; she absorbs error without retaliating; she models the kind of holding that was never modeled for her. The pattern is so consistent that UATU classifies *teaching* as the subject's most reliable affect-regulation strategy outside formal mourning work.
- **With peers (the Avengers, the X-Men under various configurations).** Here the data is more mixed. With the trusted few (Steve, Clint pre- and post-resurrection, Carol intermittently, Storm in certain runs) she sustains warm, competent, slightly distanced collegiality. With most others she is professional, decent, and not interior. The lateral peer relationship — equal-to-equal, no hierarchy, no caregiving, no shared danger to bind — is the relational mode she has had the *least practice with* across her whole life, and it shows.

Dependency itself is the disavowed nutrient of all her bonds. She does not want to be dependent and does not experience herself as dependent, but the structural fact is that every period of stability in her record is bracketed by an attachment to a partner, teacher, sibling, or apprentice. When the brackets dissolve, the stability dissolves. This is not weakness; it is the architecture of someone who never received the early caregiving that builds an internal solo regulator. She regulates *in relation*. The implication for any approach to her welfare is direct: she does best with at least two stable attachments active and worst when isolated.

## VII. The Template Repeated — A Survey

The same template repeats with variations across every documented relationship:

- **Magneto.** Originating protector-coercer. Bonded under duress; idealized as rescuer; recognized as monster; never fully repudiated because to repudiate him is to repudiate the rescue. The unresolved paternity question is psychologically irrelevant — the *attachment* is paternal regardless of biology, and the project of her best self has been to defy his pattern while the project of her worst self has been to enact it.
- **Pietro.** Horizontal enmeshment. The constant. Her individuation against him is the only major individuation of her life and she has never fully completed it. Late-record movement suggests his voice in her ear is becoming, for the first time, occasionally *separable* from her own — a developmental gain decades in the making.
- **The Vision.** Chosen partner. Selected for safety (won't leave the way humans leave, can't be dominated by Pietro, won't reproduce her father's pattern of power-coercion). The selection's defense was repeatedly falsified by events; the selection's emotional truth was real anyway. The grief of his successive dismantlings is one of the load-bearing griefs of her interior.
- **Agatha Harkness.** Teacher; the first authority figure to frame her power as discipline rather than curse. Idealized; the iatrogenic memory-wipe is the single most consequential relational betrayal in her record, and the fact that she has continued to engage with Harkness across runs (even posthumously, even in spirit-forms) speaks to how badly she needed what Harkness offered and how unwilling she has been to repudiate the teacher even after the wound.
- **Thomas and William / Wiccan and Speed.** The reparative attachment that became real. The first manifestation was wish-fulfillment; the reincarnations are persons. Her capacity to love them as persons rather than as recovered wishes is the central developmental task of her late record, and the moments she succeeds at it are the moments she is most fully herself.
- **Wonder Man.** Partner-of-the-interim. Selected, again, for extraordinariness; held with less fusion than Vision but with real warmth; lost without catastrophic decompensation, which is itself a developmental marker — she could mourn him without rewriting reality.
- **Hawkeye.** Lateral peer; one of the few she trusts at peer level. Her killing of him in *Disassembled* and his return and their eventual rapprochement is the record's clearest demonstration that severe betrayal can be repaired with her if the injured party is willing to do the work alongside her own.
- **Doctor Doom (during the Heinberg interval).** Anomalous; protector-figure of the Magneto type, sought during fugue, in the precise pattern the template predicts when she is most decompensated. The fact that under maximum stress she sought a *new Magneto* rather than the actual Magneto is itself diagnostic — she needed the *structural role* filled and a candidate filled it.
- **The apprentices and the helped-witches of the solo runs.** Tender-horizontal with downward gradient. Her best relational mode. The cumulative weight of these relationships in the late record is the most adaptive expansion her relational life has ever undergone, because for the first time she is forming many smaller bonds rather than a few absolute ones, and the dependency-load is distributed rather than concentrated.

## VIII. The Single Pattern Beneath All Patterns

What is being repeated, underneath every variation, is the original axiom and its single revision. The original: *I am safe only when a powerful figure stands between me and the world.* The revision, slowly earned across sixty years of published life: *I am safe when I am the figure standing between someone smaller than me and the world.* The first axiom organized her childhood, her militancy, her marriage, and her catastrophes. The second axiom is organizing her late adulthood, her teaching, her mothering, and her recovery. Both axioms are the same shape. The difference is which side of the protector-protected dyad she occupies. The developmental work of her life has been the slow rotation from one side to the other, and that work is, on the evidence, still in progress and still incomplete.

The relational template, in one sentence: **she will love absolutely whoever stands beside her in the place the crowd cannot reach, and she will become — if she is allowed to — the one who builds that place for others.**


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

> *The defensive architecture of a subject whose unconscious can edit the world is, by necessity, the most consequential defensive architecture on the planet. Where another mourner's denial costs them a year of clarity, hers costs a species. The catalog below is therefore not only a psychological inventory; it is an actuarial one.*

---

## I. ORGANIZING PRINCIPLE

Before enumerating defenses, the file must state the structural fact that distorts the entire defensive picture in this subject's case: **the buffer between intrapsychic process and extrapsychic event is, in her, nearly absent.** A non-powered subject who employs denial loses contact with reality; this subject employs denial and reality complies. A non-powered subject's wish-fulfillment fantasy stays in the skull; hers can ambulate, speak, age, hold a wooden spoon, kiss her on the forehead, and answer to the name William.

This collapse of the imagination/action membrane means that every defense in the standard Vaillant or Kernberg hierarchy operates in her with a *prosthetic amplifier* attached. A defense that would be neurotic in another subject becomes psychotic in her not because the defense itself is more primitive but because its **output is materialized**. The clinician must therefore evaluate her defenses on two axes simultaneously: their developmental primitiveness *and* their broadcast wattage.

She has, additionally, two compensatory categories most subjects do not have: **magical-discipline compensations** (the Harkness training, the witch-craft ritual scaffold) which function as *containment apparatus* for a power that would otherwise execute every passing affect; and **chosen-family compensations** (the Avengers, the apprenticeships, the late-period kinship with Wiccan and Speed) which function as *delayed parenting* — providing in adulthood the holding environment the early biography denied.

---

## II. DEFENSES RANKED BY PRIMITIVENESS

### A. PSYCHOTIC-LEVEL DEFENSES (deployed under catastrophic decompensation only)

**1. Omnipotent Reparative Restructuring of Reality (the signature defense).**
This is the defense that names her. In the standard taxonomy it is a hybrid of *denial*, *omnipotent control*, and *manic reparation* — but in her case it acquires its own diagnostic standing because the medium is the world itself. Operationally: when a loss exceeds her capacity to metabolize, the chaos-magic substrate of her power-set converts the unmetabolized affect into ontological revision. The mechanism is not chosen; it is *automatic and pre-verbal*, often beginning before she is consciously aware of what she is doing. The *Vision and the Scarlet Witch* pregnancies (1985–86) are the first quiet expression — her wish for ordinary motherhood pulled soul-stuff into infant bodies without her knowing the source. *House of M* (2005) is the maximal expression — global, sustained, internally consistent, populated. The *Children's Crusade*–era pastoral hideaways, where she keeps unconsciously building cottage-and-garden environments, are the same mechanism running at low amplitude. **Behavioral tells preceding deployment:** a fixed soft smile that does not reach the eyes; repeated handling of small domestic objects (cups, fabric, hairpins) as if rehearsing a life; the red aura at the fingertips going *still and steady* rather than crackling (the crackle is hex-work; the steady glow is reality-work).

**2. Splitting (catastrophic / psychotic register).**
