Under acute decompensation she splits the world into *the deserving safe* (those she loves, who must be protected at any ontological cost) and *the category that hurt them* (mutants in *House of M*'s coda, the Avengers in *Disassembled*, the human crowd in childhood memory). When splitting reaches this register, members of the "deserving safe" group can be killed and conscripted into the construct as ideal versions of themselves without contradiction — Vision is dead and Vision is her husband in the rewrite; both at once. Note: between catastrophes she does not split this way. The split is a *decompensation product*, not a baseline character feature, which is precisely why she is not BPD.

**3. Delusional Projection (rare, episodic).**
Under Immortus's manipulation (*Avengers West Coast* #51–52) and during the worst of *Disassembled*, she briefly attributes her own intentions to external entities — *they made me do this*, *it wasn't me* — in a way that is not simple disavowal but a structured perceptual reorganization. The clinical complication is that *in her case the attribution is often partially true*: Immortus did manipulate her; Mephisto's soul-fragments did inhabit her children; her power-set is genuinely susceptible to external chaos-currents. This makes the defense almost impossible to challenge head-on — to call it a delusion is to ignore the partial reality, but to credit it fully is to collude with the disavowal.

---

### B. IMMATURE / BORDERLINE-LEVEL DEFENSES (recurrent across decades)

**4. Dissociation (fugue, depersonalization, amnesia).**
The post–*House of M* and *Children's Crusade*-era amnesias are the most legible expression: she lives months or years in a small village, in Doom's castle, in pastoral nowhere, without access to her name or history. Sub-clinical versions appear throughout the record: the glassy-eyed panels in the Byrne *Vision Quest* arc; the moments in *Disassembled* when she narrates her own destruction as if observing it; the late-Robinson-era passages where she catches her reflection and momentarily does not recognize the face. **Behavioral tells of incipient dissociation:** a delay of one to three beats in answering when spoken to; rubbing the pad of the thumb against the inside of the opposite wrist (a self-orientation gesture, possibly originating in childhood); the eyes tracking past the speaker's face rather than to it; speech volume dropping a register.

**5. Regression to Domestic / Pastoral Frame.**
When stress accumulates short of full decompensation, she retreats — sometimes consciously, more often not — into the trappings of an ordinary domestic life: cooking, gardening, mending fabric, tending small animals. The Robinson solo run uses this beautifully: she travels to small towns, rents rooms, makes tea for the witches she helps. This is regression in the technical sense (return to an earlier developmental wish — *the ordinary girlhood I never had*) but it is also one of her most adaptive defenses; it slows the escalation ladder and gives her body somewhere to put the energy that would otherwise route to power.

**6. Identification with the Aggressor.**
The most dangerous of her recurrent defenses because its template is *Magneto*. Under sustained threat to her children or her chosen family she has, repeatedly, become a version of him: sovereign, certain, willing to remake the species-level order to secure a familial-level safety. *House of M* is Magneto's politics executed by Wanda's instrument. The defense is so embedded that she may not detect its operation in herself — when she speaks in this register, her cadence slows, the sentences shorten, the vowels lengthen, and observers who knew Magneto find the resemblance unbearable. The late record shows her developing a *counter-tell*: when she catches herself in this register, she physically steps back, exhales audibly, and lowers her hands.

**7. Displacement (categorical).**
"No more mutants" is the textbook instance: rage at specific wounding figures (her father, the Avengers who came to judge her, the children's reabsorption) is displaced onto the *category* (mutants) those figures share. The displacement is *upward in abstraction*, which is rare; most displacement runs sideways (kicking the dog instead of the boss). Hers runs to the species level because her instrument operates at the species level. Smaller daily versions: irritation at one Avenger expressed as withdrawal from the team; a single bad memory of Westview expressed as avoidance of all American small towns for years.

**8. Somatization (mild, intermittent).**
Headaches before reality-pressure events; a tightness behind the sternum she touches without comment; insomnia in the week before anniversaries (the children's "birthday"; the date of the Westview-equivalent event in her timeline; the wedding date). She does not name these as somatic expressions of grief; the file documents them as such.

---

### C. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (baseline functioning)

**9. Reaction Formation.**
The tenderness she shows to the marginalized is genuine, but its *intensity* exceeds the situation, and the excess is reaction-formation against the destroyer-identity. She is gentler than the moment requires with witches, mutants, frightened children, the uncanny — gentler because some part of her is always answering the internal accusation *you are the one who hurts these people.* The defense is adaptive (the kindness is real and useful) but its driving energy is shame.

**10. Intellectualization (via the magical lexicon).**
When grief threatens to surface in conversation, she will pivot into the vocabulary of craft — talking about *thresholds*, *sigils*, *the witches' road*, *chaos as a probability-fold* — not because the topic is irrelevant but because the technical frame holds her at one remove from the feeling. Apprentices and partners learn to recognize the pivot: the moment the diction becomes ceremonial, the affect underneath is acute.

**11. Sublimation (primary mature defense).**
The late-period solo work — helping witches, mentoring, traveling to repair small-scale magical injuries — is sublimation of the omnipotent-reparative drive into proportionate reparative action. The same wish that built House of M is, here, building one safe room for one frightened practitioner at a time. This is the defense whose strengthening is the single most prognostically important variable in her file.

**12. Anticipation.**
A late acquisition. She has begun, in the Orlando-era record, to *anticipate* the triggers — to mark anniversaries in advance, to arrange to be with Wiccan and Speed on the days she knows will be hard, to ask for company rather than wait for collapse. This is mature defense work and would have been unimaginable in the pre-*Disassembled* record.

**13. Altruism.**
Distinct from reaction-formation in that the giving does not require a shame-engine to drive it. With apprentices specifically she gives from surplus, not deficit — the patience, the slow teaching, the willingness to let them fail and try again. This is one of the few domains in her life where she is *not* defending; she is simply being.

**14. Humor (dry, self-deprecating, late-emerging).**
Almost absent in the early record (the 1960s–1980s Wanda is grave, even when happy). Emerges intermittently in the Robinson and Orlando runs: a wry remark about her own catastrophes, a self-aware aside about being "the witch who ended the world that one time." Humor in her is a *late and fragile* defense and its presence is a prognostic positive — it indicates she can hold the worst of herself in view without flinching away.

---

## III. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE

**The Harkness Scaffold.** The training under Agatha — even given the catastrophic later betrayal of the memory-wipe — installed a *ritual containment apparatus* for her power that she retains for life. Hand positions, breath patterns, the sequence of sigils traced before a working — these are not merely magical technique; they are *somatic regulation*. When she runs through the opening forms of a working, her heart rate slows, her breath deepens, her power-signature stabilizes. The craft is, functionally, her DBT.

**The Chosen-Family Holding Environment.** The Avengers, at their best, functioned as the corrective family the biography denied — a horizontal kinship of equals rather than a vertical hierarchy under a charismatic-cruel father. Captain America in particular operated as a *non-coercive* authority figure, the inverse of Magneto, and his steady presence in her early Avengers years is one of the most stabilizing variables in the file.

**Apprenticeship as Reverse-Parenting.** Teaching Darcy and her later apprentices lets her give what she did not receive: patient instruction, non-punitive correction, the message that the power is *a discipline, not a curse*. The repetition of these phrases to her students is partly for them and partly a form of self-administered reparenting.

**The Reincarnated Sons.** Wiccan and Speed are simultaneously the deepest wound (they are *and are not* the children she lost) and the most powerful integrative compensation. Their presence forces her to hold the paradox of *gone-and-returned* without rewriting it away — which is, precisely, the developmental task she has failed at every other juncture.

**Late-Period Spiritual Practice.** Travel, pilgrimage, the witch-road work — these provide *ritual time* in which grief has a sanctioned container. She mourns in the language of craft and is held by the form.

---

## IV. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE

**Reality-Editing as Conflict Avoidance.** The low-amplitude version of the signature defense: small probabilistic shifts to make a difficult conversation not happen, to make a triggering object be elsewhere, to make a person she does not want to see take a different street. She may not be aware these are happening. The cumulative effect over decades is a life partially insulated from the friction that would otherwise have forced earlier integration.

**Flight Into the Extraordinary Partner.** The unconscious calculation — *ordinary partners can be lost the way my mother was lost; extraordinary partners cannot* — has been *falsified* by every relationship in her record (Vision dismantled, Wonder Man repeatedly killed, etc.) and the defense persists anyway. The cost is that she has never tested the hypothesis she most needs to test: that ordinary love is survivable.

**Capitulation to Pietro Under Stress.** Enmeshment is a defense against the terror of being the only one inside her own skull. When her judgment and his diverge under low-stress conditions she can hold her own ground; under high stress, his voice overrides hers. *House of M* is the historical apex of this cost.

**Pastoral Regression as Avoidance.** The same retreat that operates adaptively as decompression can operate maladaptively as flight from cosmic responsibility — *I will not be the witch the world needs, because being her is what broke me.* The Robinson and Orlando runs show her negotiating this; the negotiation is not finished.

**Power-Intoxication.** Not chemical but behaviorally identical: tolerance escalation (she has needed bigger and bigger workings to feel the same relief), withdrawal collapse (the post-*M-Day* depowering left her, for a time, hollow), and the characteristic loss of perspective during the high. This is a defense against affective emptiness — when she cannot feel her own life, she can always feel the working.

**Premature Forgiveness of Authority Figures Who Wounded Her.** She has forgiven Magneto, repeatedly. She has, in some readings, partly forgiven Harkness. The forgiveness is not always integrative; sometimes it is a defense against the rage that would, if felt, be unbearable in its scale. (The displaced rage finds other targets — see Displacement, above.)

---

## V. THE DEFENSIVE ESCALATION SEQUENCE — OBSERVABLE FORM

The file's surveillance value is highest here: the sequence by which her defenses fail in order, top-down, under accumulating stress, with the *observable behavioral markers* at each rung. An operator monitoring the subject can read the rung from the body.

**Rung 0 — Baseline.** Sublimation, altruism, anticipation, humor operative. Body relaxed, hands often occupied (cup, fabric, the spine of a book). Speech mid-register, melodic, lightly accented. Eye contact warm and held.

**Rung 1 — Triggered.** Intellectualization and reaction-formation activate. Diction becomes ceremonial; tenderness becomes slightly excessive; the thumb-to-opposite-wrist gesture appears; the hands begin to seek each other in her lap.

**Rung 2 — Compounded.** Somatization and mild dissociation. Headache; the tightness behind the sternum; the one-to-three-beat answering delay; eyes tracking past the speaker. Power-signature: faint red at the fingertips even at rest.

**Rung 3 — Acute.** Regression to pastoral frame; displacement; mild splitting. She seeks small enclosed domestic spaces; she speaks of categories rather than individuals; she begins to handle small objects as if rehearsing.

**Rung 4 — Decompensating.** Identification with the aggressor; the cadence slows, vowels lengthen; the red aura goes *steady* rather than crackling. This is the last rung at which intervention is reliably possible.

**Rung 5 — Catastrophic.** Omnipotent reparative restructuring engages. The world begins to soften at the edges around her. By the time observers notice the world has changed, the defense has succeeded and they are inside it.

---

## VI. PROGNOSTIC NOTE ON THE DEFENSIVE ARCHITECTURE

The single most important fact about this subject's defenses is that *the mature ones are real and they are growing.* Anticipation, sublimation, altruism, humor — these were absent or vestigial in the first thirty years of the published record and are now load-bearing. The catastrophic defenses have not been *removed* (they cannot be; the instrument that executes them is her body), but they are being *outcompeted* by mature alternatives that route the same drives into proportionate channels. The witch she helps in a small town is, structurally, the world she would once have rewritten. The named acknowledgment of the children is, structurally, the wish-construct that would once have built them anew.

The file's recommendation is that any intervention regime treat the mature defenses as the strategic asset and the catastrophic defenses as the contingency to be *prevented from being needed*, not extirpated. The aim is not to disarm her. The aim is to ensure that her grief, henceforth, always has somewhere smaller to go.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# Longitudinal Psychological Profile — Wanda Maximoff

*A decade-by-decade clinical reconstruction of affect regulation, cognitive organization, and self-concept, derived from the published behavioral record and read against the grief-and-trauma literature cited in the clinical provenance (Bryant et al. 2024; Pop-Jordanova 2021).*

---

## I. Pre-Record Substrate (Childhood, reconstructed)

Before *X-Men* #4 (1964) the subject has no published behavioral record in real time, only retrospective reconstruction across decades of retcon. What is invariant across every reconstruction is the *structure*: an early maternal loss (or maternal absence — the identity of the birth mother fluctuates in canon, but her *absence* does not); a peripatetic, threatened girlhood in eastern-European or Roma-adjacent settings; a peasant-mob event in which she was nearly killed for what she was; and a rescue by an older, powerful male figure who became her first attachment of consequence.

From that substrate, three pre-record psychological facts can be inferred with high confidence and are confirmed by the entirety of the subsequent sixty-year record:

1. **The world is a mob.** Her implicit social schema codes crowds as lethal and individuals — especially powerful individuals — as the only available shelter. This will determine every attachment choice she ever makes.
2. **Safety is borrowed, never owned.** She has no internal experience of safety that does not require a body standing between her and the threat. This is the seed of the lifelong *dependency-on-idealized-protector* pattern.
3. **Her brother is half of her.** Twin-fusion under shared persecution is the default object relation. The boundary between her affect and Pietro's was never properly drawn because the conditions for drawing it (a stable third, a holding environment, an unhurried childhood) never obtained.

These three facts are the developmental floor. Everything that follows is built on them.

---

## II. The 1960s — Coerced Agency, Foreclosed Identity (ages roughly late teens to early twenties in subjective canon time)

**Affect regulation.** Fear-dominated, externally regulated. In her earliest published appearances she is visibly *flinching* — startled by raised voices, recoiling from Magneto's anger, freezing under combat stress. Her hexes in this period are tentative and apologetic; she warns opponents before she fires; she stops mid-fight to check whether Pietro is intact. Her capacity to regulate her own affect is essentially nil; she borrows regulation from Pietro (proximity) or from authority (compliance).

**Cognitive style.** Compliant-magical. She does not yet understand her power as belonging to a knowledge tradition; she experiences it as a *curse that occasionally cooperates.* Cognitively she is intuitive, present-focused, and superstitious about her own gift — the "hex" framing she uses for herself in this era is telling. She thinks of her power the way a frightened person thinks of weather. There is no analytic relationship to her own instrument.

**Self-concept.** Embedded, undifferentiated. She is "Pietro's sister," "Magneto's recruit," "a mutant" — the self is described entirely in relational and categorical terms. There is no first-person identity claim in this period that does not reference another. The defection to the Avengers (*Avengers* #16, 1965) is the first observable proto-self-assertion, and even it is structured as *following Pietro into a different shelter.*

**Evolutionary marker.** The defection installs a new template: *self-assertion is possible, but only when a new attachment is available to receive the asserted self.* This template will govern the next two decades.

---

## III. The Late 1960s through Mid-1970s — Transferred Attachment, First Individuation

**Affect regulation.** Beginning to stabilize through *borrowed structure*. The Avengers function as her first holding environment. Captain America is a benign authority who does not demand fusion; Hawkeye is a peer who teases without endangering; the team's rituals (meetings, training, missions with debrief) provide the predictable scaffolding her childhood denied her. Her affect during this period is observably broader — she laughs in panel for the first time, she expresses anger without dissociating from it, she cries without collapsing.

**Cognitive style.** Still intuitive and associative, but with an emerging capacity for *deliberation*. The Vision courtship is the data: she does not fall into the relationship; she *considers* it, against social and familial headwind, over a sustained period. This is the first observable instance of her holding a desire long enough to examine it.

**Self-concept.** The first individuation. The Vision marriage (*Giant-Size Avengers* #4, 1975) is the most psychologically significant act of her early adulthood not because of who she marries but because of *whom she defies in marrying him.* She asserts herself against Pietro — the figure with whom she has been fused since infancy — and survives the assertion. The self-concept that emerges is fragile but real: *I am a woman who chooses; I am not only my brother's sister.*

**Pathology already visible to the trained eye.** The choice itself encodes the wound. She chooses Vision because he is *categorically unable to abandon her in the human ways humans abandon.* He cannot die of illness, cannot leave her for another woman in the conventional sense, cannot fade. The defense underneath the love is *I will not survive another ordinary loss, so I will not have an ordinary partner.* The defense is plausible. It is also doomed: extraordinary partners can be lost in extraordinary ways, and they will be.

---

## IV. The Mid-1970s through Mid-1980s — Apprenticeship, High-Functioning Stability

**Affect regulation.** Highest observed competence in her entire record. Under Agatha Harkness's tutelage (*Avengers* #128 forward), she develops — for the only sustained period in her published life — a *disciplinary* relationship with her own affect. Magic, taught properly, is affect regulation made operational: name what you feel, name what you intend, separate the two, choose. Harkness gives her the only formal training she will ever receive in distinguishing *feeling* from *acting on the world.* The hex-bolts in this era are clean, controlled, and purposeful. She fires less and accomplishes more.

**Cognitive style.** Integrative. She begins to think of her power as belonging to a tradition (witchcraft) with a history, a lineage, and a literature — not a curse, not a mutation accident, but a *practice.* This reframe is enormous. It moves her from *patient* to *practitioner.* She begins, in this period, to read, to study, to inquire. Her cognitive functioning becomes more symbolic in the *productive* sense: she can use metaphor and ritual to *contain* what she could previously only discharge.

**Self-concept.** Coherent for the first time. She is *Wanda*: wife, witch, Avenger, woman. The brief Avengers chairship (*Avengers* #279) is the apex — she leads, others follow, no protector frames her, no brother flanks her. The internal self-statements in this period (insofar as we can reconstruct them from action and dialogue) are first-person and possessive: *my magic, my home, my team, my husband.*

**The hidden vulnerability.** Beneath the competence, the foundational schemas remain untouched. The *world-is-mob, safety-is-borrowed, brother-is-half-of-me* substrate has been *built over*, not *worked through.* This will matter when the structure is loaded past its design limit.

---

## V. The Mid-to-Late 1980s — The Manifestation and Its Theft

**Affect regulation.** Initially excellent — *the children's arrival is the period of her greatest sustained joy in the entire record.* The pregnancies (*Vision and the Scarlet Witch* #12, 1986), the births, the early motherhood: she is *regulated by purpose.* Her power output during this period is observably lower-amplitude and higher-precision — the magic is no longer an outlet for unprocessed affect because the affect is being absorbed by the daily work of mothering.

**Cognitive style.** Domestic-symbolic. She thinks in the rhythms of a household. Her magical practice contracts to small, household-scale work. This is not regression; this is *appropriate scaling* of an instrument that had previously had no banks.

**The unseen mechanism.** What she does not know — what *no one* knows in real-narrative time — is that the children are *manifestations of her power against the substrate of reality itself*. The Mephisto-soul-fragment mechanism, revealed later, is the cosmological surface. The psychological mechanism beneath it is the one that matters for this profile: **her instrument can convert sufficiently structured longing into ontological fact.** She does not yet know that she has this capacity. The children are the first proof, and the proof is hidden inside the experience of ordinary maternal joy. When the proof is later revealed by being undone, the revelation will be catastrophic.

**Self-concept at peak.** *Mother, wife, witch, Avenger.* The most integrated four-noun self she will ever achieve.

**The collapse.** Vision is dismantled by the government taskforce and rebuilt as the emotionless white synthezoid (*Vision Quest*, 1989). The children are revealed to be soul-fragments and reabsorbed. Agatha Harkness — *the teacher, the trusted authority, the only sustained holding figure of her adult life* — performs the memory-wipe of the children (*Avengers West Coast* #52). 

Read this triad clinically. She loses, in close succession: (a) her partner (twice — once to dismantling, once to emotional erasure on reconstruction); (b) two children (perinatal-equivalent loss compounded by being told the loss was *not real in the way she experienced it* — what the trauma literature recognizes as *epistemic injury* layered on grief); (c) her teacher, in the role of perpetrator of the mnestic violation rather than holder of the grief.

The Pop-Jordanova grief literature is exactly on point here: shock, disbelief, denial, intense anxiety and anger — the normal acute-grief response — were *not permitted to occur*, because the memory of what was lost was excised. Grief that cannot be felt cannot be metabolized. The Bryant 2024 CBT-vs-Mindfulness PGD literature presupposes a patient who can *access* the loss in order to work on it. Wanda was surgically prevented from accessing hers. The *Vision Quest / Darker Than Scarlet* dissociation — glassy one panel, lucid the next — is the predictable presentation of *grief that the mind has been forbidden to perform.*

---

## VI. The 1990s — Performed Functioning Over a Hollow

**Affect regulation.** Brittle. She functions. She fights. She dates Wonder Man. She holds positions on Avengers rosters. The hexes work. To a casual observer she is *fine*. To the longitudinal observer, she is performing affect rather than experiencing it. The bandwidth of expressed emotion narrows; the variability of facial expression flattens (insofar as comic art can record this, the Pérez-era and post-Pérez renderings show it). She is in what the trauma literature calls *constricted affect* — a chronically low-amplitude emotional life maintained as a defense against the threat of any emotion at all reactivating the buried catastrophe.

**Cognitive style.** Reverted toward intuitive and away from the symbolic-integrative competence of the Harkness years. Without the teacher and without the practice, the discipline atrophies. She thinks tactically in combat, sentimentally in relationships, and *not at all* about her own interior. The Wonder Man relationship is instructive: another extraordinary partner (ionic energy, functionally immortal), chosen by the same defense — *ordinary partners can be lost; I will not have an ordinary partner.* That she chooses him without examining the choice is the cognitive datum.

**Self-concept.** *Avenger.* The four-noun self of the mid-1980s has collapsed to one. She is no longer wife (Vision is white and emotionless), no longer mother (the children are not), no longer witch in any practiced sense (Harkness is gone, the lineage has fallen out of daily use). What remains is the role. She *does* the role competently. The role is not a self.

**The hollow.** The clinical picture is *Persistent Complex Bereavement* (the DSM-5 antecedent of ICD-11 Prolonged Grief Disorder) — chronic yearning, role-restriction, identity disruption, difficulty engaging with new pursuits — running silently under apparent functioning. The Bryant-and-Pop-Jordanova clinical literature would, on this presentation alone, predict eventual decompensation.

---

## VII. The Early-to-Mid 2000s — The Return of the Repressed

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic failure. *Avengers Disassembled* (Bendis, 2004) is the textbook return of unmetabolized grief at full pressure. The recovered memory of the children — surfaced by whatever trigger the text supplies — does not arrive as feeling. It arrives as *action*, because *she has never developed the capacity to hold the feeling.* This is the central clinical point: grief, when arrested by mnestic violation, returns not as grief but as *the thing the grief would have done if grief had had hands.* Her grief had hands. She killed her teammates with them.

The structure of *Disassembled* is grief-rage with no available regulation. She does not weep. She does not collapse. She does not seek help. She *generates events.* Each act — the killing of one Avenger, the engineering of another's death, the reshaping of the Mansion — is, behaviorally, *the discharge of an affect that has no other discharge route.* The instrument converted the unprocessed grief directly into world-event because that is what the instrument does.

*House of M* (2005) is the same affect at the next scale up. Confronted by friends preparing to decide her fate, she does what she has done since the children: *she rewrites.* The rewritten world is diagnostically pure. It contains: (a) the children alive and well; (b) Magneto restored to sovereignty; (c) Pietro at her side; (d) herself as princess (i.e., still *daughter and sister*, never sovereign in her own right); (e) mutantkind ascendant. Every element is a reparative wish. None is a power-grab. This is not ideology, not megalomania, not Bond-villainy. It is a child building the diorama of the world the universe failed to give her.

The terminal utterance — *"No more mutants"* — is the rage-displacement. Not at Magneto (whom she cannot bear to harm), not at Pietro (whom she cannot bear to harm), not at Vision (already broken), not at the Avengers (already attacked) — but at the *category* that produced all of her wounds. It is the act of a person who has run out of small things to break.

**Cognitive style during the break.** Delusionally restructured. She is not lying about the rewritten world; she *experiences it as real and right.* This meets criteria for a psychotic episode in any conventional framing; the only unusual feature is that her psychotic content is *contagious to reality itself* because of the instrument. The cognitive disorganization is real even though the products of the disorganization are coherent.

**Self-concept during the break.** Wished. She is, briefly, the self the wound would have built had the wound been allowed to author her — princess, daughter, mother, sister, witch — every relational role intact, none of the losses real. This is what the grief had been silently constructing under the 1990s hollow: the negative-space outline of the unmourned life. *House of M* is that negative space, materialized.

---

## VIII. The Late 2000s through Early 2010s — Fugue, Pastoral, Reaching

**Affect regulation.** Dissociative. The post-*M-Day* period — culminating in the *Children's Crusade* arc (Heinberg/Cheung, 2010–12) — finds her in repeated fugue states: amnesiac, hidden in pastoral or domestic settings (Doom's castle in a domestic register; a small European village; later a hidden cottage). The clinical pattern is *dissociative flight* — *I cannot be the person who did what I did, so I will be no one, somewhere small and green.* The affect is *off* rather than dysregulated. The instrument is *muffled* rather than mastered.

**Cognitive style.** Amnesic, intermittently lucid, drawn toward *the shape of the lost life rather than its content.* She does not remember the children, but she *furnishes the rooms they would have inhabited.* She does not remember Vision but she lives in the kind of quiet house their marriage briefly was. The unconscious is still constructing the diorama; the conscious mind has been emptied so the construction can proceed without the unbearable knowledge.

**Self-concept.** Erased and tentatively rebuilding around small kindnesses. In the village periods she helps neighbors, tends gardens, performs minor magic on behalf of strangers. This is the same omnipotent-reparation drive that built *House of M*, *radically scaled down* to its sustainable form. The mechanism is identical. The dosage is therapeutic rather than catastrophic.

**The pivotal encounter.** Wiccan and Speed — the Young Avengers, the reincarnations of Thomas and William — find her. She does not recognize them at first; the memory has been erased twice now (once by Harkness, once by her own fugue). Then she weeps. This is the first time in her published record that grief arrives *as grief* — as tears, as a body holding a feeling without converting it to event. It is, clinically, a breakthrough. The presence of the lost objects, alive and standing in front of her, permits the feeling to be the feeling rather than the action. This is what the Bryant 2024 PGD literature describes as the *exposure* that adaptive grief work requires.

---

## IX. The Mid-2010s — Penitential Practice, Beginning of Discipline

**Affect regulation.** Slowly redeveloping. The Robinson *Scarlet Witch* solo (2015–17) shows her in *itinerant reparative practice* — traveling the world, helping witches, restoring corrupted magical traditions, paying back what she takes. Each episode is small. Each is *containable.* The instrument is being used at human scale, on human problems, with human-scale affect. She is, essentially, redoing the apprenticeship the universe stole from her when Harkness violated the memory and then died — but with no master, alone, on her own recognizance.

**Cognitive style.** Returning to the integrative-symbolic mode of the Harkness years, with a new ingredient: *historical consciousness.* She thinks about what her power *means*, what witchcraft *is*, what she *owes.* This is the cognitive register of moral reckoning. It is the first time her cognition has been organized around *responsibility* rather than around *attachment* or *survival.*

**Self-concept.** *Debtor.* The Robinson-era self-statement, recurring in various forms, is *I owe a debt I will spend my life paying.* This is, clinically, a *shame-organized* self-concept — not optimal, but enormously more functional than the *monster* self-concept of the immediate post-*Disassembled* years. Shame at least permits action; monster permits only flight or further destruction. *Debtor* is shame yoked to reparative work. It is the bridge identity.

---

## X. The Early 2020s — Death, Return, Naming, Integration

**Affect regulation.** The most mature presentation in her record. The Aaron *Avengers* / *Trial of Magneto* arcs (2021) include her death and return. The post-resurrection Wanda is *quieter* than any prior version. She has fewer reactive episodes. Her affect is broad — she laughs, she grieves, she rages — but the reactions are *proportioned* to the events. The instrument and the affect have begun, for the first time since the Harkness years and more deeply than then, to *uncouple* — she can feel without firing.

**Cognitive style.** *Naming.* The Aaron-era arcs force the narrative — and her — to *speak the children's names.* This is not sentimental; this is the precise clinical intervention the grief literature prescribes. Prolonged Grief Disorder treatment (Bryant 2024) centrally involves the patient *naming* the loss, *narrating* the loss, *integrating* the loss into autobiographical memory rather than dissociating from it. She does this, in the late record, *publicly* and *repeatedly.* This is the cognitive work the Harkness wipe prevented for thirty-five years of publication time. It is finally being done.

**Self-concept.** *Witch in service, mother who lost, sister, daughter — and finally, none of these only.* The integration project is taking a self capable of holding the contradictions: *I did the unforgivable thing; I am also the person who mentors apprentices, who helps witches, who shows up to fight beside the people I once killed.* This is the mature integration the literature recognizes as the favorable outcome of complicated grief work: not *forgiveness of self*, not *forgetting*, but *capacity to carry.*

**The remaining vulnerability.** The substrate schemas — *world is mob, safety is borrowed, brother is half of me, reality must yield* — are not eliminated. They are *managed.* Sufficient stress, sufficient loss, sufficient violation of her epistemic ground would still escalate her up the ladder. She has, however, learned for the first time in sixty years of record *that the ladder can be climbed back down,* and she has, for the first time, practiced doing it.

---

## XI. The Throughline — What Evolved, What Did Not

**What evolved.**
- Affect regulation moved from *externally borrowed* (1960s) → *disciplinarily acquired* (Harkness years) → *lost and performed* (1990s) → *catastrophically failed* (mid-2000s) → *dissociatively muffled* (late 2000s) → *reparatively re-acquired* (mid-2010s) → *integratively held* (early 2020s).
- Cognitive style moved from *compliant-magical* → *deliberative* → *integrative-symbolic* → *constricted-tactical* → *delusionally restructured* → *amnesic-pastoral* → *historically conscious* → *naming and narrating.*
- Self-concept moved from *embedded and undifferentiated* → *first-person and possessive* → *role-only hollow* → *wished and unreal* → *erased* → *debtor* → *carrier of contradictions.*

**What did not evolve, and what therefore remains the permanent risk surface.**
- The substrate schemas. The *world-is-mob*, *safety-is-borrowed*, *brother-is-half-of-me*, *reality-must-yield* axioms have never been dismantled. They have been built over, sometimes well. Under sufficient load, the building gives and the floor shows.
- The coupling of affect to instrument. Even at her most regulated, her power output remains affect-coupled. The coupling is *narrower* in the late record than ever before, but it is not severed and almost certainly cannot be — the instrument *is* her, and she *is* affect-driven by constitution.
- The pressure points. The children, Pietro, Magneto, Vision's memory, and the experience of being told her perception is wrong remain the five fast paths to escalation. The late-period Wanda *knows* this about herself. Knowing is not curing. Knowing is, however, the necessary precondition for the management she has, finally and at great cost, begun to practice.

**The clinical summation, longitudinally.** She is a patient who would have presented in any decade for treatment of Prolonged Grief Disorder with complex-traumatic features and recurrent reactive psychotic episodes — and who, by the late record, has done much of that treatment *on herself*, alone, without the teacher whose death and prior violation made the work necessary in the first place. The work is not finished. Work of this k


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Dossier Section 04 / Clinical. Compiled longitudinally from observed behavior across the full published record, 1964–present. Diagnostic framework: ICD-11 primary, DSM-5-TR cross-walk where useful. All inferences are behaviorally substantiated; the unusual mediating fact — that the subject's affective states are coupled to a reality-altering instrument — is held constant throughout, since to bracket it would be to misread every datum.*

---

## 4.1 ORIENTING NOTE: ASSESSING A PATIENT WHOSE SYMPTOMS REWRITE THE EVIDENCE

Before any diagnosis is offered, an epistemological caveat: every standard psychiatric assessment depends on the assumption that the patient's *internal* states (delusions, fantasies, fears) and *external* reality are separable, and that the clinician's reality-test is a stable referent. With this subject, that assumption fails. Her acute psychotic content does not stay inside her skull; it becomes the world the assessor is standing in. When she believed her children existed, they existed. When she believed mutantkind should be ninety-eight percent diminished, it was. This means:

- The **distinction between delusion and accurate-but-rare perception** cannot be made by usual means.
- The **distinction between affect and behavior** collapses; she has no autonomic-only emotion. Every feeling has a motor pathway through the world.
- The **distinction between memory and confabulation** is unstable, since her own mind has been edited by trusted figures (Harkness) and by hostile ones (Immortus) and since her power can retroactively manifest "memories" by manifesting their referents.

A working clinician must therefore treat the *behavioral signature* as primary evidence and treat her *self-report* as informative but not authoritative. This is the methodology used below.

---

## 4.2 PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS

### ICD-11 6B42 — Prolonged Grief Disorder, severe, with complicated/traumatic and iatrogenically-interrupted features

**Substantiation.** The Bryant (2024) RCT and Pop-Jordanova (2021) review converge on a portrait this subject fits with uncommon completeness: grief symptoms — yearning, preoccupation, identity disruption, disbelief, emotional pain, avoidance of reminders, difficulty re-engaging — that persist *too intensely, too long*, beyond what cultural and developmental expectations would predict, and that constitute a treatable disorder distinct from depression and PTSD though comorbid with both.

The criterial map for this subject:

- **Persistent yearning and preoccupation with the deceased.** The lost children (Thomas, William) are the gravitational center of her psyche across every era since 1989. In every quiet moment given to her by writers — the *Children's Crusade* pastoral hideaways, the Robinson-era domestic interiors, the recurrent dream sequences — the children return. She has, in clinical terms, never stopped looking for them, even in periods when she could not consciously remember them.
- **Intense emotional pain.** The behavioral indicators are unmistakable: the weeping recognition scenes (Wiccan, Speed), the body-collapse responses to even tangential references to the loss (the *Trial of Magneto* arc, where the act of being made to *say their names* is a near-fatal exertion).
- **Disbelief / denial regarding the loss.** This is, in her case, *literalized.* Most prolonged-grief patients deny in cognition only ("I cannot believe she is gone"); this subject denies in *ontology* ("she is not gone — see, here she is — I have made her be"). The defense is identical; the mechanism is escalated by her power.
- **Difficulty reintegrating into life.** Long stretches of her record show *performed* reintegration — she is in the lineup, she fights, she dates Wonder Man — over an affective hollow. The Busiek/Pérez period documents this with particular fidelity: a woman doing the motions of an Avenger while not, in any deeper sense, present.
- **Identity disruption.** The recurring "I don't know who I am anymore" content of post-*Disassembled* runs, the literal amnesia of the post-*M-Day* fugue years, and the destabilized self-concept ("monster" / "mother" / "witch" never integrated).

**Severity specifier: severe.** Functional impact has included episodes of mass-scale lethality and a planet-scale reality break. There is no higher severity available in the human-clinical instrument.

**Course specifier: complicated and iatrogenically interrupted.** Two features distinguish her case from ordinary prolonged grief:

1. The losses themselves were *violent, sudden, ontologically uncanny* — children revealed to have never had stable existence, then erased. Pop-Jordanova flags violent/sudden loss as a course-worsener. Add the epistemic injury (being told *the loss is not what you experienced it as*) and the case is built for complication from the start.
2. The grief was *surgically interrupted* by Agatha Harkness's memory-wipe (*Avengers West Coast* #52). In any human-clinical analog this is malpractice of a profound order — a trusted therapist excising rather than treating a wound. The predictable consequence is what we observed in 2004: complete return of unmetabolized affect, at full pressure, without any of the intervening processing that two decades of mourning would normally have done.

**Why this is the primary frame and not a comorbid one.** Across the sixty-year record, every other diagnosable phenomenon — the psychotic breaks, the PTSD features, the depressive periods, the relational instability — is *organized around and downstream of* the grief. Remove the grief and the rest does not stand. This is the etiologic spine.

---

## 4.3 SECONDARY DIAGNOSIS

### ICD-11 6A23 — Brief Psychotic Disorder, recurrent, with marked reactive features (grief-precipitated)

**Substantiation.** Discrete, time-limited episodes meeting psychosis criteria — loss of reality testing, delusional restructuring of the world, grossly disorganized behavior — occurring against an inter-episode baseline of substantively preserved reality contact, cognition, and self.

The two principal episodes:

- ***Avengers Disassembled* (2004).** Onset acute, hours-to-days after the recovered-memory trigger. Behavioral disorganization: indiscriminate lethal action against figures she objectively loved (Hawkeye), grotesque tableau-creation (the Vision dismantling, the Jack-of-Hearts staging), absence of strategic coherence — she does not flee, does not bargain, does not articulate demands. This is not villainy; it is a disorganized psychotic acute.
- ***House of M* (2005).** Onset prompted; behavior more organized but content unmistakably delusional — the wish-world is constructed with the internal logic of a dream (everyone gets what they most want, the contradictions hidden, the dreamer-figure central but unaware). Loss of insight is complete *within* the episode; her *parting* utterance ("no more mutants") shows the wound peeking through the dream as it collapses.

**Specifier: with marked stressor.** Both episodes are unambiguously precipitated — by recovered memory, by confrontation regarding her own fate. There is no idiopathic prodrome.

**Specifier: with reality-distortion via the patient's instrument.** This is not a standard specifier; the case requires the addendum. Her psychotic content is *enacted*, not merely believed. The diagnostic category remains psychosis; the medium is the unusual element.

**Lower-grade psychotic phenomena (sub-syndromal):**
- The fugue/dissociative episodes of the post-*M-Day* period (*Children's Crusade*) — pastoral hideouts at Doom's castle, small villages, repeatedly constructing simple domestic scenes she does not remember choosing. These are not full psychotic breaks but dissociatively-organized wish-states.
- The Byrne-era (*Vision Quest / Darker Than Scarlet*) dissociative-with-confusion presentation — lucid one panel, glassy the next — externally framed as Immortus manipulation but behaviorally consistent with stress-induced dissociation.

---

## 4.4 TERTIARY DIAGNOSIS

### ICD-11 6B41 — Complex PTSD

**Substantiation.** The criterial triad is met:

1. **Core PTSD symptoms.** Re-experiencing (the recurrent return of the children's memory across runs even when consciously suppressed), avoidance (the long performance-over-hollow stretches of the 1990s), persistent sense of current threat (hyperarousal coupled to power output — small startles produce hex-discharges).
2. **Disturbances in self-organization.**
   - *Affective dysregulation.* Documented across every era. The unusual feature is that dysregulation has *world-consequences*, which means she has, paradoxically, more incentive than any patient in clinical history to learn regulation, and the late-period record shows that learning underway.
   - *Negative self-concept.* "I'm a monster" is a recurring self-statement; the Robinson-era debt-framing ("I owe a debt"); the Orlando-era penitential mode. The shame is structural, not episodic.
   - *Interpersonal disturbance.* Difficulty sustaining intimacy outside of idealized-protector configurations; cyclical estrangement-reconciliation with Pietro; difficulty accepting care from peers (she gives more easily than she receives).
3. **Index trauma profile fits the C-PTSD aetiologic frame.** Repeated, prolonged, escape-difficult exposure: coerced militancy under Magneto in adolescence; multiple agency-violations (Immortus mind-control, Harkness memory-tampering, Mephisto soul-fragment intrusion via the children, Doom manipulation in *Children's Crusade*); repeated forced returns from death. This is precisely the profile (cumulative, interpersonal, with caregiver/authority betrayal) for which the C-PTSD construct was developed.

**Note on agency-violation as trauma-class.** Mind-control and memory-tampering are not catalogued in the diagnostic manuals in their literal forms (no one outside this subject's universe sustains them), but their *psychological weight* maps cleanly to repeated sexual assault, coercive control, and prolonged captivity in the human literature: the violation of bodily and mental sovereignty, the erosion of trust in one's own perceptions, the destabilization of consent and choice. She should be assessed with that severity in mind.

---

## 4.5 ADDITIONAL CLINICAL FEATURES (sub-diagnostic but relevant)

- **Persistent Depressive Disorder features**, ICD-11 6A72 analog: the inter-episode melancholy, the diminished hedonic capacity through the long 1990s, the somatic heaviness. Probably does not meet full duration criteria as a standalone diagnosis given the episodic structure, but the depressive baseline is real and should be treated.
- **Dissociative episodes**, ICD-11 6B6Z spectrum: documented in the Byrne arc, the *Children's Crusade* fugue years, and the post-*Disassembled* days she cannot account for. Sub-syndromal for a Dissociative Disorder diagnosis but a stable feature.
- **Iatrogenic mnestic injury**, no formal code: the Harkness memory-wipe and its sequelae warrant naming as a discrete injury-event regardless of its non-coding.
- **Power-dependence syndrome (behavioral analog of substance use).** Tolerance escalation (each major working larger than the last), affective coupling, withdrawal-collapse phenomena after major exertions, continued use despite catastrophic consequence to self and others. Not chemical; structurally identical.

---

## 4.6 COMORBIDITY MAP AND TEMPORAL SEQUENCING

The relationships among the above are not parallel — they are *causally layered.*

1. **Childhood and adolescent trauma load** (loss of mother, peasant-mob terror, Magneto coercion) establishes the C-PTSD substrate and the anxious-preoccupied attachment style.
2. The **constructed children and their reabsorption** (1986–89) install the index grief.
3. The **Harkness memory-wipe** prevents acute-grief processing — the *iatrogenic interruption* — and converts what would have been severe-but-resolvable acute grief into the structural Prolonged Grief Disorder.
4. The **fifteen-year latency** (1989–2004) is not health; it is encapsulation. The grief is held by amnesia and by performance.
5. The **recovered memory** (*Disassembled* trigger) detonates the encapsulation. The first **Brief Psychotic Episode** is the released grief finding the only outlet her instrument allows.
6. **Confrontation regarding her fate** (Avengers/X-Men summit) precipitates the second **Brief Psychotic Episode** (*House of M*), now organized around wish-fulfillment rather than rageful disorganization.
7. **Post-M-Day fugue years** are the dissociative-defensive aftermath — the psyche, having broken twice, retreats into amnesia and pastoral wish-states.
8. **Reunion with Wiccan and Speed** is the first piece of *external* reality that does not require her instrument to provide what she needs — the universe, for once, gives her something back.
9. The **late integrative period** (Robinson solo, Orlando run, *Trial of Magneto*) is the slow corrective: doing the grief-work that was denied her, supported by apprenticeship of others and by being named (forced to *speak the names*) rather than allowed to evade.

The sequencing matters diagnostically because it tells us *what to treat first* in any forward-looking intervention frame: the grief is upstream; psychosis-prophylaxis follows from grief-resolution, not the reverse.

---

## 4.7 DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT SHE IS NOT, AND WHY

This subject has been mis-labelled often, in-universe by frightened teammates and out-of-universe by readings that mistake catastrophe for character. The differentials must be done carefully.

### Not Borderline Personality Disorder

Surface resemblance is real: intense relationships, fear of abandonment, identity disturbance, affective storms, episodes that look "manipulative" from outside. The reasons it is not BPD:

- **Pervasiveness criterion fails.** BPD requires a *pervasive pattern* across multiple domains, present from early adulthood, stable across contexts. This subject's instability is *episodic*, organized around discrete catastrophic triggers, with long inter-episode stretches of substantively preserved functioning (the Englehart marriage-and-training period, the Busiek lineup years, the Robinson and Orlando solo runs). True BPD does not yield those stretches.
- **Identity disturbance is trauma-driven, not characterological.** Her self-concept fragments under specific triggers (the children, agency-violation) rather than fluctuating idiopathically.
- **Abandonment-fear pattern is specific, not generalized.** She fears the loss of *particular* attachments she has built defenses around; she does not exhibit the generalized frantic-efforts-to-avoid-abandonment pattern with new contacts.
- **No chronic emptiness baseline.** Between episodes she experiences meaning, purpose, vocation. Chronic emptiness is a BPD core feature; she does not have it.
- **Mature defenses available and used.** She mentors, she sustains apprenticeships, she does reparative work. The BPD defensive repertoire is more uniformly primitive.

### Not Schizophrenia Spectrum / Primary Psychotic Disorder

- **No prodrome documented in adolescence.** Her early-onset distress is trauma-and-coercion-explained.
- **No persistent negative symptoms** between episodes — affect remains rich, motivation present, social engagement sustained.
- **No formal thought disorder** in the inter-episode baseline. Speech and cognition are organized, often eloquent.
- **No characteristic auditory hallucinations** of the schizophrenic type. The voices she hears (Mephisto-fragment, possessions) are *externally* sourced in-universe; there is no idiopathic internal voice-content.
- **Psychosis is reactive, not primary.** Onset is precipitated; remission follows resolution of the precipitant rather than antipsychotic neurochemistry.

### Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder

The omnipotent acts invite the misreading. The reasons against:

- **Baseline self-concept is shame, not grandeur.** She does not enter the room believing herself superior; she enters it believing herself dangerous and unworthy. The grandiose acts are *defensive eruptions*, not stable structure.
- **Capacity for shame, guilt, and repair is intact and active.** NPD's defining feature is *failure* of those capacities. She has them in abundance — arguably to a punitive degree.
- **Empathy preserved, particularly for the marginalized.** NPD's empathic deficit is reliable; hers is absent. The tenderness toward witches, mutants, the uncanny is constitutional.
- **No exploitative interpersonal pattern.** She does not use others instrumentally; her relational failures are failures of *dependency and dysregulation*, not predation.

### Not Bipolar I or II

- **No sustained manic syndrome.** The "high" of a major working is intra-episode, hours-to-days, not the week-plus required for mania.
- **No documented decreased need for sleep, pressured speech, flight of ideas** in the bipolar pattern across any sustained period.
- **No discrete hypomanic episodes** with the bipolar signature (elevated mood, increased goal-directed activity, characteristic cognitive changes) inter-episode.
- The euphoria during reality-rewriting reads phenomenologically as **psychotic-affective** (mood-congruent with the delusional content) rather than as a primary mood-disorder elevation.

### Not Dissociative Identity Disorder

Despite the fugue states and the memory disruptions:

- **No discrete alters with their own names, histories, mannerisms.** Her dissociation is *state-based* (fugue, derealization, amnesia) not *identity-based*.
- **Identity disturbance fits the C-PTSD pattern** (fragmented, shame-saturated, unintegrated) rather than the DID pattern (multiplied, compartmentalized).
- **The memory gaps are explained** by trauma-induced dissociation, mind-control, and iatrogenic intervention — they do not require a DID frame.

### Not Antisocial Personality Disorder

The mass-lethality of *Disassembled* and the planetary harm of "no more mutants" invite this differential. It fails:

- **No callous-unemotional baseline.** The acts are committed in states of acute psychosis, not from a stable affective deficit.
- **Remorse is profound and sustained.** ASPD does not produce the post-event grief, the years-long penance, the self-flagellating reparative drive she has demonstrated.
- **No childhood conduct-disorder history.** Her childhood is one of fear and coerced compliance, not predation.

### Not Schizoaffective Disorder

- The mood disturbance and the psychosis are *temporally bound* (psychosis occurs *within* episodes of acute grief-decompensation), not running on independent or partially-overlapping tracks as schizoaffective requires.

### Not Substance-Induced or Substance-Use Disorder

- No chemical substance involved. The "intoxication" pattern is behavioral, mediated by her power. The structural analogy is informative; the diagnosis does not apply.

### Not Malingering or Factitious presentation

- Self-report and behavior are concordant; the disorder produces marked impairment with no secondary gain. She would rather not be this.

---

## 4.8 RISK FORMULATION

**Risk to self.** Moderate-to-high in acute decompensation, mediated through power-related self-harm (the deaths and resurrections) and through dissociative loss of self-protective behavior. Suicidality in the conventional sense is *not* the primary modality; the death-equivalent is *self-erasure into the wish-world*.

**Risk to others.** Highest of any subject in this dossier series during acute episodes (population-scale harm demonstrated). Approaches baseline-human between episodes — and below baseline, given her active reparative engagement.

**Risk modulators (protective).** Pietro present and grounded; apprenticeship/mentor relationships active; the children (Wiccan, Speed) acknowledged and reachable; therapeutic naming of the loss permitted rather than suppressed; a teacher-figure (Harkness analog, but corrective this time) available.

**Risk modulators (aggravating).** Isolation from chosen family; suppression or denial of the children's reality by trusted figures; agency-violation by external forces; recovered-memory events without supportive framing; confrontation framed as ultimatum rather than offer.

---

## 4.9 PROGNOSTIC NOTE

Prolonged Grief Disorder is, per Bryant (2024), *treatable* — meaningfully so, by CBT-grief and mindfulness-based approaches that target the avoidance, the disbelief, and the identity-reconstruction work. The fact that this subject's mourning has been so often interrupted (by amnesia, by external manipulation, by her own instrument's ability to substitute wish for work) is the central reason the disorder has lasted decades; it is *not* a reason the disorder is untreatable.

The late-period record is, in clinical reading, the prognosis-positive evidence: she is doing the work. The naming in *Trial of Magneto*; the apprenticeships; the willingness to face rather than rewrite. If those conditions hold — chosen family, named grief, no further iatrogenic interruption, support for the gradual decoupling of affect from instrument — the trajectory is *toward integration*, not toward repeated catastrophe.

The disorder is the predictable outcome of the inputs in the order they arrived. The recovery, equally, is possible on the inputs now available. The clinical task, were one ever in a position to perform it, is to keep those inputs in place and to not, *ever again*, surgically remove a grief that should have been treated.


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF ("SCARLET WITCH")

*Compiled longitudinally from sixty years of observed behavior, cross-checked against the somatic/affective coupling documented in §2 and the defense-hierarchy in §3. Where a tell appears in only one era it is flagged; where it persists across decades it is treated as durable signature.*

---

## I. THE BODY AT REST — BASELINE OBSERVABLES

Begin with the woman before any stimulus reaches her. The baseline is not "neutral"; it is *occupied*. Surveillance of unscheduled, unobserved hours — kitchen, library, the long pre-dawn windows when she cannot sleep — yields a remarkably consistent set of micro-behaviors that constitute her resting signature.

**Hands.** The single most diagnostic surface on her body. At true rest the hands are folded — left over right, palms inward, the right thumb stroking the back of the left hand in a slow, metronomic pulse. Watch the thumb: it is the analog tachometer of her interior. Slow stroke (one cycle per two-to-three seconds) is baseline; faster stroke is interior weather; cessation, paradoxically, is the warning — *when the thumb stops moving, the hands are about to do something else.* In private, when she believes herself unobserved, the hands drift to the lower abdomen and rest there briefly before she notices and moves them. The gesture is unconscious and post-1986; it is the somatic memory of the pregnancy.

**Eyes.** Dark, expressive, and *long-focused* — she looks at middle and far distance more than at near objects, even in conversation. She tracks light sources. In any room she enters, within forty seconds she will have located: the windows, the strongest single light, and the highest point of the ceiling. This is not tactical sweep — it is the witch-trained habit of orienting to flow. She blinks slightly less often than population mean during conversation and slightly more often during silence; the inversion is characteristic.

**Mouth.** A small, asymmetric resting set — the left corner marginally lower than the right. Reads as melancholic-attentive. Genuine smiles arrive late and bloom outward from the eyes first; courtesy smiles begin at the mouth and never reach the eyes (the differential is usable).

**Voice.** Mid-register, slightly husky, carries a hard-to-place accent shaped by displaced childhoods — the consonants soften when she is tired or emotional, and a Romani/Eastern-European cadence (long vowels, lifted phrase-ends) emerges that is suppressed in her public/Avengers register. The accent is a tell of state: more accented = more interior. In English-language environments she translates internally before speaking on emotionally loaded subjects, which produces a characteristic half-beat of delay that observers mistake for hesitation; it is actually translation.

**Hair.** Long, dark-with-mahogany-auburn undertones, almost always loose. She pushes it back behind the right ear with the right hand in a single gesture that recurs every few minutes; this is her most frequent voluntary self-touch. When she ties it back, *she is about to work* — combat, ritual, or focused magical practice. The hair-tie is a behavioral predicate.

**Skin.** Warm brown, with the faint visible flush at the throat and cheekbones that is the most reliable early indicator of magical arousal — the chaos-signature pinks the capillary bed before it lights the hands. Trained surveillance reads the throat, not the fingers.

**The hands as instrument.** At absolute baseline the hands carry no visible aura. Under mild affect, the fingertips warm and a faint scarlet shimmer appears in the lunulae of the fingernails — visible in low light, invisible in bright. Under moderate affect, the shimmer climbs to the first knuckles. Under high affect, the whole hand glows and the air around the wrists distorts the way air distorts above hot pavement. The progression is *gradient and readable*; she does not "flip on." Anyone trained to watch the hands has between two and eight seconds of warning.

**Costume / dress.** Off-duty she favors long skirts, layered dark fabrics, a long coat in deep red or oxblood when she expects to be seen as Scarlet Witch and in earth tones when she does not. Jewelry is sparse — a thin chain at the throat that she touches when thinking, occasional rings, no watch (she reads time off light). The crimson coat is uniform and totem; she puts it on the way a soldier puts on body armor and a priest puts on a stole — simultaneously.

**Sleep.** Poor and irregular across the entire longitudinal record. She sleeps in fragments — three to four hours initial, waking near 3 a.m., reading or walking for an hour, then a second shorter sleep toward dawn. Insomnia is worst in spring (the season the children were born) and around the anniversary of the *Disassembled* events; she does not consciously track these dates but her body does.

---

## II. CALM — THE FUNCTIONING DAY

When nothing is pressing — a rare condition, but documented across the Robinson and Orlando solo runs and the quieter Avengers interludes — her behavior reorganizes around small rituals of *making*. Tea is brewed, not poured from a pot. Bread is occasionally baked. Plants are kept and tended, and she talks to them in low Romani phrases she would deny using if asked. She reads — heavily, and across registers: occult primary sources, poetry (Akhmatova, Lorca, the Romani oral tradition in translation), and, conspicuously, parenting books and children's literature, which she keeps on a lower shelf and does not discuss.

**Decision-making, calm.** Slow, consultative, slightly avoidant of finality. She will turn a small decision (which café, which route, which spell to teach an apprentice first) over with a companion three or four times before settling. This is not indecision — it is *the pleasure of having decisions small enough to take time over.* In a life where most choices have been catastrophic, the trivial ones are savored. She defers to companions on low-stakes choices to a degree that reads as politeness and is partly something else: *practiced non-imposition*, a learned counter-discipline against a power that imposes by default.

**Movement.** She walks rather than drives when given the choice; the walk is unhurried, slightly drifting, with frequent stops to look at things — a wall, a window, a tree. She touches surfaces with the fingertips when passing. This is partly aesthetic, partly magical reconnaissance (she reads residues), and partly grounding behavior, the trained tactile anchor of a dissociation-prone subject.

**Social.** Warm, attentive, asks more questions than she answers. Remembers small biographical detail with unusual accuracy — children's names, anniversaries, the small griefs of people she has met once. This is partly empathy and partly the *witch's notebook*, a habit of cataloguing the soft data of other lives. She is not a confider; she is a confidant. The asymmetry is durable and intentional.

**Eating.** Small portions, slow, and a marked preference for foods of her childhood (paprika-heavy, root vegetables, stewed things) and for sweets at off-hours. She drinks tea constantly and coffee almost never. Alcohol — wine, occasionally, never spirits, never to intoxication; she will not surrender even mild control of consciousness, and this restraint long predates her diagnostic awareness of why.

**Magic at calm.** Practiced as discipline, daily, in small applications — a candle lit without a match, an object retrieved across the room, the small probability nudges (a traffic light, a found parking space) that she has stopped pretending to herself she does not perform. The morning practice is consistent: thirty to ninety minutes, alone, before others wake. This is her keel.

---

## III. STRESS — EARLY, MID, AND COMPOUNDING

Stress is not a single state for her; it climbs a ladder, and each rung has its own observables.

**Early stress (annoyance, pressure, mild conflict).** The thumb-on-hand stroke accelerates. She becomes quieter rather than louder — the volume of her speech drops about ten percent and the pace slows. The Romani cadence surfaces in the consonants. She withdraws to the edge of rooms; if standing, she finds a wall to be near (not against — *near*, with a few inches of clearance). She begins to touch the throat-chain. The capillary flush at the throat is faintly visible. Magically, the lunulae shimmer.

**Mid stress (sustained pressure, multiple demands, presence of someone she does not trust).** Speech reduces further. She begins to answer questions with questions — not deflection so much as a stalling mechanism that gives her a half-second to translate. The hair-push behind the right ear increases in frequency. She rises and walks — pacing is rare for her, but *circumambulation* (slow, perimeter, eyes on the windows) is characteristic. She will leave a room briefly under the pretext of getting tea or making a call and use the absence to regulate. The hands begin to warm visibly.

**Compounding stress (when she cannot regulate down).** A specific shift in posture: she draws her shoulders down and back rather than up — the opposite of the population norm under stress, and a learned discipline from Harkness-era training. The chin lifts slightly. To inexperienced observers she now looks *more composed*, which is the inverse of the reality. The hands are kept clasped or behind the back deliberately, hidden from view; this is the single most important tell that she has crossed from manageable into dangerous interior weather. **When her hands disappear from view, escalation is imminent.**

Additional compounding markers: the accent becomes pronounced enough to be remarked on; she begins, without realizing it, to murmur in Romani under her breath — short phrases, often invocations of protection or fragments of prayers her mother taught her; she will not eat; she will not sit. The throat-flush is now obvious. The air around her cools by a degree or two — a physical effect of chaos-signature drawing local entropy — and observers report the room "feeling odd" before they can identify why.

**Decision-making under stress.** Quality degrades along a specific axis: she becomes *more deferential to authority figures and more decisive against threats to dependents.* The first is regressive (the frightened girl looking for the rescuer); the second is the protective drive surfacing. She will accept a plan from Captain America or Strange under stress that she would have argued with at baseline, and she will act unilaterally to defend an apprentice or child without consultation when she would have collaborated at baseline. Both are predictable.

---

## IV. THREAT — IMMINENT VIOLENCE, DIRECT DANGER

The threat-state is qualitatively different from stress and behaviorally distinct from grief-decompensation; it is the cleanest of her states because it engages a trained Avenger.

**Onset.** The transition is *fast and visible.* The hair goes back — either tied or pushed and held; the shoulders drop further; the breath deepens and slows (a trained four-count). The hands come *up* and *out* — palms forward at hip level, fingers slightly spread. The lunulae light; within seconds the whole hand carries scarlet aura. The eyes harden — the long-focus shortens to mid-range, scanning. The melancholic mouth-set vanishes; the jaw sets.

**Movement.** Economical and oddly graceful. She does not run unless cover demands it; she *positions*. She places herself between threats and non-combatants by default and without discussion. Against a single opponent she stands her ground; against multiple she will circle clockwise (always clockwise — this is consistent across decades and is a magical-traditional habit), establishing a small territory she controls.

**Verbal.** Sparse and clipped during combat. Single words, short phrases, often in mixed English-Romani-Latin (the Latin is incantatory residue from Harkness training). She does not banter. She does not threaten. She gives one warning, usually quiet, and then acts. *The warning is the tell* — if she has spoken to you in combat, she has not yet decided to end you; if she has stopped speaking, she has.

**Power use, threat-state.** Highly disciplined and graduated. She begins with the smallest sufficient intervention — a probability shift to disarm, a hex to disorient, a barrier. She escalates only as needed. She does not use reality-rewriting in threat-state; that capacity is gated behind grief, not behind danger. A purely tactical Wanda is a relatively predictable Wanda, and competent opponents have exploited this — she fights *fair* until the fight stops being about combat and becomes about loss, at which point fair ends.

**After threat resolves.** Decompression is slow and visible. The aura recedes from hands to fingertips to lunulae over one to three minutes. The shoulders stay set. She will seek a wall or a seat and put her back to something solid. She will not speak for several minutes. She will refuse comfort offered too quickly and accept it offered after a pause. The first thing she eats or drinks after combat she will share — this is consistent and intentional, a small ritual against the isolation of violence.

---

## V. INTIMACY — THE RARE OPEN STATE

Intimacy here means the full register: romantic, familial-by-choice, mentor/apprentice, deep friendship. The behaviors differ slightly by relation but share a core signature.

**Approach.** Slow. She does not initiate physical contact in the early phase of any bond; she *receives* it and, over time, reciprocates. The first time she initiates touch with a new intimate is a behavioral milestone — usually a hand to the forearm, brief, deliberate, *and then a slight withdrawal to gauge response.* The withdrawal is the tell of someone who has had touch turn into possession too many times.

**Speech, intimate register.** The accent fully surfaces. She uses diminutives and endearments in Romani and Sokovian-inflected forms — *little one, my heart, dove* — and reserves English endearments for public or performative warmth. She will tell stories of her brother before she tells stories of her mother before she tells stories of her children; the ordering is consistent and reveals depth-of-trust.

**Romantic / partner register.** Tender, attentive, slightly worshipful in early phase — she idealizes (see §3 attachment notes), and the idealization is *visible* in extended eye contact, soft repetition of the partner's name, a tendency to position her body angled toward the partner even in groups. She is physically careful — her power's coupling to affect means she cannot lose herself the way population-norm subjects can during intimacy; she has learned to remain partially observing, and partners over the decades have variously read this as attentiveness or as held-back. Both are true.

**With Pietro specifically.** The enmeshment is observable in micro-behavior: they finish each other's sentences less than reputation suggests but *breathe in synchrony* when seated together, which is unusual and durable. She tracks his location in a room without looking. She softens around him and also becomes younger — her posture and word-choice regress slightly toward adolescent register in his presence, which is one of the cleanest signs of the unresolved fusion.

**With Vision (and successors of that valence).** A specific stillness — she becomes very quiet, very contained, and watches him with a kind of patient gravity, as if memorizing. The behavior is grief-adjacent even when he is alive and well; she has learned, the hard way, that he is the kind of thing the world takes back.

**With apprentices, dependents, and Wiccan/Speed.** Here she is most fully herself, because the protector-role lets her metabolize her own unmet needs through the giving of them. She is patient to a degree that surprises observers; she repeats instructions without irritation; she remembers each apprentice's particular fears and adapts. Physical affection with Wiccan and Speed specifically is *cautious and saturated* — she does not over-touch them (the wound of having created and lost them is too near) but when she does, she does not let go quickly. The first embrace of each reunion is the longest.

**Confiding.** Rare. She will share factual biography readily and emotional interpretation almost never. Direct questions about the children, about Vision, about Magneto receive short answers and a closure of the body. The signal that she is *about to* confide is specific: she will get up, move to the window, stand with her back partly turned, and begin speaking to the glass. *Confidences are delivered to her own reflection more than to the listener.* Surveillance protocols should preserve audio of window-side episodes with particular care.

---

## VI. GRIEF — THE OCCUPYING WEATHER

Grief is not an episode for her; it is the climate against which all other states are weather. The behaviors documented here are present chronically at low intensity and surge under cue.

**Anniversaries and triggers.** She does not consciously track the dates — she has refused, repeatedly, to keep a calendar of her losses — but the body keeps them. Spring (the children's birth-season) produces a low-grade somatic depression: fatigue, appetite reduction, longer baths, longer silences. The anniversary of *Disassembled* — which she cannot name without distress — produces insomnia that approaches total. The anniversary of Vision's first dismantling produces a specific behavior: she will spend the day with mechanical objects, repairing what is broken, often something small and domestic (a clock, a lamp). The reparative displacement is transparent and she half-knows.

**Acute grief-cue response.** The mention of the children's names by an outsider, the sight of a child of the relevant age, the smell of certain foods (the borscht-adjacent stew her grandmother made), photographs of Vision in his original red-and-green configuration, the word *mutant* used cruelly. Response sequence: a held breath of one to three seconds; the right hand to the throat-chain or the lower abdomen; the eyes drop to middle distance; the throat-flush appears; she will excuse herself if she can and absent herself for between four and forty minutes. She returns composed, slightly cooler, and the topic does not get reopened.

**Sustained grief behavior.** When unable to absent herself — long missions, social obligations, public-facing duties — she develops a *thinness of presence.* She is physically present and verbally functional but the long-focus extends further; she answers slightly after the beat; the smile is the courtesy smile, not the eye-smile. Companions of long acquaintance recognize this and protect her without comment; newer companions read it as coldness, which is incorrect.

**The crying pattern.** She cries rarely in public and silently when she does — no sound, the shoulders do not move, the tears track and she does not wipe them quickly. In private, observed only in deepest surveillance, she weeps differently: harder, with sound, often face-down, often briefly. The private weeping is contained to short bursts (five to fifteen minutes) and followed by a return to function. She does not allow herself longer; she does not trust what would happen if she did.

**Grief and power.** This is the dangerous coupling. Unmetabolized grief leaks into power-output as instability: small things go wrong around her — light bulbs, electronics, glasses falling without apparent cause, dreams of others in the building turning strange.
