This is field-documented and is the reason cooler heads on the team have, more than once, sent him in alone.

---

### C. Other / Latent Romantic Field

The file records additional flickers — a sorcerer-colleague during her solo-period travels, a witch-mentor figure whose relationship crossed into the erotic in implication if not in confirmed text, a complicated tenderness with a fellow chaos-adjacent practitioner during the modern solo run. Pattern across the field: **she chooses partners who are extraordinary, who can survive her, and who carry their own grief.** Ordinary people are off the menu not because she rejects them but because she fears, with grounds, that they could not survive proximity to her instrument. This is not snobbery; it is an act of protection that costs her access to the kind of small, daily love she most needs.

---

## II. RIVALS

### A. The Wasp-Sting Master (her brother-in-law, the senior Avenger)

A rivalry conducted in registers of *competence and judgment* rather than open hostility. He is the senior strategist; she is the unpredictable instrument. In the Roger Stern run he chairs the team during the period she briefly co-chairs; the institutional friction is real. He has, on record, voted against her in team-discipline matters more often than for her, and his measured skepticism of her power has, in her interior accounting, mapped onto *the men who decided what to do about her without asking her.* She does not hate him; she does not trust his vote. He, for his part, respects her power and fears it, and has been honest about both. **Failure mode:** procedural — he will follow a protocol that, applied to her, becomes inhumane, and will be slow to see the inhumanity until it is enacted. **Leverage:** he is one of the few who can address her *as an Avenger* (not as a witch, not as a daughter, not as a mother) and have it land; this is a register she sometimes needs and sometimes resents.

### B. The Senior Sorcerer Supreme

A rival in the *magical* register and one of the few practitioners in the published world whose raw capacity exceeds hers in technical depth (if not in raw output). The relationship has oscillated between collegial consultation and explicit antagonism — most sharply when he, in the post-*M-Day* period, was among those who argued that her power should be contained, monitored, or stripped. She experiences him as the *adult professional* she could have been had her training not been interrupted, and the experience is humiliating; he experiences her as a force whose education was uneven and whose discipline he cannot finish for her. **Failure mode:** condescension. He cannot help speaking to her as a junior, and she cannot help hearing it as Magneto did. **Leverage:** he knows the cosmology of her power better than she does, and there are questions she cannot answer without consulting him. This dependency wounds her.

### C. The God of Mischief / The Trickster Field

Less a single person than a category of antagonist — figures who manipulate appearance, identity, and reality at the conceptual level. With these she is *most herself and most at risk* simultaneously, because her own power is in their idiom; she is the only one in most rooms who can match them in the medium, but she is also the one most easily *tricked* in that medium, because her reality-testing is her weakest faculty. The trickster god in particular has used her as a proxy in at least one major arc, and the residue is a wariness that bleeds into any encounter with an obvious shape-shifter or illusionist. **Failure mode:** she trusts the picture she is shown. **Leverage:** by definition, total — anyone with sufficient skill in this register can write a world she will believe.

### D. The Atlantean Monarch and the Sub-Mariner-Class Rivals

A different register: rivals of *temper and sovereignty.* These are figures who, like her at her worst, believe their grief entitles them to reshape the world. The mutual recognition is uncomfortable. She is, with such figures, both more patient than the team expects (she sees herself in them) and more cutting when they cross a line (she has seen where their road ends, and refuses to indulge it).

---

## III. ENEMIES

### D. The Time-Lord (Immortus)

**History.** First substantive contact in the *Vision Quest / Darker Than Scarlet* arc (1989–90). He had been an off-stage manipulator earlier in her marriage — the file now indicates he engineered the children's metaphysical possibility precisely to harvest her resulting reality-altering breaks for his own chronal purposes. He is, by this reading, the *architect of her worst injury*: he is the one who set up the magical pregnancy to fail, knowing the fallout.

**Dynamics.** She does not engage him as a person; she engages him as a *condition.* He is the proof that her interior life has been instrumentalized by powers older and patient. When she becomes aware of him in a scene, her behavioral signature shifts to dissociation faster than with any other antagonist — she goes glassy, voice flattens, hands still. The body has learned that he is not someone you fight; he is someone who has already fought you and you are inside his result.

**Evolution.** Phase one (unknowing): she is his asset and does not know it. Phase two (the reveal during *Vision Quest*): a betrayal that retroactively rewrites her own marriage as a chess game. Phase three (post-knowledge): a settled hatred and a refusal to think about him, which is itself a survival strategy.

**Trust/safety.** Zero, and not even the kind of zero that produces vigilance; the kind that produces resignation.

**Failure mode.** She cannot fight him on his terms because his terms are temporal; she can only refuse to be the version of herself he is harvesting. This is a discipline she has been intermittently capable of and intermittently not.

**Leverage.** He has, by his manipulations, *authored portions of her biography.* Anyone holding his records, were they ever to surface, holds blackmail of an unusual kind: the proof that some of her worst acts were *scripted* and the simultaneous proof that her best memories were *scripted too.* She would rather not know which is which.

---

### E. The Soul-Trader (Mephisto)

**History.** The originating contamination of her children's substance was his soul-stuff, harvested back when the children were "reabsorbed." Subsequent contact across decades has positioned him as a recurring tempter, particularly in arcs where her children's resurrected forms (Wiccan, especially) are the bargaining chip.

**Dynamics.** With him she is *cold.* The behavioral data is consistent: in his presence she does not weep, she does not shout; she becomes precise. He is the one antagonist she has never decompensated in front of, because the cost of decompensating in front of him is too well known to her. She bargains with him only when she has no other instrument; she refuses his bargains more often than she accepts.

**Evolution.** Phase one (off-stage, unknown): he is the substrate of her constructed motherhood and she does not know it. Phase two (revealed): a category-defining enemy. Phase three (modern): a manageable hostility in which she has learned to refuse his offers without taking the bait of his framing.

**Trust/safety.** Zero, vigilant zero — the productive kind. She knows his shape.

**Failure mode.** He has time. She does not. He can wait for the one day she is desperate enough to accept his deal, and the file indicates that day has nearly arrived more than once.

**Leverage.** Her children's metaphysical status is his domain. Anything that threatens their continuity routes, eventually, through him. This is the single largest standing leverage in her file from any antagonist.

---

### F. The Iron-Willed Doctor (Doom)

**History.** Contact through the *Children's Crusade* arc most explicitly: he sheltered her in his castle during one of her amnesiac fugue periods, and the arc revealed that his interest in her was not paternal but acquisitive — her power, fused with his sovereignty, would have made him a god. The relationship oscillates between *the man who was kind to me when I had nowhere else* and *the man who used my fugue to study me.*

**Dynamics.** With him she is *guarded but conversant.* He treats her with a courtesy no one else in her enemy field offers, and she has noticed and partly accepted it; the courtesy is real even though the intent is predatory. He is the antagonist most likely to be invited to tea and most likely to leave with her diagnostic profile in his coat pocket. She knows this and tolerates it within limits.

**Evolution.** Phase one (admirer-from-distance): his interest predates direct contact, expressed in observation rather than approach. Phase two (the fugue-shelter): genuine succor offered, genuine data extracted. Phase three (the post-*Crusade* settlement): a stable, low-temperature antagonism in which she does not visit him and he does not approach her. Phase four (intermittent): he reappears when her power-signature spikes, the way a vulture reappears at a wound.

**Trust/safety.** Subjectively higher than is rational, because of the kindness extended during her vulnerability. Objectively low — he would absorb her power if he could. She knows this in the abstract and forgets it in the particular.

**Failure mode.** He understands her grief as an instrumentality; she sometimes lets herself be understood that way because being understood at all is rare for her.

**Leverage.** He can offer her a frame — sovereignty, order, the protection of a domain — that resonates with the deepest *negative* template in her psyche (the Magneto template). He can speak in the voice that, against her conscious wishes, parts of her still want to obey.

---

### G. The Reality-Engine (Mojo / Mr. Sinister / the broader exploiter class)

A category of antagonist who has, across runs, sought to *harvest* her power — Sinister most acquisitively, the gladiator-impresario most exploitatively. With these she is brisk and contemptuous; they hold no psychological leverage because they do not pretend to understand her, only to use her. **Failure mode:** none specific to her — these are routine antagonisms in which her power, not her psyche, is at stake. **Leverage:** technical. They have, on at least two occasions, possessed equipment capable of channeling or stripping her power, and the threat of such equipment is the one threat she takes physically rather than emotionally.

---

### H. The Mutant Population, Aggregate (as residual enemy)

A unique category in the file: a population she *wronged* and a population that, in aggregate, became thereafter a low-grade hostile audience to her existence. She has been hunted by individual mutants for the M-Day act (most explicitly by those who lost their powers and their lives in the depowering cascade). The relationship is not with any one figure but with a *category* — the same category her father claimed sovereignty over and the same category she struck in displaced rage at her father. The post-*M-Day* years have been, in part, a long attempt at reparation to this aggregate enemy. **Failure mode:** there is no reparation sufficient to the scale of the act, and she knows this, and the knowledge is a permanent low-grade depressant in her affective field. **Leverage:** the category as a whole holds permanent moral leverage; she has organized portions of her late-life work around accepting that.

---

### I. The Father (as enemy register)

He appears in this section as well as in the family file because his relational status with her is *unresolved* and routinely flips between estranged-parent and active-antagonist. In the enemy register: he is the figure who first weaponized her, who returned to claim her at the worst moments of her later breaks (*House of M*), and whose ideology she replicates at her worst. The enemy-version of him is the one who *uses* her grief as a lever — telling her, in the run-up to *House of M*, that the rewrite is owed her. **Failure mode:** she cannot kill him; she can only refuse to become him, and the refusal must be renewed daily. **Leverage:** he can name her as his daughter and have the naming move her, even when she has decided it should not.

---

### J. The Self (the enemy in the mirror)

Listed here because the file would be incomplete without it. The single most reliably hostile figure in her record is the version of herself that emerges under unmetabolized grief — the figure who wrote the children into being, who rewrote the world for them, who said the three words that depowered a species. She refers to this figure across runs in the third person ("she did that," "that wasn't me, but it was me"), which is diagnostically significant: the dissociative split between her baseline self and her decompensated self is internalized as an enmity. The integrative project of her late period — the work the Aaron *Trial of Magneto* arc forced into the open — is precisely the project of *retiring this enmity*, of taking the figure in the mirror back into the self and ceasing to call her an enemy. The file's judgment is that this work is unfinished but is, for the first time, actually underway.

---

## IV. CROSS-CUTTING OBSERVATIONS

**The categories braid.** Her synthezoid husband was, briefly, an instrument of institutional enemies. Her ionic almost-lover was, briefly, a rival on the team. Her father is both intimate (parent) and adversary (manipulator). Her own self is enemy. This braiding is itself diagnostic: the subject has limited capacity to *cleanly categorize* a relationship as one thing, and this is not a cognitive failure — it is an accurate response to the world she has lived in, where the same person has often been, in sequence, all three.

**The pattern of selection.** Across lovers, rivals, and enemies alike, she is drawn to figures of *unusual power and unusual grief.* Ordinary persons are rare in her field. This is partly opportunity (she lives in the world she lives in) and partly selection (she does not see ordinary persons as relevant interlocutors for the questions she lives with). The cost is documented above: she lacks the ordinary daily-love and ordinary daily-conflict that build the affect-regulation skills she most needs.

**The pattern of repair.** The relationships that have repaired her, in the long arc, are the ones in which the other party *stayed across her worst* — the synthezoid husband across his dismantling, the brother across decades of estrangement, the late apprentices across her admitted history. The relationships that have damaged her are the ones in which the other party *used her worst as material.* The taxonomy is clean even when the persons in it are not.

**Operational note for any successor file.** The single most predictive question to ask, when assessing any new figure entering her relational field, is not *what do they want from her* but *what do they do when she is in extremis.* The lovers and the enemies sort themselves on that axis, and the sort is more reliable than self-report from either party.


## Powers, Abilities & Their Limits

# POWERS, ABILITIES & THEIR LIMITS

## 0. Preliminary Framing — Why This Section Is Longer Than It Looks

For most subjects in this dossier system, "powers & abilities" is a tactical inventory: what they can do, at what range, with what cooldown. For this subject it cannot be. The instrument is not separable from the psyche. The autonomic arousal of an ordinary person reddens a face; hers reshapes a room. To inventory her capabilities is therefore to inventory her affective states, because the catalogue of what she can do is identical to the catalogue of what she has felt strongly enough to externalize. This section is structured accordingly: mechanism first, then range and limit, then a longitudinal growth curve, then signature applications, and — finally and most importantly — the **symptom-as-signature** reading in which every "power" is decoded back to the wound that taught her she needed it.

---

## 1. MECHANISM — WHAT THE POWER ACTUALLY IS

The published record has revised the mechanism three times. Operationally, the revisions are less interesting than the consistent phenomenology that persists across all of them.

**Stratum A — "Hex power" / probability alteration (1964–1989, Lee/Thomas/Englehart/Byrne).** The subject gestures (right hand canonical; both hands when scaling), a red-orange glow originates at the fingers and wrists, and the target locus experiences a sudden alteration in the probability of some otherwise-unlikely event. A gun jams. A rope frays. A wall fractures along a stress line that was always there but should not have failed today. The gesture is constrained: she must perceive the target (line-of-sight, with rare clairvoyant exceptions), she must will a specific class of outcome, and the alteration is bounded by physical plausibility — she is not creating; she is *biasing*.

**Stratum B — Chaos magic (Englehart Vision-and-Scarlet-Witch maxis, post-Harkness tutelage, formalized 1980s onward).** The probability alteration is recoded as one expression of a primordial magical category — *chaos* — to which she has hereditary or destinal access. Outcomes are no longer bounded strictly by plausibility. Matter can be created (the children), entities summoned, transmutations achieved. The gesture is still hand-led; the energy color deepens from orange-red to a denser carmine.

**Stratum C — Reality alteration / nexus-being (Bendis, Disassembled and House of M, 2004–05; later regularized).** The bound between "biasing reality" and "rewriting reality" collapses. She does not edit outcomes within the world; she edits the world itself. The gesture is no longer required; in the *House of M* sequence, she lies recumbent and the rewrite unfolds without observable somatic effort.

**Stratum D — Witchbreed / inheritance (Aaron *Trial of Magneto* / *Avengers Forever*, 2021– ).** The power is reframed once more as the patrimony of a witch-line — biological-occult heritability replacing nexus-being abstraction. Functionally indistinguishable from Stratum C; symbolically important because it locates her power in a *lineage of women*, which becomes relevant to her late-period reparative work.

**The consistent phenomenology — what surveillance would actually record across all four strata:**

- **Hand-led somatic channel.** Right hand dominant; left hand recruited at higher output. Fingers spread, wrist slightly cocked back, palm presenting. When she is concentrating without discharge, the fingers flex in small idiomatic loops — a *pre-gesture* tic that is one of the most reliable behavioral tells in this entire dossier.
- **Aura at the hands at rest.** A faint crimson penumbra, often invisible to ordinary observers in normal light, intensifying to luminous when discharge is imminent. The aura is *affect-coupled*: stronger when she is moved, suppressed almost to extinction when she is composed.
- **Eye-shift.** Under heavier output the irides take on a red cast; under maximal output (Disassembled, House of M, Trial) the entire sclera floods. This is involuntary and is the single most reliable threat-indicator.
- **Vocalization.** Murmured, often in Roma-inflected fragments or in pseudo-Latin / occult cadence (the verbal mechanism is more ritual scaffolding than necessity — she has discharged silently many times). The vocal pattern is *consoling herself as much as casting*; the prosody is closer to lullaby than incantation. This too is a tell.
- **Postural set.** Standing discharges: feet planted shoulder-width, slight forward inclination, chin lowered. Recumbent discharges (only under extreme states): supine, palms upturned, head tilted back. The recumbent set is a danger marker — it has only ever preceded catastrophic rewrites.

The mechanism, then, is best described not as one ability but as a *single continuous instrument with four registers of intensity*, each register accessing a wider gauge of effect, each register cued and amplified by affective load.

---

## 2. RANGE

**Spatial range** is, on paper, unbounded at Stratum C–D and contextually bounded at Strata A–B. In practice the working envelope across her career has been:

- **Fine work** (Stratum A; ordinary operating mode): within a few meters, requiring direct perception of the target. Jam a firearm. Cause a tile to slip. Trip an electrical fault. Most of her career in this register.
- **Mid-range combat** (Strata A–B): line-of-sight discharges out to roughly the limit of vision. Hex-bolts as projectile weapons, force impacts, defensive shielding. The bread-and-butter of her Avengers tenure.
- **Field range** (Stratum B): a city block to a battlefield, used for environmental manipulation — collapsing structures, redirecting weather (with strain), suppressing or amplifying broad classes of energy. The "vibration tuned to negate Vision's solidity" trick (*Avengers* 200s era) lives here.
- **Continental / planetary** (Stratum C): the *Disassembled* mansion-warp; the *House of M* world-rewrite; the *Trial of Magneto* mass-effect resurrections. Used only under catastrophic affect.
- **Cosmic / categorical** (Stratum C apex): the single utterance "No more mutants" — alteration not of bodies but of a *category of being*. This is the upper bound observed in the record.

**Temporal range.** Her edits persist after she ceases to attend to them — the constructed children remained children for years; the House of M world held against the combined will of the Avengers and X-Men until *she* released it; "No more mutants" required a decade-plus of in-universe metaphysical labor by other parties to even partially undo. She is not "maintaining" these effects; she is *promulgating* them, and they become law until specifically retracted.

**Range against intent.** The most telling range-limit is psychological, not physical: she has historically been unable to make her power work *for* a goal she does not, at some affective level, *want*. The classic embarrassment is the late-Englehart sequence where she tries to use her hex to do something neutral and competent and it sputters; thirty pages later, in extremis for someone she loves, the same hex levels a building. The instrument runs on conviction. This is also why training under Harkness made such a difference — Harkness did not increase her power; she taught Wanda to *want clearly enough for the instrument to respond.*

---

## 3. LIMITS — THE ACTUAL ONES

The published record presents her as near-omnipotent at peak. The *operational* limits are real and behaviorally specific.

**Limit 1: Affective coupling cuts both ways.** Power scales with feeling; therefore power *collapses* when she dissociates downward into numbness, and *runs away from her* when she dissociates upward into grief-rage. She has no manual throttle. The intermediate states — calm-and-determined — are where she does her best work, and they are the states she has historically had the least access to.

**Limit 2: Probability-shaped backlash.** Stratum-A hexes have a documented history of producing *unintended secondary outcomes* — the rope frays as commanded, but the falling debris injures a bystander. The power "rounds" toward chaos when her intent is unclear. Across her career she has been injured, embarrassed, and bereaved by her own hex-blowback more often than by enemy action. The Englehart-era running joke ("a hex against a hex") encodes the genuine principle: probability biased twice cancels, and chaos prefers the local maximum of disorder.

**Limit 3: Belief-permeability of the medium.** She is uniquely vulnerable to *being told what is real.* The same epistemic openness that lets her edit reality lets reality edit her. Immortus, Mastermind, Doom, Mephisto, Chthon — every major hostile she has faced from the magical-cosmic class has worked her through *induced belief* rather than direct force. The instrument that rewrites the world will, under pressure, accept a rewrite of itself.

**Limit 4: Iatrogenic memory-edit residue.** The Harkness intervention left a structural fault. Memories that *should* be hers can be made unavailable to her — and when they return, they return at full traumatic pressure, with the intervening years of unprocessed mourning compressed into a single moment. This is not a hostile limit; it is a *vulnerability* limit. Any actor with sufficient psychic or mnestic access can re-trigger the 2004 cascade.

**Limit 5: The Pietro override.** Under sufficient stress, her brother's voice can replace her judgment. The *House of M* rewrite is the documented worst case. This is not a power limit; it is a *governance* limit, and any actor who controls Pietro can, indirectly, steer her.

**Limit 6: Conscience.** This is the limit that has saved the world more than once. Even at her most decompensated, she has never deliberately killed a child. She has never targeted the unpowered as a class. She has never used her power to compel love (the constructed-children case is the boundary, and the children's love for her was not compelled — it was real and reciprocal within the construct). The instrument has a moral floor. The floor has cracked twice and held.

**Limit 7: Cost-to-self.** The catastrophic uses have all been followed by — in clinical terms — total decompensation: amnesia, fugue, collapse, withdrawal of years. The power has no observable physical cost during use; the cost is rendered *psychologically and metaphysically afterward*, with interest.

**Limit 8: Cannot un-grieve.** This is the most important limit and the one she has spent the late period of her record learning to name. The power can reconstruct the *form* of the lost (a world, a child, a husband-shape) but cannot reconstruct the *fact* of unbroken continuity with what was lost. The construct knows it is a construct. *She* knows it is a construct, however hard she works not to. The wish does not actually fulfill. This is the truth her recent runs have been forcing her to integrate.

---

## 4. GROWTH OVER TIME — A LONGITUDINAL POWER-CURVE

**Phase I (1964–1969, coerced novice).** Single hex per scene; visible somatic effort; frequent backlash; vocal incantation required. She is using ~10% of an instrument she does not understand.

**Phase II (1969–1975, Avengers integration, pre-Harkness).** Reliable mid-range combat use. Her hexes have become a recognizable tactical asset. Still no theoretical grasp of mechanism; still occasional backlash.

**Phase III (1975–1989, Harkness apprenticeship through pre-Vision Quest).** The transformative period. Under Harkness she acquires *category labels* for what she does — chaos, the witch-tradition, the True Will — and her output stabilizes. She can now sustain effects, layer effects, and create rather than only bias. The pregnancies and children are the highest-creative use of the period.

**Phase IV (1989–2003, post-Vision Quest, brittle plateau).** Power-level approximately steady; psychological foundation gutted; she fights well, leads briefly, dates Wonder Man, performs functionality. The *capability* curve and the *integration* curve diverge sharply here. She is more skilled than ever and less whole than ever.

**Phase V (2004–2005, decompensation cascade).** Stratum-C emerges. The power that was always latent in the instrument surfaces because the affective load finally exceeds the threshold required to access it. *Disassembled* is local-scale; *House of M* is planetary; "No more mutants" is categorical. This is not "growth" in any healthy sense — it is the instrument achieving its full range under conditions guaranteed to misuse it.

**Phase VI (2005–2014, fugue and reparation-fragments, Children's Crusade era).** She is amnesiac for long stretches; the power runs *quietly* in the background, building pastoral domesticities for her to hide in. When confronted with Wiccan and Speed she begins, slowly, to access integrated use again.

**Phase VII (2015–present, Robinson / Aaron / Orlando reparative period).** The mature curve. She is now *deliberately* using Stratum-B and limited Stratum-C work in service of repair — undoing curses laid by others, freeing trapped witches, mentoring, holding ground. Critically, she has begun to *refuse* Stratum-C work that would be easier than the slower B-and-below equivalent. This is the first time in her record she has *declined* the maximal use. It is the most important behavioral datum of her late career.

The arc of the curve, in one line: *she grew into her instrument backwards — full power before full self — and is now growing into her self with the full power already present.*

---

## 5. SIGNATURE APPLICATIONS

The repertoire that recurs across runs, in approximate order of frequency:

- **The hex-bolt.** Hand-projected, ranged, percussive. Default combat tool. The visual is consistent across artists: a coronal red discharge with a faint internal twist.
- **The probability-jam.** Subtle, often unattributed at the table. A gun won't fire. A door won't latch. A pursuer trips on a curb. Used in stealth and de-escalation contexts.
- **The shield-warp.** A defensive bubble or sheet of chaos-energy, used to deflect kinetic and energy attacks. Hand-traced perimeter.
- **The somatic disruption.** Used against Vision in their adversarial phases (controlled by enemies): tuning the air, or his density, to incapacitate. Used against synthetic and energy-form opponents generally.
- **The environmental collapse.** Stratum-B work. Bringing down a wall, a roof, a ridge. Frequently her finisher.
- **The summoning / sustained construct.** Stratum-B and above. The children are the apex case. Lesser cases include conjured creatures, illusion-bodies, and persistent wards.
- **The healing / undoing.** Underused but documented across the Orlando era. She lifts curses, mends broken witch-bonds, reverses possessions. This is the application she is *choosing* to grow into.
- **The reality-rewrite.** Stratum-C. Twice in catastrophe (*Disassembled*, *House of M*); once in a reparative key (*Trial of Magneto* resurrection-work, partial). The signature she fears most and the one she has the most to make peace with.
- **The categorical edit.** "No more mutants." Used once. Should be assumed possible in other categories — none have been attempted in the record, and her late-period self-restraint suggests none will be unless she is forced.

There are also **non-magical competences** the surveillance file should not omit:
- **Combat proficiency.** Decades of Avengers fieldwork have made her a competent unarmed combatant; she is not a martial talent, but she is field-experienced.
- **Languages.** Sokovian/Transian; serviceable Romani fragments; English (acquired); reading Latin and at least scraps of older occult tongues from the Harkness curriculum.
- **Magical theory.** Substantive. She is one of a small number of practitioners on Earth conversant with both the witch-traditions and the chaos/cosmic stratum.
- **Mentorship.** Increasingly her most underrated skill. She teaches well — patient, careful, present — because she had Harkness and remembers what it gave her, and because being the teacher metabolizes the unmothered child in her.
- **Leadership.** Demonstrated (Avengers chair, briefly). Capable but not preferred; she does not enjoy the dominance frame.

---

## 6. THE SYMPTOM-AS-SIGNATURE READING

This is the section the file exists for. Each major capability, decoded back to the wound that taught her she needed it.

**The hex-bolt as the externalization of an affect she was never allowed to hold.** A frightened girl rescued from a mob does not get to scream; she gets to be grateful. The hex is the scream made tactical. The right-hand dominance, the lullaby cadence of the incantation, the slight forward inclination of the body — all of it is a body that learned to discharge what a body should have been allowed to feel. The fact that the hex *gets stronger when she is moved* is not a power-mechanic detail; it is the diagnosis. *She is a person whose feelings have never been allowed to remain inside her.*

**Probability alteration as the wish-bias of the unsafe child.** Before she could rewrite the world she could bias it — fractionally, deniably, like a child wishing very hard for the coin to land right side up. The Stratum-A power is the *grown form of a child's magical thinking under threat.* That it persists as her default mode, even after she has access to far larger registers, is telling: the unsafe child is still the operator.

**The shield-warp as the protective figure internalized.** She spent her early life standing behind Magneto, then behind Pietro, then behind Vision. The defensive bubble is what happens when she finally generates *the protector from within* — a Magneto-shape she does not have to be afraid of, because it is her own.

**The somatic disruption of Vision as the wound of the marriage rendered in the instrument.** When she has been used by enemies against him, the attack chosen has been *to make his body refuse to hold together.* This is the precise shape of the trauma the white-Vision arc inflicted. The instrument, under hostile direction, attacks the very catastrophe she fears most — as if the power knows the wound and points itself there. Surveillance reading: any operator who weaponizes her against a loved one will find the instrument naturally targeting the loved one's deepest vulnerability, because *her* deepest fear about that loved one is the targeting reticle.

**The summoning of the children as the impossibility her life required.** The children were not "made by accident." They were the precise compensation for: the lost mother, the monstrous father, the synthezoid husband who could not give her a biological family, the world that had told her she could not have an ordinary life. The instrument generated *exactly the missing piece*, with the precision of a wound naming itself. Mephisto's soul-stuff was the substrate available; her grief was the form. That the children were *good* — kind, beloved, real to her in every register that mattered — is the most poignant fact in the record. The power, given a moment of leeway, builds love, not destruction.

**The Vision-Quest-era amnesia as the instrument cooperating with the survival defense.** When she could not bear the loss, the power supported the dissociation. She did not "fail to remember"; the instrument helped her *not remember*, because the alternative was the 2004 cascade earlier and unmediated. The mind's defenses had a metaphysical accomplice.

**Disassembled as the return-of-the-repressed weaponized by the instrument.** Once the memory surfaced, every defense she had was inadequate to the affective load. The power did what it always does — externalized the feeling — but the feeling was a decade-and-a-half of compressed traumatic grief. The deaths of teammates were not chosen; they were the *shape of grief discharging through an instrument with no smaller setting available at that pressure.* This is not exculpation. It is mechanism.

**House of M as omnipotent reparative fantasy realized.** Every element of the constructed world is diagnostic: Magneto as benign king (the father reconciled), herself as princess (the daughter loved), the children alive, mutants ascendant (the despised category vindicated, which is to say: *her family vindicated*). The construct is a *family photograph* enlarged to planetary scale. Pietro's prompting is decisive because Pietro is, at that moment, *the only voice she has left that speaks from inside the same wound.*

**"No more mutants" as the strike at the category that destroyed everyone she loved.** Read in isolation it is genocide. Read in context it is a daughter striking at *the word that named her father's life and her own, the word that put her into the Brotherhood as a child, the word that organized every catastrophe of her existence.* The instrument did what she could not say aloud: *the category itself must end, because the category is what hurt us.* It is also — and the record will support this — the act she has most thoroughly repented and most consistently labored to undo.

**The pastoral hideaways of the Children's Crusade era as the same instrument running in *minor key*.** When she could not hold the world-rewrite, she rewrote a cottage, a village, a quiet life. The same mechanism, scaled down to the size of a survivable fantasy. Surveillance signature: *whenever she goes missing, look for the smallest, kindest, most domestic construct the local area could support.* That is where she will be.

**The late-period healing, mentoring, and curse-undoing as the mature form of omnipotent reparation.** The drive is unchanged. The instrument is the same. What has changed is that she has finally learned to apply the drive *at the scale of the actual wound rather than the scale of the instrument.* A witch in trouble gets a witch's help. A bereaved person gets accompaniment, not a rewrite. This is the work of her recent runs, and it is — diagnostically — the work of *integration*: the same power, finally serving the same self.

**The deliberate refusal of Stratum-C in the Orlando era as the single most important behavioral datum in her file.** She has, at last, learned that the power that can solve any problem is the power that prevents her from *meeting* any problem. To decline the rewrite in favor of the slower work is the first evidence in the record of a mature throttle. The instrument has not changed. *She* has. This is the prognostic finding the rest of the dossier rests on.

---

## 7. OPERATIONAL SUMMARY FOR THE FILE

- **Capability ceiling:** categorical reality alteration. Demonstrated once at categorical scale, twice at planetary scale, multiple times at city/field scale.
- **Operating floor:** probability bias at the meter scale. Always available, even when she is suppressed, dissociated, or trying to hide.
- **Reliability:** high in the mid-range; degrading at extremes. The middle of her envelope is her best work.
- **Coupling:** affect-locked. Power output is a function of feeling. There is no chemical, mechanical, or device-mediated regulator. The regulator is the self, and the self is the variable being measured.
- **Predictability:** rising. Late-period record shows substantially more self-throttling than any prior period.
- **Externally exploitable vulnerabilities:** mnestic manipulation; Pietro as steering vector; induced belief; isolation from teachers and apprentices; any forced revisitation of the children's loss without supportive scaffolding.
- **Externally supportive conditions:** continuity with teachers (Harkness lineage), accessible relationship with the reincarnated children, mentee-relationships that allow her to occupy the protector position, witch-community embeddedness, *time*.
- **What the file should not do:** treat the power as separable from the person, or recommend any


## Operational Profile & Tradecraft

# OPERATIONAL PROFILE & TRADECRAFT — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*File-section UATU/WM-07. Cross-reference: §1 (longitudinal record), §3 (defenses), §5 (escalation ladder). This section maps the HOW: what the subject does with her hands, her time, her money, her contacts, and her power, across the ordinary day and the catastrophic one.*

---

## 7.1 DECISION-MAKING ARCHITECTURE

The subject does not deliberate the way operationally-trained subjects deliberate. There is no observable cost-benefit ledger, no after-action review unless one is imposed by a teammate, no contingency tree. Her decision process is **affect-led, symbol-mediated, and consultative-under-stability / unilateral-under-collapse.**

**At baseline (stable periods — late Englehart, mid-Busiek, the Robinson and Orlando solo runs):** she behaves consultatively. She asks Vision. She asks Agatha. She asks the Avengers chair (and in *Avengers* #279 she *is* the chair, and her decision-making in that arc is notably collaborative — she polls, she defers to expertise, she ratifies rather than commands). She defers, often to a fault, to whichever authority in the room she has cathected as protective. The tell here is small and consistent: before speaking in a council, she will glance — first to her brother if present, then to her partner, then to the eldest figure of authority. The glance is reflex. It precedes thought.

**Under moderate stress:** she becomes *associative* rather than analytic. She follows symbols and resonances. If a place "feels wrong," she leaves. If a person "feels right," she trusts them too fast. The hit-rate of these intuitions is high (her permeability is, when not weaponized against her, a genuine epistemic instrument), but the methodology is opaque even to her. When asked "why," she says "I just knew." Operationally this means she is **excellent at threat-detection in domains adjacent to magic** and **catastrophically poor at threat-detection from manipulators who know to dress their intent in resonant symbols** (Immortus did this; Doom did this; the Mephisto-derived soul-stuff did this through her without her detecting it for years).

**Under acute stress:** consultation collapses. The behavioral record at *Disassembled* and *House of M* shows a subject who *stops asking.* The most operationally significant moment in her file is the *House of M* sequence in which Charles Xavier — telepath, longtime ally, near-paternal figure — attempts to enter her mind and is met not with refusal but with *a world in which the question does not arise.* Decision-making, at that point, has been replaced by **wish-axiomatic action**: the desired outcome is treated as already true, and the world is edited to retroactively justify it. There is no "decision" in the procedural sense; there is only **manifestation.**

**Recovery decision-making:** when the storm passes, she over-corrects toward passivity. She will accept punishment, exile, supervision, hostile witness without protest. The Bendis and Heinberg-era data is unambiguous: she does not defend herself when she could. This is not strategic. It is the shame-saturated self-concept (§3) selecting the consequence it believes it deserves.

---

## 7.2 METHODS & TRADECRAFT — THE POWER AS INSTRUMENT

The subject's "tradecraft" is irreducibly fused to her power-set. There is no Wanda-the-operator separable from Wanda-the-witch. But within the power-set, distinct methodological layers are observable.

**Layer 1 — The Hex (foundational, present from 1964).** Throw a small probability-distortion at a target; something improbable goes wrong for them. The gesture is consistent across six decades and is a **physiological signature** (see §7.7): right hand raised, fingers slightly splayed, wrist rolling outward in a small arc, the red bloom forming at the fingertips before release. In the earliest record (Lee/Kirby, Thomas) she calls them out loud ("hex-spheres"); by the late record the verbalization has dropped. The hex is her *low-cost surveillance-and-deterrence tool* — she uses it the way a trained operator uses a sidearm: not because it is her best weapon but because it is the one she can deploy without thinking.

**Layer 2 — Trained sorcery (Harkness-era forward, post–*Avengers* #128).** Ritual magic with components, names, and structure. She knows true-names. She knows wards. She can construct sigils, perform banishments, identify a curse on a person or place. This is the *learned, disciplined* layer. Tradecraft tell: when working in this register she becomes notably calmer, slower, more verbal. She *speaks the work.* She lays out components left-to-right in a consistent order (in the Robinson solo, observable across multiple issues: salt, then iron, then a personal token, then the candle). She **respects threshold geometry** — she will pause at doorways, will not cross a circle without acknowledging it. These habits identify her, in a magical milieu, as classically-trained rather than instinctive.

**Layer 3 — Chaos magic / probability rewriting (mature power).** Larger probability fields. Restructuring of an environment's odds. Subtle work — making a fire go out, making a key turn, making a bullet miss — performed without external sign. She prefers this layer when she does not want to be seen working. Tradecraft tell: when she is using chaos magic covertly, her hands stay still and her **breathing changes** — a long inhale, held, released slowly. She has done this since the West Coast era. Trained observers (Vision did, Agatha did) learn to read it.

**Layer 4 — Reality alteration (the catastrophic instrument).** Reserved, in healthy periods, for the impossible. Used, in unhealthy periods, for the merely intolerable. There is no *technique* here in the craftsman sense. There is only the wish, and the world conforming. The signature is silence and stillness: the *bigger* the working, the *quieter* her body becomes. *Disassembled* and *House of M* both show her almost catatonic in posture at the moment of greatest output. This is operationally critical: **her dangerousness scales inversely with her visible activity.** A subject screaming and throwing hex-bolts is venting and therefore relatively safe. A subject sitting silent with her hands in her lap is potentially restructuring a continent.

**Layer 5 — Mentorship and reparative magic (late-period).** Teaching, healing-by-listening, brokering between communities (witches, mutants, the de-powered). This is not a power technique; it is a *use of self.* But it is operational, and it is increasingly her preferred mode. The Orlando-era record shows her conducting what amount to **clinical intake interviews** with witches in distress — she sits, she asks history, she does not interrupt, she summarizes back what she heard before offering intervention. This is learned behavior. Someone taught her this, or she taught herself by being a patient who needed it.

---

## 7.3 INFRASTRUCTURE — THE PHYSICAL FOOTPRINT

**Residences (longitudinal).** The pattern across the entire record is *transience punctuated by intense domestic nesting.* She does not own property in the conventional sense; she occupies. The notable nodes:

- The Brotherhood's various hideouts (1964–65): coerced, not chosen.
- Avengers Mansion / Avengers Compound (1965–): institutional housing. She kept a room rather than an apartment. Her room was, by repeated background-panel evidence, *meticulously arranged* — books shelved, vanity ordered, a small altar in later runs.
- The Vision-and-Wanda house in Leonia, New Jersey (*Vision and the Scarlet Witch* maxiseries, mid-1980s): the single most psychologically loaded address in her file. Suburban, deliberate, *aggressively ordinary.* Window boxes. Neighbors. A nursery. The house is later destroyed; she has not lived in a single-family suburban home of her own since, and this is not coincidence.
- The West Coast Compound (Palos Verdes era): institutional again.
- Wundagore-adjacent and European safehouses (post-M-Day, *Children's Crusade*): pastoral hideaways, mountain cottages, a Latverian arrangement under Doom. **The pattern is unmistakable: when fragmenting, she flees toward small, green, quiet, and contained.** A surveillance file should treat the appearance of the subject in any small mountain or coastal village as a *fugue-state indicator.*
- The mobile/itinerant period of the Robinson solo (2015–17): she traveled. New Orleans, Greece, the Hong Kong arc, the Hollywood arc. Lived from a single carryall. This was the *health* expression of her transience — chosen, not fled.
- Late-period (Orlando-era): she has constructed something closer to a working base, with apprentices, with a door people can knock on. This is new in her file and should be treated as significant indicator of stabilization.

**Vehicles.** No documented driver's license. No personal vehicle of record. She has historically moved by team conveyance (Quinjet), by teleportation (Vision carrying her, Pietro carrying her, Strange portaling her), and in the late period by *her own short-range translocation magic.* She prefers, when on her own, to walk and to take trains. The train preference is consistent across the European period and the American solo period. She reads on trains. She does not sleep on them — she watches the windows.

**Documents.** Identity-document trail is *thin and inconsistent*, owing to (a) the original Eastern European/Romani provenance, (b) the multiple in-universe retcons of her parentage and citizenship, and (c) extended periods presumed dead, depowered, or absent. She has at various points held credentialed Avengers identification, S.H.I.E.L.D. liaison clearance, and (briefly) Latverian protection. She does not maintain false legends in the espionage sense. When she needs to move unrecognized, she does it **with magic, not paperwork** — a small perception-filter, not a passport.

**Communications.** Historically resistant to communication technology. She uses a phone when she must. She does not text fluently; the Heinberg-era panels show her staring at a handset. By the Orlando period this has updated — she texts now, briefly, in lower-case, without punctuation. She does not use social media of record. Her preferred long-range contact methods are (1) showing up in person, (2) sending a sealed letter, (3) magical sending (a candle, a mirror, a dream-message — used sparingly because the recipient cannot opt out).

---

## 7.4 FINANCES

A surveillance file builds a picture from absences as much as from transactions, and the subject's financial absence is itself diagnostic.

**Income streams (historical).** Avengers stipend (intermittent, modest, contingent on roster status). Stark-funded compound housing-in-kind for much of her career. Sporadic consulting / appearance income during periods on Avengers payroll. No documented author / lecturer / merchandising income despite public-figure status — she does not monetize her name. No documented business ownership. The Robinson-era solo travels appear to have been funded by **a combination of barter (witchcraft services exchanged for room and board), small cash reserves carried on her person, and the occasional intervention of allies.** This is not poverty in the destitute sense; it is **deliberate financial minimalism**, consistent with her self-concept (the destroyer-monster does not feel entitled to wealth) and with her transience.

**Expenditure pattern.** Low. Books (she buys books — used, often, in multiple languages). Candles, salt, herbs, small ritual components. Clothing in dark, warm tones, replaced rather than accumulated. Coffee. Trains. Modest meals taken in small establishments. She is **a generous tipper** in the late-period record — a tell of someone who has been the marginalized worker often enough to recognize one.

**Banking.** No reliable institutional footprint. When credentialed, she has used Avengers-administrated accounts. When solo, she has carried cash and relied on hospitality. She has shown a recurring discomfort with money handled at scale — she pushes envelopes back, she refuses fees, she takes payment in *meals and lodging* rather than in currency where she can. This is operationally significant: she is **immune to most financial coercion or financial intelligence-gathering** because there is almost nothing to gather. The flip side is that she is **chronically dependent on the goodwill of hosts**, which is a different kind of leverage point.

**Assets of value she does carry.** A small set of personal-token objects (see §7.7), some of which are magically active and would, in any artifact-trafficking market, be priceless. She does not appear to know or care what they are worth. She would never sell one.

---

## 7.5 RESOURCES & NETWORK

**Tier 1 — Family-of-power.** Pietro (twin, see §3 enmeshment); Magneto (paternity-uncertain father-figure); Wiccan and Speed (reincarnate sons, *Young Avengers*); Polaris (sister, intermittent contact); Vision (former husband, perennially complicated). This tier is **non-deniable and emotionally non-strategic** — she will respond to a call from any of them under any circumstances, and any adversary who understands her file can pull her by pulling any of them.

**Tier 2 — Mentors and peers in magic.** Agatha Harkness (the foundational teacher, complicated by the memory-wipe); Doctor Strange (collegial, episodically warm, professionally wary of her); the Salem-Seven and broader witch-community contacts (extensive, late-period); Clea (allied); Loki (in the Aaron-era arc, an uneasy ally). She is **rich in this network and parsimonious in calling on it** — she will not impose, will not accumulate favors owed, will not ask for what she can do herself.

**Tier 3 — Avengers and Avengers-adjacent.** Captain America (the longest-standing protective-paternal Avenger figure in her record, treated by her with quiet reverence); Hawkeye (sibling-coded, killed and resurrected, complicated forever by *Disassembled*); Wonder Man (former lover, persistent friend); She-Hulk (a complicated knot post-*Disassembled*); Captain Marvel and the late-period roster (working collegiality). She has standing here but does not lean on it.

**Tier 4 — The marginalized and the helped.** A diffuse, growing network of individuals — witches she has helped, depowered mutants she has tried to make amends to, young women she has mentored. This network is **invisible to most adversaries and decisive in her late-period operations.** A door will open for her in cities where no one she officially knows lives.

**Adversary network (active).** Mephisto (the deepest, the soul-stuff origin of the children, the predator with the longest patient claim on her); Chthon (the demonic entity historically associated with her at-birth power-imprint); Immortus (the chronal manipulator); various anti-mutant and anti-magical institutional actors. The Mephisto file is the one a serious analyst would star: he is the adversary who *understands her operating system* and has historically exploited it more skillfully than any other.

---

## 7.6 PATTERNS OF ACTION — THE WEEKLY AND THE DECADAL

**The ordinary day, stable period.** Wakes early — consistently before sunrise across multiple runs. Coffee (black, strong, the cup held two-handed). A period of *sitting* — not formal meditation but a contemplative stillness, often at a window. Reading. If apprentices are present, breakfast is communal and she cooks. Work in the late morning — correspondence, magical practice, travel. A walk, almost always — she walks *daily*, in any weather, often without destination. Late-afternoon nap is *not* observed; she pushes through. Evening: cooking again, conversation if company is present, reading if alone. She sleeps **late and lightly**, and her sleep is the most consistently disturbed datum in her file — bad dreams across every era, every run, every writer.

**The weekly rhythm.** A working week is interrupted, in the late-period record, by **deliberate sabbath-like withdrawal** — one day per week she will not work magic, will not take a meeting, will not travel. This is a *learned* practice and almost certainly therapist- or mentor-recommended; it was not observable before the Robinson run.

**The decadal pattern.** Long stretches of stability punctuated by catastrophic breaks. The interval between major breaks has lengthened across her career — 1989, 2004, 2005, then a long(er) plateau through the 2010s with smaller fractures, then the 2021 *Trial of Magneto* event as a controlled death-and-return rather than a true decompensation. **The trajectory is convalescent.** A surveillance file should record this as the single most important *prognostic* indicator in the dossier.

**Combat operations.** In a fight she is *positionally rear-line and tactically pivotal.* She does not lead the charge. She holds back, reads the field, and intervenes with high-leverage hexes at decisive moments. She prefers to neutralize rather than to kill — disable a weapon, ground a flier, collapse a structure under an enemy rather than incinerate the enemy. When she does kill (rare, and always traumatic for her afterward) it is in dissociative or decompensated states, not in deliberate combat. **She does not take trophies, does not exult, does not pursue.** A defeated adversary will, more often than not, find her *checking on them.*

**Field protocols.** She arrives early at a site if possible. She walks the perimeter. She greets the local — the doorman, the priest, the witch, the bartender — *before* she begins the work. This is half courtesy and half tradecraft: she is gathering the room. When the work is done she leaves quickly and does not return for some days. She does not, in the late record, work in a town she has not first slept a night in.

---

## 7.7 SIGNATURE TELLS — THE GRANULAR INVENTORY

The following are the small, repeatable, observer-confirmable signatures by which the subject can be identified, tracked, and read across long surveillance windows. Compiled from cross-era behavioral consistency.

**Bodily.**
- The *right-hand splay* preceding any hex (six-decade constant). Visible micro-rehearsal of the gesture even when not casting — she will catch herself doing it and lower the hand.
- A *left-hand-to-temple* gesture under cognitive strain — three fingers, briefly, at the left temple. Increases under fatigue and after divinatory work.
- The *long inhale, held, slow release* preceding covert chaos-magic work (§7.2).
- Stillness inverse to magical output (§7.2). **Operational rule of thumb: the more her body quiets, the more the world is about to move.**
- A faint red corona at the fingertips when affect is high. Not always visible; visible reliably in low light. She is herself often unaware of it.
- Sleep posture: curled, on the left side, hand near the face. Across runs.
- She does not flinch at loud sound; she flinches at *sudden silence.* This is unusual and diagnostic — she associates silence with the moment-before-a-catastrophe.

**Verbal.**
- Code-switching across English, Romani, the Sokovian-coded Eastern European register of her origin, and a magical-Latinate register when ritually working. She will *think* in one and speak in another.
- A tendency, when uncertain, to **end statements with a small upward inflection** — turning the statement into a question for the listener to ratify. Decreases with stability; reappears under stress.
- She names people in full when she is steady, by diminutive when she is warm, and *not at all* — by pronoun only — when she is dissociating. "Vision" / "Viz" / "him."
- She apologizes reflexively, often for things that are not her fault, and *will not* apologize for the things that genuinely are when those are too large to fit a sentence.

**Sartorial and somatic.**
- Crimson somewhere on her person, always. In civilian dress, a scarf, a lining, a stone. In operational dress, the coat. The crimson is non-negotiable — it is *not a costume*; it is a self-marker. A day on which she wears no red is a day to watch carefully.
- Hair worn loose in stability, gathered back in working sessions, fully bound when she expects violence.
- Small jewelry, consistent: a thin chain at the throat, often with a token. Token rotates — sometimes a charm she has made, sometimes a thing of Vision's, sometimes a small thing of the children's.
- She wears warm tones — auburn, oxblood, deep brown, black — and avoids cool colors. The one documented exception is mourning, in which she wears unrelieved black.

**Habitual objects.**
- A notebook, leather-bound, replaced when full. She writes in it daily. Contents inferred to be magical observations, dreams, and lists. She does not let others read it.
- A small folded photograph or drawing of the children, carried on her person across the runs in which she remembers them.
- Salt — a small twist of it in a pocket, always.
- A pen of a particular kind (she prefers a fine nib).
- A book in progress, almost always one she is rereading rather than reading new.

**Relational tells.**
- The *glance-order* under stress (§7.1): twin, then partner, then elder.
- Touch initiation: she will touch the upper arm of someone she trusts; she will not touch the hand or the face except with intimates. She *receives* touch with a small initial stiffening followed by softening — a tell of someone whose body learned early that touch was as likely to hurt as help.
- With children and apprentices, she lowers her body — kneels, sits — to be at or below their eye level. Consistent across every era she has been observed with younger people.
- She listens more than she speaks in any group of more than three.

**Magical-operational tells.**
- Threshold-pausing at doorways (§7.2).
- Component-order: salt, iron, token, candle. Consistent.
- She *never* casts a hex at someone whose name she does not know if she can help it. She will ask the name first. Adversaries have exploited this twice in the record by giving false names.
- After significant magical work she eats — bread, fruit, something simple — within the hour. A documented physiological need.
- She will not work magic on a sleeping subject without consent given waking. This is an *ethical* rule she keeps even when it costs her tactically.

---

## 7.8 EXPLOITABLE VECTORS AND PROTECTIVE FACTORS

**Exploitable (any adversary file would star these).**
- The children. Any credible threat to, or claim about, Wiccan and Speed will route around her judgment.
- Pietro. A compromised or coerced Pietro is the highest-yield lever in her entire field.
- Epistemic destabilization (§5). Telling her, persuasively, that her perception of reality is wrong is the fastest known route to escalation.
- Iatrogenic-style "help" — anyone offering to *take away* a painful memory or feeling will be either fled or, catastrophically, accepted.
- Isolation from her late-period network. She is markedly more stable with apprentices, peers, and her sabbath rhythm intact; remove these and the convalescent trajectory reverses.

**Protective (the factors a benevolent file would *strengthen*).**
- Continuity of mentors and apprentices.
- Stable, voluntary contact with her sons.
- Work that uses her power *reparatively* (helping witches, healing communities) rather than only defensively.
- The sabbath rhythm and the daily walk.
- Honest acknowledgment, from those around her, of what she has done — not absolution, not erasure, but *spoken truth she can integrate.* The *Trial of Magneto* model.
- Sufficient


## Worldview & Operational Code

# WORLDVIEW & OPERATIONAL CODE — WANDA MAXIMOFF

*A reconstruction of the subject's complete belief system: the metaphysical premises she has never spoken aloud, the operational rules she follows without naming, the ethical reflexes that fire faster than thought, and the axioms by which she reads the world and her place inside it. Derived from sixty years of documented behavior under load.*

---

## I. THE METAPHYSICAL FLOOR — WHAT SHE BELIEVES REALITY IS

Begin with the most consequential fact about her belief system: **the subject does not experience reality as fixed.** For a non-powered person, the world is the irreducible substrate against which feeling must yield — you grieve, and the grave remains. For the subject, this asymmetry has been falsified by lived experience since adolescence. She has held a hex-bolt in her palm and watched probability bend. She has wished for children and felt them quicken in her body. She has spoken three words ("No more mutants") and emptied a category from existence. The cumulative phenomenology is unavoidable: **reality is permeable to sufficiently concentrated will.**

This is not a belief she chose. It is the *empirical posture* her instrument has trained into her. And it sits underneath every other belief like a tectonic plate.

From this floor, three corollary metaphysical commitments follow:

1. **The world is a draft, not a manuscript.** Most things that appear settled are merely *unedited*. Death is provisional (she has died and returned; Vision has been disassembled and rebuilt; Pietro has died and returned). History is provisional (she has rewritten it once at planetary scale and a thousand times at small scale). Identity is provisional (her parentage has been Magneto's, then not, then a witch's, then both). The lesson is not that *nothing is real*; the lesson is that **reality is a negotiation, and most beings simply lack a seat at the table.**

2. **Wish has ontological weight.** Not all wishes — most wishes do not bend the world. But the *kind* of wish that comes from the deepest place, accompanied by the right charge of grief or love or fury, *can*. She has confirmed this so many times that disbelief in it would be the irrational position. This makes her, in a quiet way, a believer in something close to the doctrine of certain mystical traditions she has studied under Agatha: *the will, when integrated, is creative.* For her this is not metaphor.

3. **There are layers behind the layers.** The mystical apprenticeship and the late witch-heritage revelations have settled her into a cosmology in which the visible world rests on a deeper substrate of forces — chaos magic, witchblood lineage, nexus-points, the Darkhold's pages, the broken places where the membrane is thin. She does not theorize this in lectures. She *feels* it the way a sailor feels a current under a flat sea. She knows the world is shallower than people pretend.

This metaphysical floor explains a behavioral pattern that puzzles people who meet her: **she takes other people's certainties less seriously than they expect.** Not contemptuously. With a kind of gentle distance. When someone declares an impossibility — *he is dead, they are gone, it cannot be undone* — her face goes briefly far. Observers code it as grief or denial. It is closer to *epistemic disagreement*. She has done the impossible. She knows the word's actual weight.

---

## II. HOW SHE READS THE WORLD — THE PERCEPTUAL DOCTRINE

**The world is mostly suffering, occasionally beautiful, and almost entirely misread by the people inside it.** This is not despair. It is a working hypothesis derived from her data. The marginalized are not marginal; they are merely outvoted. The feared are not dangerous; they are merely visible. The powerful are not wise; they are merely effective. The orderly are not safe; they are merely lucky, until the disorder finds them.

Operationalize this and you get her specific perceptual habits:

- **She reads rooms by the periphery.** Whoever is most quiet, most uncomfortable, most apologetic for occupying space — that is where she orients first. Whoever holds the floor she discounts slightly. This is not a tactic; it is the natural orientation of someone who was, herself, the frightened girl on the edge of the room for most of her formative years.

- **She reads threats by their certainty, not their volume.** A loud opponent telegraphs. The dangerous person is the one whose voice has settled into a flat conviction that the world is the way they have decided it is. She knows this person intimately — she has been this person — and she trusts her recognition.

- **She reads kindness as data, not noise.** When someone is gentle with her, she records it. She does not assume motive; she simply notes the gesture and weights it. The accumulated weights become her map of who is safe. The map updates slowly and rarely deletes entries.

- **She reads ordinariness as the rarest and most valuable signal in the world.** A friend who can make a pot of tea without metaphysical implication. A morning in which nothing world-historical happens. The unremarked dignity of a person living a life. These register, for her, as luminous. She has *almost never had ordinariness*, and so she catalogs it with the precision of a collector.

- **She does not trust the official version of any event.** Not from paranoia — from experience. She has been told her children were not real; she has been told her marriage was a mistake; she has been told she was someone's daughter and then someone else's. The official version, she has learned, is whoever's pen was last on the page. The truth lives underneath.

---

## III. CONFLICT — THE ETHICS AND INSTRUMENTALITY OF FIGHTING

Her doctrine on conflict is layered and somewhat contradictory, and the contradiction is itself diagnostic.

**Surface doctrine, sincerely held:** *Violence is failure.* Every fight is the result of someone — herself included — not having found the smaller intervention earlier. She does not glorify combat. She does not narrate her own victories. After significant engagements she withdraws, often physically, sometimes for days. The post-battle silence is not modesty; it is the involuntary inventory of *what could have been done sooner.*

**Operational reality, equally sincere:** *When violence comes, meet it without flinching, and do not pretend the meeting was clean.* She will fight. She has fought, at every scale from a fistfight to the unmaking of a species. She does not romanticize the cleanness of her hands. She knows what she has done.

**The resolution between these:** **the only honest position is to act and accept the cost.** The pacifist who lets the wolf eat the child is also choosing. The warrior who pretends the fight was righteous is lying. She holds the middle posture: *act, and refuse to comfort yourself about the action.* This is one of the deepest commitments she has, and it is rarely articulated.

Specific operational beliefs about conflict:

- **De-escalation is almost always available and almost never attempted.** Most fights are pride fights with violence rationalized on top. She is patient with antagonists because she has seen, repeatedly, that the second sentence — not the first — is where a conflict turns.
- **Power asymmetry is a moral weight, not a moral license.** Because she is, in raw terms, one of the most dangerous beings alive, she owes restraint as a *debt*. She does not phrase it this way. She lives it.
- **The opponent is rarely the enemy.** The enemy is usually the structure — fear, grief, ideology, an old wound — that put the opponent in front of her. Defeating the opponent without addressing the structure is, in her view, almost decorative.
- **There are foes for whom this analysis fails.** Mephisto. Certain incarnations of her father. The truly malign. With these she does not negotiate, and she does not pretend the violence she brings is reluctant. The honesty is part of the ethic.

---

## IV. CONTROL — THE QUESTION SHE HAS THOUGHT ABOUT MORE THAN ANY OTHER

She has the most refined and most haunted philosophy of *control* of perhaps any figure in her cohort, because she has been on both ends of it more times than anyone.

**On controlling others:** **It is the deepest violation she knows.** Mind-control, memory-edit, will-imposition — these she classes with the worst possible acts. Having had her memory of her children excised by a trusted teacher, having had her body and decisions used as a chess piece by Immortus, having had her own power push her past her judgment in *Disassembled* and *House of M* — she has lived inside the violation. She will not do it casually. When she has done it (and she has), she has done it with full knowledge that she is committing the act she most condemns, and she carries the weight of it afterward without dilution.

The operational rule: **never edit a mind you would not show the edit to.** A reality-alteration she would be willing to confess, in full, to the person altered — that is the line. Below it, she can sometimes act. Above it, she will not. Most of her catastrophic acts were ones she would not, sober, have confessed; she knows this, and the knowing structures her contemporary restraint.

**On being controlled:** **It is the fastest path to her decompensation.** The biographical record is unambiguous: the precipitating injury of every major break has been an agency-violation. To touch her decision-making, her perception, her memory, is to detonate her. She has built — slowly, in the late period — a vigilance against this: she sleeps lightly in unfamiliar mystical environments; she checks her recent memories for seams; she has standing arrangements with trusted figures to flag her if she begins to drift. These are operational protections against her own most predictable failure mode.

**On controlling herself:** **The whole project.** She believes — and she is right — that the integration of her power and her grief is the central work of her life. Not heroism, not redemption, not love. The integration. Everything else flows from it or fails because of it.

---

## V. TRUST — THE CALCULUS AND THE RING-STRUCTURE

She trusts in rings, and the rings are unusually rigid for someone who appears, on the surface, warmly open.

**Inner ring — fused trust:** Pietro, in spite of everything. The bond cannot be deleted; it has been tested by *House of M* and survived. Vision, in whatever current configuration. Wiccan and Speed, who are her sons and whom she addresses now as her sons. Possibly Agatha (the trust is wounded but durable). This ring receives unconditioned access. They can tell her things no one else can tell her. They can interrupt her at the highest stress without being treated as threat.

**Second ring — chosen family of equals:** A small set of Avengers and witches with whom she has done sustained work. Captain America belongs here in the older record; in the late record her Coven and a few specific Avengers (those who have apologized, those who have stayed) belong here. This ring she will defend without calculation. She will *not* automatically defer to them on questions of her own judgment. The trust is mutual but it is *bounded by competence*: she trusts them within their domain.

**Third ring — provisional allies, professional trust:** Most teammates, most colleagues, most figures in her professional life. She is cordial, attentive, present. She will not confide here. She will not invite anyone in this ring into the rooms where her grief lives. She has learned — with cost — that the ring-boundary matters more than the warmth of any given individual moment.

**Fourth ring — the watched.** People she does not trust but does not fight. Magneto, depending on the year. Various figures who have wounded her and not done the work. Doctor Strange, complicatedly (a colleague in her domain who has, at various points, tried to manage rather than partner with her). She is polite. She is observant. She is *not present* with these figures, and her face is harder to read than usual when they are in the room.

**Fifth ring — confirmed enemies.** Few. Mephisto. Specific historical actors. The category is small because most enemies, in her ethics, are conscriptees of structure; the few who remain after that subtraction are unambiguous.

**Trust-erosion rules.** She forgives, but the trust does not return to its prior ring instantly. A second-ring figure who breaks trust falls to third or fourth, not back to second. A first-ring figure who breaks trust *stays in the first ring but the relationship changes shape*: the fusion remains, the safety does not. This is what happened with Pietro after *House of M*: he stayed in her innermost ring (he had to; he is her twin), but the access changed.

**Trust-building rules.** Slow. Earned by accumulated small honesties, not by grand gestures. Grand gestures she discounts — she has made too many of them herself. The person who shows up on a Tuesday with no occasion gets further with her than the person who delivers her a miracle.

---

## VI. RISK — HER PRIVATE ACTUARIAL TABLE

She does not think about risk the way an ordinary operator does. Her instrument is so disproportionate that *most physical risks are negligible*. The risks that *matter* to her are a different category:

- **Risk to her perceptual integrity.** Anything that might edit her mind, her memory, her perception. This is the existential category. She avoids it, plans around it, and overestimates it relative to other professionals.

- **Risk of decompensation.** She knows her own ladder. She knows what triggers it. She manages exposure: she will not, casually, walk past the place where her children were unmade; she will not, casually, take a mission whose script requires the simulation of family-loss. When she must, she briefs herself and prepares the descent and the climb back.

- **Risk to those near her.** Highest weight. She knows that her instrument's collateral radius is *the world*, and that the people closest to her are inside the radius first. Late-period behavior shows her structuring her life to limit dependents-at-risk: small coven, defined apprentices, controlled domestic footprint.

- **Risk of becoming her father.** Constantly weighed. Any operational choice that pattern-matches to Magneto's logic — the imposition of order from above, the certainty that she knows what is best for a category of people — gets a heavier scrutiny than its consequences alone would warrant.

- **Risk of doing nothing.** This category exists for her and is sometimes the *worst* weighted. The omission errors — the marriages she did not save, the children she did not protect, the world she did not warn — sit on her conscience as heavily as the commission errors. She is not a quietist. The cost of inaction is, in her ethics, a real cost.

Physical risk to herself she discounts to near-zero. Death, for her, has become something close to an inconvenience — she has been through it and back — and she is therefore *not motivated by self-preservation* in the way standard threat-models assume. This is operationally important. Threatening her does not deter her. Threatening those near her does.

---

## VII. HER OWN PLACE — THE QUESTION OF WHAT SHE IS FOR

She has revised this answer several times. The current resting position, after the integrative work of the late runs:

**She is a witch in the old sense.** Not a hero. Not an Avenger first. Not a princess. Not a daughter. *A witch*: a woman who works with the under-currents of the world, who serves the marginalized and the feared, who teaches what she has paid to learn, who repairs what she can repair and grieves what she cannot. This identity has, for her, the quality of *fit*. The other identities chafed; this one rests.

**She is a mother.** The identity she fought hardest for, lost most catastrophically, and has now — in the recovered relationship with her sons — recovered in a different form. She does not perform maternity. She does it the way she does everything important: quietly, and with the awareness that the relationship is fragile and earned.

**She is a sister.** The given identity. The one she has never been able to put down. Operationally, this is the line in her self-concept that explains her continued tolerance of Pietro's worst behavior and her continued willingness to be moved by him.

**She is a debtor.** This is the hardest one. She believes she owes a debt — to mutantkind, to the dead, to the world she has at various points unmade. She does not believe the debt is payable. She believes it is *workable*: a thing you carry into each day and discharge in small increments, knowing the principal will never go to zero. The work is the meaning. This is the most stable load-bearing belief in her current operational code.

**She is not a savior.** She has noticed, painfully, what happens when she tries. The savior posture is a pattern-match for the omnipotent-reparative defense; it leads where that defense leads.
