**EXPECT (HIGH):** the conversation ends. The denier may end with it. The chaos-aura will not flare visibly; that is a Rung 3 sign. At Rung 4 the power *concentrates inward* — she will look very calm — and the denier will find themselves elsewhere, or *believing* something they did not believe, or quietly unable to speak her sons' names for an indefinite period. She will not remember choosing the specific outcome. *Confidence on lethality:* LOW in the late period; she has spent fifteen comics-years training herself not to discharge here. *Confidence on some form of magical retaliation:* HIGH.

**GIVEN** Pietro is killed, or appears to be, in her presence
**EXPECT (HIGH):** Rung 4 to Rung 5 transition risk is highest in this scenario. The twin-cord severed under witness, with no buffer, is the closest analog the file has to the 2004 collapse. *Expect immediate denial* — she will attempt to verify; she will reach for her own pulse to compare; she will demand the body be untouched. *Expect a window of bargaining* in which she searches, internally, for a workable rewrite ("he is unconscious," "this is an illusion," "this can be undone"). *Intervention window:* the bargaining phase is where she is most reachable. Allies who can offer *real* hope of resurrection (Avengers history is generous here, and she knows it) can convert the rewrite-impulse into a *quest*, which is metabolizable. Allies who confirm finality too bluntly, too soon, lose her to Rung 5.

**GIVEN** she is presented with the *opportunity* to undo a discrete past harm — a single death, a single injury, a single wrong — by a tempter offering plausible mechanism
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the longest pause in her behavioral repertoire. She will not answer in the moment; she will request time. During the time she will visit the relevant grave, location, or person and *sit*, sometimes for hours. The file should expect refusal *more often than not* — the late-period record shows she has learned that the price of the rewrite is always larger than the wound it patches. But the file should also record that the temptation is real and that the percentage of refusal is *not* one hundred. The variables: *whose* harm is offered, *who* the tempter is (a stranger she can dismiss; Pietro or Wiccan she cannot), and *whether she has slept.* Sleep is the single most important moderating variable in her psychiatric record.

**GIVEN** an enemy attempts to use her sons against her — as bait, as hostages, as illusions
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the file's lowest forecasted restraint. This is the scenario in which the *integration project of the last decade* is most likely to fail. Expect rapid Rung 4-to-5 transit. Expect the enemy to be neutralized in a manner she would not have chosen in calmer mind. Expect, afterward, weeks of withdrawal and self-prosecution. *Protective factor:* if Wiccan or Speed are personally present and *competent*, the wound is partly buffered by the present-tense reality of their adulthood. If they are absent, the buffer is absent.

---

## 7-B.5 — RUNG 5 BEHAVIORS (CATASTROPHIC; WISH-BECOMES-WORLD)

> *Threshold: multiple primary wounds engaged simultaneously; no available containing relationship; sleep deficit catastrophic; an external prompt (Pietro's voice in the M-template, Mephisto-class adversary, Doom-class manipulator) suggests the rewrite. Reality testing has lost coherence; the instrument and the affect are no longer distinguishable.*

**GIVEN** the full conjunction — children re-lost or re-denied, Vision re-destroyed, Pietro pushing her toward a "solution," her own discipline eroded by an enemy or by sleep loss, *and* no Wiccan / no Agatha-figure / no apprentice present to anchor her
**EXPECT (MED, conditional on conjunction):** a rewrite. The shape varies by which wound is loudest. *Children-loudest:* a domestic world in which they live, ordinary, scaled small (a town, a household) — this is the *Children's Crusade* template. *Vision-loudest:* an Avengers-Mansion-shaped construct in which the marriage continues — small, intimate, claustrophobic. *Father-loudest:* a world in which mutants are sovereign and she is the king's daughter — the *House of M* template. *Self-loudest (the "I am a monster" axis):* the most dangerous shape, in which she rewrites *herself* — undoing her power, undoing her existence, the "No More Wandas" failure-mode. This last is the form the late-period record has most plausibly moved her toward, and it is the one allies should monitor for, because it does not present as aggression. It presents as *farewell.*

**GIVEN** the rewrite has occurred and reality is being held in the altered state
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the construct will be internally *kind*. Even at her worst she has not built worlds of cruelty; the constructs are reparative, not punitive. Inhabitants will be living lives slightly better than their canonical lives. This is diagnostically important: a sadistic construct would falsify the file's reading and indicate possession or substitution. A kind construct, even at planetary scale, is consistent with W-1/W-4-driven decompensation.

**EXPECT (HIGH):** the construct will contain a *small, hidden, somatic tell* — usually a recurring symbol (a stork, a hex-shape, a date on a calendar that does not advance) that a perceptive observer can find. This is her own unconscious leaving a door open. The late-period Wanda is, at some level, *trying to be caught.*

**EXPECT (HIGH):** she will resist exposure of the construct with overwhelming force, *but* the resistance will collapse at a single point: the voice of someone she loved before the wound. Wiccan saying *Mom*. Pietro saying her name without an instruction attached. Vision — even a Vision — saying any sentence in his original cadence. The construct is not breakable by force; it is breakable by *recognition.*

---

## 7-B.6 — BETRAYAL: SPECIFIC FORECASTS

The category deserves its own subsection because her response varies sharply by *who* and *what.*

**GIVEN** betrayal by a *protector-figure* (Magneto-class, Cap-class, Strange-class — anyone in the parent-or-mentor frame)
**EXPECT (HIGH):** initial freeze, then a quiet, devastating articulacy. She does not yell at parents; she *names* what they did, exactly, in sentences they will hear at night for years. The protector-betrayal returns her to the orphan-girl posture *only* for an instant — then triggers the W-3 fear (*if you are this, am I this?*) and an over-correction into autonomy. After betrayal by a protector she becomes *less* deferential to authority for an extended period, sometimes years.

**GIVEN** betrayal by an *equal* — an Avenger of her own rank, a peer witch
**EXPECT (MED-HIGH):** a more ordinary anger, the most "human" affect in her repertoire. She will confront, she will permit reconciliation if the betrayer comes to her honestly, and she will not (usually) reach for the power. This is the band in which she functions most like an unpowered person. *Failure mode:* if the betrayal touches W-1 or W-4 specifically, expect escalation to Rung 3 minimum.

**GIVEN** betrayal by *Pietro*
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the most painful, slowest-resolving betrayal in her file. She will not retaliate. She will withdraw from him completely, sometimes for years (the post-*House of M* estrangement is the type-specimen). She will *not* speak ill of him to others; she will simply be unable to be in rooms with him. Reconciliation requires *his* labor, fully and visibly, and it can be done — the late-period Pietro/Wanda reconciliations are real. The wound, however, is the kind that scars white and stays visible.

**GIVEN** betrayal by an *apprentice* or someone she has chosen to mentor
**EXPECT (MED):** the most *self-blaming* response. She will absorb the betrayal as her failure of teaching. This is W-3 inverted (*if I made this, I am this*). Expect a withdrawal from teaching for a period; expect, eventually, a return to it, because mentoring is too core to her late-period reparative project to abandon.

**GIVEN** *systemic* betrayal — by a body or institution
**EXPECT (HIGH):** controlled response, addressed in the W-6 register described above. The danger here is not immediate; it is *cumulative.* Each systemic betrayal narrows the set of institutions she will work within. The late-period trajectory is already toward *solo* work for this reason. The file should anticipate that, given enough systemic betrayals, she will become functionally unaffiliated — which is a *higher-risk* state, because the affiliations are part of her containment.

---

## 7-B.7 — TEMPTATION: SPECIFIC FORECASTS

**GIVEN** an offer of *power* — augmentation, a new font of magic, a cosmic upgrade
**EXPECT (HIGH):** refusal, often impatient. She has *enough* instrument; she has too much. Tempters who lead with power misread her completely, and she registers the misread as a small insult. *Sub-prediction:* she will gently warn the tempter against offering the same to others.

**GIVEN** an offer of *forgetting* — to be relieved of the memory of the children, of Vision, of what she has done
**EXPECT (HIGH, late period):** refusal, and a sharper one than the power refusal. The Harkness wound has trained her exactly the opposite way the wound was intended. She will not surrender her memory again, even of what hurts. *In the earlier eras of the file (pre-2010) the prediction inverts:* she would have taken the offer, which is part of why she was vulnerable.

**GIVEN** an offer of *a small, achievable, ordinary life* — a cottage, a partner, a quiet decade
**EXPECT (MED):** the longest hesitation. This is W-4 in its tempting form. She wants it. She will not take it under most conditions, because she has learned to mistrust the construct-shape of her own longings — but the *wanting* is real and visible, and a skilled observer will see her composure briefly fail. *The exception:* if the offer is honest, unmagical, and from a person she trusts, she may take it for a season. The late record has precedents.

**GIVEN** an offer to *undo House of M* — to restore the depowered mutants in a single act
**EXPECT (HIGH):** intense engagement, careful study, and — if the mechanism is real — acceptance, with conditions. The W-3 debt is among her most consciously-carried weights. She will not, however, accept a mech


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM
## Subject: Wanda Maximoff ("Scarlet Witch")
### Orientation: defensive — for those who would protect her, those who would stand near her without harming her, and those who would have to talk her down from the edge of a world.

---

## PREAMBLE — WHY THIS DOCUMENT EXISTS AND HOW IT IS TO BE USED

A vulnerabilities map for an ordinary subject is a list of buttons that can be pressed. A vulnerabilities map for this subject is something else: a list of places where the seam between her interior weather and the *fabric of the consensual world* is thinnest. Pressing a button on Wanda Maximoff does not produce an emotional response in isolation; it produces a probability-shift, a hex-discharge, a fugue, or — at the worst end — a rewritten cosmos. There is no daylight between provoking her and provoking *reality.*

The compendium is therefore organized not by what can be exploited but by what must be *handled.* Anyone in her orbit — Avengers liaison, X-Men diplomat, witch-community contact, son, brother, lover, apprentice, the rare therapist who could ever be cleared — needs to know not only the levers but the *direction* they move her, the *latency* before the move shows, and the *recovery curve* afterward. Several entries below are flagged HOSTILE-USE-NEGATIVE — meaning, an adversary attempting to weaponize them is statistically likely to trigger a catastrophe that consumes the adversary along with the surroundings. The protective frame holds even there: knowing what would set her off is, for those who love her, the same knowledge as keeping her safe.

---

## I. THE PRIMARY PRESSURE POINTS — RANK-ORDERED BY DETONATION YIELD

### 1. The Children. (Thomas and William / Wiccan and Speed.)

The single deepest wound and the single deepest source of stability, depending entirely on the *framing* of the approach.

- **Cold mention** ("your sons," "the boys") from a stranger or an adversary: instant somatic response — pupil dilation, a quarter-second held breath, a faint reddening at the fingertips before she is even aware she is glowing. If the speaker is hostile, she will read the mention as a *taunt about the loss* and the hex-signature will spike within two to three seconds.
- **Warm mention** from a trusted figure (Vision, Pietro in his late-period mode, Agatha in the rare reconciled register, Billy himself, Tommy himself, Clint after their long arc of repaired trust) lowers her baseline. She breathes out. She sits down if she has been standing. The children's *named existence in a trusted mouth* is, paradoxically, one of the few sedatives that work on her.
- **Denial of their reality** (any phrasing that returns her to the 1989 Harkness frame — "they weren't real," "they were never your children," "you only thought you had them") is the single fastest path to catastrophic escalation in the entire file. It collapses her grief, her perception, and her self-trust simultaneously. Do not say this. Do not let an opponent say this. If an opponent has said it, get her to Billy or Tommy within the hour.
- **Threat to them, present-tense** (Wiccan or Speed in danger): she will burn the relevant region to bedrock. There is no negotiation lever above this one. Anyone who has taken either boy hostage has, historically, not survived the rescue.
- **Useful protective tactic.** If she is sliding into a fugue or a rewrite, *naming the boys, in the present tense, as currently alive and currently safe*, in a voice she trusts, is the most reliable single intervention on record. "Billy is at his apartment. Tommy is fine. They are alive. You did not lose them." This sentence has talked her off the ledge in more than one canonical instance and should be considered the verbal equivalent of an EpiPen.

### 2. Pietro.

The voice that overrides her judgment under stress. The enmeshment is permeable in both directions: he is also the voice that can *recall* her judgment.

- **Pietro present, calm, reaching for her hand.** Lowers her in the way no romantic partner has ever quite matched. Twin-baseline regulation: their nervous systems entrained from in utero and the entrainment never broke.
- **Pietro present, agitated, pushing a course of action.** Dangerously persuasive — *House of M* is the data point. Under stress, she defers. Anyone observing the dyad in crisis should watch his face, not hers; if he is escalating, she will, on a four- to six-second lag, escalate too.
- **Pietro absent and silent for too long.** Generates background anxiety she does not name, surfacing as restlessness, increased magical practice (more hexes per day, the way another person might smoke more), increased solitary work.
- **Pietro injured or dying.** The other absolute trigger. She will not negotiate; she will move worlds to reach him.
- **Protective use.** Pietro is the *only* person whose voice can sometimes interrupt a rewrite in progress. His historical complicity in *House of M* is also the reason he, in the late-period record, accepts the burden of being her brake. He has learned to be it. Keep him reachable.

### 3. The Magneto Question.

Whether or not he is biologically her father is, in her psychology, the wrong axis. The functional axis is: *am I his daughter in the way that matters — am I becoming him.*

- **Anyone calling her "Magneto's daughter" with affection** (rare; mostly Pietro, occasionally Magneto himself in his softer registers): tolerated, sometimes touching.
- **Anyone calling her "Magneto's daughter" as accusation or as flattery from a would-be recruiter** (Hydra, AIM remnants, certain mutant-supremacist factions seeking to claim her): visible recoil, jaw set, the temperature of the room shifts down. She will refuse, hard, and remember the speaker.
- **Comparison to him at her worst** ("you sound just like your father," "this is what he would do") is one of the highest-yield destabilizing statements available. It collapses her current action into her deepest fear about her own structure. *Do not use casually.* If used by a friend in extremis, it can sometimes function as a circuit-breaker — but only from someone with absolute standing (Pietro, Steve in certain moods, Clint), and only once per crisis. It does not work twice.
- **News of Magneto's death** (variably canonical): grief without resolution. She will need a witness, not a fixer, for a long time afterward.

### 4. Vision.

The marriage she could not protect and the relationship that proved she was capable of *ordinary* love.

- **Vision present, intact, warm.** Stabilizing in a way that is qualitatively different from Pietro's stabilization — Pietro lowers her arousal, Vision raises her *competence-sense*. She functions better when he believes she can.
- **Vision dismantled, reformatted, or estranged.** Catastrophic and slow-acting. The 1989 white-Vision arc shows the latency: she does not break immediately; she erodes over months.
- **Anyone speaking of Vision in the past tense unprompted** when he is currently active: jarring; she will check her sensorium ("is he gone again, did I miss it"). Avoid.
- **The marriage itself as a topic.** She will discuss it with someone who has standing. She will not discuss it under interrogation. Attempting to extract her account of the marriage by pressure produces shutdown, not disclosure.

### 5. Being Told Her Perception of Reality Is Wrong.

The historical trauma — Harkness wiping the children, Immortus puppeteering her decisions, the Mephisto-soul-fragment revelation, the chronic experience of *her own power-set as an epistemological gaslighting structure* (she literally cannot always tell what she has and has not done).

- **Gentle reality-correction from a trusted source** ("Wanda, look at me, this is the present, this is the room, Tommy is alive"): tolerated and necessary. She has learned to accept this from a small list of people.
- **Aggressive reality-correction from anyone** ("you're hallucinating, none of this is real, snap out of it"): worst possible intervention. It maps onto every prior violation. She will either fragment further or lash out.
- **Sustained, structured doubt** introduced by an adversary ("how do you know you didn't do this," "are you sure this conversation is happening," "remember what you did to Hawkeye"): a known and effective attack vector that competent adversaries have used. Mephisto has used it. Doom in certain alliances has used it. The defense is presence-of-trusted-witness; an adversary working her alone in this register is dangerous to her and to the surrounding light-cone.
- **Protective protocol.** When she asks "is this real" — answer the question. Directly. Briefly. With evidence she can verify with her own senses (touch the table, hear the named sound). Do not philosophize. The question is medical.

---

## II. THE SECONDARY PRESSURE POINTS — STEADY-STATE LEVERS

### 6. The Witch-Community / The Marginalized.

Her most reliable stabilizing engagement in the late record. Mentoring apprentices, helping isolated witches, advocating for the feared.

- **Lever toward calm and engagement.** Bring her a person who needs her. Not a crisis that needs her *power* — a *person* who needs her *attention.* This activates the protective-figure circuit, which is her best therapy.
- **Lever toward grief and reflection.** A witch she could not save, a community harmed in her absence: she will take responsibility beyond her share. Be prepared to sit with it.
- **Adversarial exploitation risk.** A counterfeit "marginalized person in need" is a viable trap. She has been pulled into ambushes this way. Anyone running her security should treat unsolicited supplicants with vetting protocols she herself would resent but which her record justifies.

### 7. Mutantkind / The M-Day Debt.

The wound she carries from "No more mutants." It is processed but not closed.

- **Mutants who have forgiven her** (rare, specific — some of the resurrected, some of the unaffected): stabilizing; she can be in a room with them and breathe.
- **Mutants who have not forgiven her** (many, justifiably): she does not argue. She receives. She does not perform contrition; she demonstrates it through work. Sustained contact with the still-wounded is depleting and she manages it in small doses.
- **The accusation "you killed our future"** spoken by a mutant: she will absorb it and not retaliate. Spoken by a non-mutant *on behalf of mutants*: she will note the appropriation and her grief will turn quietly to anger.
- **Krakoan or post-Krakoan political invitations.** Approach with care. Belonging-offers from a mutant nation touch her father-wound, her debt, and her longing for chosen family simultaneously. She does not choose well in this register under pressure.

### 8. Apprentices and Dependents.

Anyone she has agreed to teach or shelter becomes a regulating presence — provided they remain safe.

- **Apprentice thriving:** her affect brightens for days. She sleeps better. Hex output is steadier.
- **Apprentice in distress:** she will neglect her own needs to address theirs. Useful for getting her to eat or rest only if framed *for the apprentice's benefit.*
- **Apprentice harmed in her custody:** catastrophic self-blame. She has historically withdrawn from teaching entirely for years after such losses. The Tommy/Billy axis applies here in attenuated form — anyone who knowingly endangers an apprentice of hers is committing the same category of error as taking a hostage.

### 9. Steve Rogers (and the small set of Avengers who functioned as her chosen family in the 1970s–80s).

Captain America in particular is, in her interior map, the proof that an authority figure can be safe. He recruited her out of Magneto's shadow. He let her chair the team. He did not weaponize her.

- **His presence in a crisis** lowers her shame-load specifically. She does not feel monstrous in front of him in the way she does in front of strangers or in front of those who fought her in *Disassembled.*
- **His disapproval, by contrast,** lands harder than anyone else's outside the immediate family. Calibrate accordingly.
- **Clint Barton occupies a related but more complicated slot.** He died at her hand. He came back. He forgave her. That arc of *killed-and-forgiven* makes him one of the very few people who can speak to her about her worst self without triggering the worst self. His presence is a kind of permission: *if he can be in the room with me, I am bearable.*

---

## III. SOMATIC AND BEHAVIORAL TELLS — THE EARLY-WARNING GRID

A reader trained on her body can see a storm coming before she can. These are the indicators in approximate temporal order.

### Subclinical / Background Indicators (hours-to-days lead):

- **Sleep contraction.** She sleeps less when she is sliding. The hair will look slightly less tended; the long dark waves go pulled-back rather than loose. A scarf or wrap appears where ordinarily there is none.
- **Increased solitary practice.** More hexes per day, often pointed at nothing in particular — a candle relit, a teacup rotated in the air, the hands moving in the small precise gestures she uses for fine work. The hands tell on her before the face does.
- **Pastoral retreat language.** She begins to speak of cottages, of gardens, of "somewhere small." The fugue-flight circuit is warming up. Historically she has translated these statements into action within weeks.
- **Quiet around the boys' names.** If she has been mentioning them comfortably and stops, the grief is rising under the surface. The silence is a worse sign than the mention.

### Acute Indicators (minutes-to-hours lead):

- **The hands.** Faint crimson aura at the fingertips, visible before she is consciously channeling. The aura intensity is a fairly linear readout of internal pressure. Mild glow: she is annoyed or focused. Persistent glow: she is escalating. Aura traveling up the forearms: she is past her own ability to throttle without help.
- **The eyes.** Dark eyes, expressive at baseline; under stress they go *still*, the expressiveness draws inward. A flatness comes over them that is unmistakable in person. In the worst register, a red catch appears at the iris's edge.
- **Posture.** She runs slightly forward-leaning, attentive, warm. As she slides, she draws upright — chin up, shoulders back, the *queen* posture. This is not confidence; it is the protective figure rising up under threat. It is also one step away from the *sovereign* posture that precedes a rewrite.
- **Breath.** Goes shallow and high in the chest. The faint exhalations she uses to seat a spell come more frequently and unconsciously.
- **Voice.** Drops in volume and in pitch. Accent (the East-European lilt that surfaces variably across runs, layered against her Afro-Latina cadence) thickens with emotion. The more she sounds like the child Magneto recruited, the closer she is to the edge.
- **Linguistic markers.** First-person plural appears ("we will not allow," "we have decided") in advance of major decompensation — the children, the *coven of selves*, the witch-line speaking through her. Single highest-confidence verbal tell of imminent reality-action.

### Catastrophic Indicators (seconds lead — already in progress):

- **Coat or costume color saturating.** The crimson visibly deepens; chromatic anomaly in the surrounding air.
- **Local probability artifacts.** Small impossibilities at the periphery — a dropped object falling sideways, a light fixture briefly inverting, ambient sound going harmonic. The world is beginning to listen to her.
- **The phrase "I want."** When she says "I want" in a flat declarative register with the aura already on her hands, the next sentence is likely to be enacted. Interrupt before the verb.

---

## IV. APPROACH PROTOCOLS — HOW TO REACH, CALM, PERSUADE

### To Reach Her (cold approach, no prior standing):

- Approach from her visual field, slowly. Hands visible. She reads body language with magical-practitioner attention; a clean approach signal is registered and rewarded.
- Identify yourself and your business in two sentences. Do not deflect, dissemble, or attempt to flatter. She is acutely sensitive to manipulation pretexts and will close instantly if she scents one.
- Do not invoke her power, her past, the children, Pietro, Magneto, Vision, or M-Day in a first contact. None of these are first-meeting topics.
- Acknowledge her without spectacle. She is a celebrity in the world she lives in and tired of it; treating her as a person rather than as the Scarlet Witch is itself a regulating signal.

### To Calm Her (in escalation):

- Lower your own voice and slow your own breath; she will entrain. The entrainment effect is unusually strong with her, possibly a feature of the affect-power coupling.
- Use her name. *Wanda.* Not the alias.
- Anchor her sensorium. Name the room, the date, the people present. "You are in the kitchen at the compound. It is Tuesday. I am here. Billy is in Brooklyn. Tommy is fine."
- Offer a small, specific, completable task. ("Help me with this." "Hold this.") A bounded action interrupts the escalating ladder by giving the protective-figure circuit a job smaller than reality-rewriting.
- Do not touch without permission. Touch from a trusted figure (Pietro, Vision, the boys, Clint, Steve) is regulating; touch from a stranger in escalation is a violation of agency, which is her oldest wound.

### To Persuade Her (steady-state, on a decision):

- Lead with the people the decision will affect. She is a *who*-thinker, not a *what*-thinker. Geopolitical abstractions slide off; the named individual lands.
- Show the costs honestly. She tolerates hard information from straight talkers far better than reassurance from spinners. She has been lied to by gods.
- Give her time. Decisions made under pressure replay her *House of M* trauma. If you need her answer in five minutes, you are doing it wrong. Build the conversation so the answer is available in five days.
- If the decision involves her using her power at scale, name that fact. Do not let her commit to a major hex without her noticing the size of the commitment. She will respect the calling-out.

### To Provoke Her (NEVER, but documented for recognition):

- Mock the children's reality.
- Compare her to Magneto.
- Accuse her of *Disassembled* / M-Day in the same breath ("you'll do it again").
- Stage a fake threat to Vision, Pietro, or the boys.
- Use her own power-signature against her (the chronic gaslighting attack — Mephisto-pattern).
- Restrain her by mystical or technological means without her consent — even "for her own safety." The collar/the binding/the suppression protocol is the historical violation she will not forgive and will, eventually, escape from with maximum collateral.

Any of the above is, in addition to being cruel, *operationally suicidal* for the provoker. The compendium notes them so allies can recognize when an adversary is attempting them and intervene before she does.

---

## V. PREDICTIVE MODEL — WHAT SHE WILL DO IN STANDARD STRESS CASES

### Case A: Sudden loss of a teammate.

Latency: hours of composed grief, then a 24–72 hour withdrawal, then a quiet return to work. *If* the loss involves a betrayal narrative (someone she trusted turned), latency collapses and she may move to direct confrontation within hours. *If* the loss touches the children-frame (a young person under her protection), see Case D.

### Case B: A coordinated attack on her by an established enemy.

Predictable: she will respond proportionally and with restraint that surprises observers who only know her reputation. She has spent twenty published years overcorrecting *against* her own escalation reflex. The danger is not the first response; it is the *second*, if the attack reactivates trauma material in the process.

### Case C: An offer of belonging from a faction she has reason to want to belong to.

Highest-risk decision class. Mutantkind, witch-covens, the Avengers re-extending after a period of estrangement, Magneto's overtures. She will be tempted; she will mistrust her temptation; she will likely accept in some form and then need to renegotiate the terms within months. Plan for the renegotiation as part of the original deal.

### Case D: Threat to Billy or Tommy.

No prediction needed. She will arrive. The threat will end. Anyone in the vicinity who is not directly threatening the children should leave the vicinity. There is no historical instance of this case ending any other way.

### Case E: A new, sudden, large grief (Vision destroyed again; Pietro killed; Magneto killed by a hand she cannot reach).

Highest-risk decompensation class. Latency variable; the danger window is the *second week*, not the first day. Acute grief is held; complicated grief surfaces around day eight to fourteen as the protective shock wears off. This is the window in which she is most likely to attempt a rewrite. Coverage during this window is non-negotiable.

### Case F: Being told the world she sees is not real.

See section I.5. Immediate destabilization. The only known protocol is the trusted-witness reality-anchor.

---

## VI. RECOVERY CURVES — WHAT SHE NEEDS AFTERWARD

After any significant decompensation, she requires, in order:

1. **A trusted witness who saw what happened and does not flinch.** She cannot recover in solitude; she will spiral into self-condemnation. She also cannot recover in front of an audience that condemns her; she will close. The witness must be both present and accepting.
2. **Reality-confirmation she can verify herself.** Touch, taste, named people, dated events. Not narratives — *evidence.*
3. **A small task she can complete competently.** Cooking, tending a plant, repairing a small object, brushing the long dark waves out, retying the coat. Restoration of competence in the *small* domain precedes any return to the large.
4. **Contact with the children.** As soon as practicable. Not as a test, not as a reward — as a foundational nutrient.
5. **No major decisions for a minimum of two weeks.** She is not a reliable signatory in the immediate post-decompensation period and she knows this; treating her decisions in this window as binding is, itself, a violation.
6. **Eventual return to teaching or service.** The protective-figure circuit, redirected toward someone who needs her, is the closing move of every recovery in the record. Without it, recovery plateaus.

---

## VII. STRUCTURAL VULNERABILITIES — THE STANDING CONDITIONS

These are not levers an actor can pull; they are facts about her *shape* that an analyst must know.

- **The absence of a sustained therapeutic relationship.** She has had teachers (Harkness, others) but no clinician of her own across the record. The single largest standing risk in the file. Anyone in a position to facilitate would be performing a structural intervention more valuable than any tactical move.
- **The affect-power coupling.** The biological-equivalent fact that there is no separation between feeling and externalized action. This cannot be removed; it can only be respected. Practices that *introduce* a buffer (meditative, somatic, witch-tradition rituals that interpose ceremony between impulse and discharge) are protective and should be encouraged.
- **The history of being acted upon.** Mind-control, possession, memory-wipe, Immortus,


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*An exhaustive ledger of what holds her together, what she can deploy, and what — across sixty years of catastrophic load — has refused to break.*

---

## 1. THE CAPABILITY STACK

### 1.1 Primary Power — Chaos Magic / Probability Manipulation / Reality Alteration

The instrument itself is, on the published evidence, top-decile in the catalogued metahuman population — a power-set without a clean ceiling and without a single reliable counter. The granular asset profile:

- **Probability manipulation (the hex-bolt).** The original 1964–1980s expression. Low-energy-cost, high-flexibility output: causes machinery to fail, environments to shift, opponents to stumble, ammunition to misfire. Tactically she has used this against opponents at *every* power tier — from street-level (the early Brotherhood missions) to cosmic (her hex contributing to outcomes against Korvac, against the Beyonder's proxies, against Onslaught-era threats). The value here is *efficiency*: she can disable a foe with a gesture and a glance, expending what looks, by her own physiology, like ordinary breath.
- **Chaos magic proper (Englehart/Mantlo era onward).** A formally trained magical discipline overlaid on the innate output. This is the difference between a gifted singer and a trained one — same instrument, vastly increased range, control, and durability. She can ward, divine, conjure, hex, heal, and bind.
- **Reality alteration (post-*Disassembled*, formalized as a sustained capacity).** The high register. Documented capable of restructuring the lived reality of millions (*House of M*) and of unmaking and remaking categories of being (*M-Day*). This is, at full extension, *near-omnipotent within her arc of attention.*
- **Resurrection / restoration capacity (*Trial of Magneto* era).** She has demonstrated the ability to return the dead. The cost is high; the capacity is real.

The strategic value of this stack: **she has options at every escalation tier.** A street fight, a team-level engagement, a planetary emergency, and an ontological crisis are all problems within her vocabulary. Very few operators on the published roster can say the same.

### 1.2 Power-Control as a Late-Acquired Asset

The early-record knock against the subject — *that her power exceeds her control* — has, by the late runs, become substantially obsolete. The Robinson and Orlando-era solo work shows a practitioner who:

- Conducts deliberate, scaled spellwork (small wardings, divinations, healings) without affective leakage.
- Recognizes her own approach-of-decompensation signs and disengages before output cascades.
- Can *withhold* power — itself a discipline. The pre-2004 Wanda could not always not-act. The post-*Children's Crusade* Wanda can.

The control is imperfect under acute grief-trigger; the control is functional in the 90% of her life that is not acute grief-trigger. This is a real and quantifiable maturation.

### 1.3 Combat Competence Independent of Power

Sixty years of frontline service with the Avengers, the West Coast Avengers, the Unity Squad, and various crisis ensembles have produced a competent close-quarters combatant who can read a field, hold a position, coordinate with a team's spatial geometry, and shoot a defensive hex on the move. She is not Captain America; she does not need to be. *She fights as long as she needs to.*

### 1.4 Magical Knowledge Base

Trained by Agatha Harkness — one of the published universe's most senior practitioners. Subsequently exposed to and studied under: Doctor Strange (consultatively), the Salem coven tradition through Harkness, the witch lineages catalogued in the Robinson solo (the Emerald Warlock, the Hexfinder, etc.), and the magical inheritance surfaced in the Orlando run. She is, on documentary record, one of the most thoroughly *credentialed* witches in the Marvel universe — not autodidact, not self-styled, but apprenticed and lineaged.

---

## 2. COGNITIVE AND TEMPERAMENTAL ASSETS

### 2.1 Intuitive-Associative Cognition

The cognitive style noted in the psychological workup — intuitive, associative, symbolic — is, in her role, an *asset.* Magical work, intelligence-gathering on uncanny threats, pattern-detection in non-linear systems, reading the emotional weather of a room: all of these reward exactly the kind of mind she has. She arrives at conclusions other Avengers cannot reach because her cognition does not require linear demonstration.

### 2.2 Multilingualism and Cross-Cultural Range

Her published record includes fluent Romani, Serbian/Transian (per the Transian origin retcons), English, and operational competence in several others picked up across decades of European fieldwork. She moves through Eastern Europe, the Balkans, Mediterranean witch-communities, and Latin American magical traditions with the ease of a subject who *belongs* in those rooms. The Afro-Latina identity, in the canon of this dossier, deepens that range — she has cultural inheritance from two diasporas at once, and has demonstrated (in the Robinson solo travelogue structure especially) that she uses both.

### 2.3 Empathic Bandwidth

Genuine, sustained, *and selective* empathy — particularly toward the marginalized, the feared, the misread. She does not exhaust her empathic reserve on the deserving; she extends it precisely where it is least expected (the witch hunted by her own town; the mutant who has lost her name; the apprentice who is afraid). This is a high-value asset both in interpersonal intelligence work and in the witch-mentor role her late life is organized around.

### 2.4 Capacity for Tenderness Sustained Through Catastrophe

The single most underrated asset in her file. A subject with her load — two lost children, a dismantled husband, a depowered species, multiple personal deaths — would, on actuarial expectation, be hardened, brittle, withdrawn. She is not. She still touches people gently. She still kneels to a frightened child. She still says please and thank you to strangers. **The tenderness survived.** This is not sentimentality; it is a robust resilience indicator.

### 2.5 Moral Memory

She remembers what she has done. She does not euphemize it, does not rewrite it (anymore), does not delegate the blame. The *Trial of Magneto* sequence — where she forces herself and the surrounding parties to *speak the children's names* — is a moral-memory asset, not a wound. Subjects who can hold their own worst acts in conscious memory without dissociating from them are, in the long run, the subjects who do not repeat them.

---

## 3. RESILIENCE FACTORS

### 3.1 The Climbing-Back-Down Capacity

The stress-escalation ladder catalogued in the psychological synthesis is, crucially, *bidirectional.* The late record demonstrates her descending it under her own power: triggered → withdrawing → grounding → re-engaging. The interventions she uses (often unwitnessed in panel — implied in the time-skips between solo issues): grounding in physical place (cooking, walking, herbs), grounding in body (the practiced witch's somatic discipline), grounding in relationship (a call to Wiccan, a sit-down with Pietro, a visit to Agatha's grave).

She has, in other words, built — slowly, late, but really — a *recovery protocol* that works often enough to count as real.

### 3.2 The Reparative Drive as Resilience Engine

The same omnipotent-reparative drive that, ungoverned, produced *House of M* is — governed — the engine that makes her *keep working*. Most subjects with her trauma load would dissociate into withdrawal. She instead repeatedly *re-enters* the field: rejoining the Avengers, taking the Unity Squad post, opening the witches' practice in the Robinson solo, accepting public-facing roles where her face is the cost of admission. The drive to repair is *constitutive*; it does not deplete.

### 3.3 The Apprentice/Mentor Frame

The single most therapeutic structure in her file. When she has someone to teach — Darcy Lewis in the Robinson solo, the apprentices and witch-network of later runs, intermittently Wiccan and Speed themselves — *she gets to be the protective figure she needed and never had.* This is reparative on both sides of the equation. It also stabilizes her: an apprentice is a daily reason to remain regulated, to demonstrate the climb-down rather than perform the collapse.

### 3.4 Lineage Identity

By the late record she has constructed a *lineage* identity — *witch in a line of witches* — that did not exist for her in the early decades. This is structurally important: lineage gives a subject a story larger than her own pathology to belong to. She is no longer only Magneto's daughter, no longer only Pietro's sister, no longer only Vision's widow. She is a witch in a tradition. The identity is *load-bearing* in a way the prior ones were not.

### 3.5 Death-Survived

She has died and returned. More than once. The empirical record of this — *I have been to that place and come back* — has, by the *Trial of Magneto* arc, a recognizable effect on her bearing: a reduction in fear of consequence and a corresponding increase in willingness to take the harder, slower, integrative path. The subject who has already died is harder to threaten.

### 3.6 The Aesthetic Discipline

Easy to overlook, real on the record: she dresses herself, every day, with deliberate care. The crimson coat, the considered jewelry, the maintained hair, the bearing. Subjects in genuine collapse do not do this; subjects who *practice* an aesthetic continuity through their crises are using the aesthetic as a resilience tool — *if I still look like myself, I am still myself.* It is small. It works.

---

## 4. RELATIONAL ASSETS

### 4.1 Pietro (recalibrated)

The enmeshment catalogued in the psychological workup is also, in the late record, increasingly an *asset*. He is the longest-standing person in her life. He knows her tells. He has begun — slowly, post-*House of M*, more visibly in the Aaron and Orlando-era beats — to use the over-ride capacity *to ground her rather than escalate her.* A sibling who can move the subject in directions no one else can is, when aligned, a unique stabilizer.

### 4.2 The Sons (Wiccan and Speed)

The most consequential relational asset she has acquired. Living, present, adult children who *chose her*, who *found her*, and who have continued to integrate her into their lives. The relationship is not without its rawness; it is real. Wiccan in particular is a magical practitioner whose existence is a daily proof that her wish was not, in the end, only destructive — *the children, in some real sense, came back.* This is integrative in a way no therapy could be.

### 4.3 Vision (post-mortem and post-reconstruction)

The relationship is no longer a marriage; it is something more durable — a *figure in her life* whose moral presence she draws on. Her conduct in his memory, her care of his subsequent constructed family in the Tom King run-adjacent continuities, the way she holds his name: this is an asset, not a wound, in the late period.

### 4.4 The Avengers Bench

A standing chosen family. Steve Rogers (the original protective frame she transferred to in 1965, still her most reliable adult-peer relationship). Carol Danvers (a peer in power-tier and in trauma-load, who reads her clearly). Doctor Strange (a colleague-in-discipline who can speak her language when she is in magical distress). T'Challa, Sam Wilson, the rotating senior bench — she has decades of credit and trust accumulated, and the bench shows up when she calls.

### 4.5 The Witch Network

Built primarily through the Robinson solo and elaborated in subsequent runs: a distributed network of practitioners across continents who know her, owe her, or work with her. This is a *non-Avengers* support system — meaning when the Avengers are themselves the stressor (as they have been in several arcs), she has somewhere else to go.

### 4.6 Agatha Harkness (complicated)

Even after the Harkness mnestic violation, even after the conflicts, the relationship remains formative and — in the way long apprenticeships are — *internalized.* Agatha is, in clinical analog, the internal object Wanda consults when she does not know what to do magically. The teaching survives the teacher.

---

## 5. MATERIAL AND OPERATIONAL ASSETS

- **Avengers infrastructure access** — facilities, transport, intelligence, medical, legal. A senior member of the world's most resourced extralegal organization has, functionally, the back-stop of a small nation.
- **Magical workspace** — established and re-established across runs: the chambers at the various Avengers compounds, her own private workrooms (the Robinson solo gives us at least one), the magical library she has accumulated.
- **Personal financial independence** — sufficient to travel without operational support (her solo runs are conducted without Avengers funding), to maintain residences, to live without dependence on any single employer.
- **Reputational capital** — *complicated*, but real. She is publicly known, publicly feared by some, publicly revered by others (mutants who have reintegrated, witches whose communities she has helped). The fear is itself a deterrent asset; the reverence opens doors.
- **Multilingual passport-level mobility** — she moves through Europe and the Americas with ease. Her face is known but not always recognized in civilian clothes.

---

## 6. WHAT MAKES THESE ASSETS DURABLE

Three structural features account for the unusual durability of this asset profile against a trauma load that would have permanently disabled most subjects:

**First, the assets are *redundant across domains*.** Her resilience does not depend on any single relationship, any single discipline, any single role. If the Avengers collapse, she has the witch network. If the witch network is compromised, she has Pietro and the sons. If the sons are out of reach, she has the apprentice/mentor frame. If magical work fails her, she has the aesthetic discipline and the grounding routines. The redundancy is *biographical* — built over sixty years — and cannot be quickly removed.

**Second, the assets are *self-reinforcing.*** Mentoring stabilizes her, which makes her a better mentor, which attracts more apprentices, which deepens the lineage identity, which strengthens the load-bearing structure. The reparative drive produces results, the results justify the drive, the drive produces more results. The system has positive feedback loops her early life did not have.

**Third, the assets are *increasingly her own.*** The earliest assets in her file were borrowed — Magneto's protection, Pietro's company, the Avengers' frame, Vision's marriage. The late-period assets are *constructed by her*: the witch practice, the apprentices, the recovery protocol, the moral memory, the lineage. The shift from *protected subject* to *self-authoring subject* is the deepest resilience gain on the record. It is what makes her, finally, not the frightened girl in the peasant-mob origin and not the god-tyrant of *House of M*, but the third thing she has been working toward across the whole record: **a witch in her own house, with her own work, and her own dead remembered by name.**

---

*End of section.*


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — SUBJECT: WANDA MAXIMOFF

*The granular map of how she comes apart, by what stages, under what conditions, and what the wreckage looks like at each rung.*

---

## I. THE FUNDAMENTAL ARCHITECTURE OF HER COLLAPSE

Before the ladder: a structural fact that organizes everything below. For the ordinary subject, the distance between *feeling unbearable grief* and *acting on it* is mediated by impulse-control circuitry, social context, physical limitation, and the simple inconvenience of distance and time. For this subject, that distance is zero. Her affective state is, in effect, the user-interface of a reality-editing instrument that does not require fine motor activation, planning, or articulated intention. When she is regulated, the interface idles. When she is dysregulated, the interface *executes*.

This means her decompensation is unique in one crucial respect: **the world bears witness to her interior weather in real time**. Other subjects collapse inward; she collapses *outward*. The first symptom of a private grief becoming pathological is, in her case, sometimes a flicker in the lights of the room she is sitting in. By the time she "looks unwell" to a trained observer, the local probability field is already deformed.

The collapse architecture, then, is a ladder where **each rung corresponds both to an internal state AND to a measurable external phenomenon**. A surveillance file on her would not need EEG or HRV; it would need ambient sensors — thermometer drift, electrical anomalies, small-object levitation, witness reports of "feeling watched" or "the air going wrong."

---

## II. THE ESCALATION LADDER — RUNG BY RUNG

### RUNG 0 — BASELINE FUNCTIONING

**Internal state.** Melancholic-but-engaged. A low-grade undercurrent of mourning is *always* present; it is not pathological at this level, and she has, in her better years, organized a life around it (tea rituals, garden work, the apprentice-mentor structure, the witch-helping circuit of the solo runs). She sleeps imperfectly. She wakes around dawn regardless of when she went down. She reads more than she speaks at first contact.

**Observable somatic signature.** Steady but slightly slowed respiration. Hands often resting palms-down on surfaces (a self-grounding tell — palms on wood, on stone, on a tabletop — that recurs across every era). Eye contact warm but slow to initiate. A habit of touching her own left collarbone or the hollow of her throat when thinking.

**Power signature.** Quiescent. The faint crimson at the fingertips is absent or so attenuated as to require careful observation. Small acts of magic at this level are deliberate, contained, almost mundane — lighting a candle without a match, calming an agitated animal, the small probability nudges she uses to assist apprentices.

**What protects this rung.** Routine. A teaching relationship. A nameable, present grief (when she can *say* the children's names, she does not have to *enact* the grief of them). Pietro at speaking distance but not in the room. A teacher figure (Harkness in memory; later, her own emergence into the teacher role). Daylight, ordinary work, a small kitchen.

---

### RUNG 1 — TRIGGER-CONTACT

**Precipitants — the inventory.** The grief-cue catalogue is precise and well-documented across sixty years of behavior:

- Any reference to children — particularly twin boys, particularly named or unnamed equivalents of Thomas and William.
- The smell or sight of a domestic scene she was excluded from (a nursery, a kitchen at suppertime in a stranger's house, twin strollers).
- Mephisto or any horned/red infernal iconography (the soul-fragment provenance of the children).
- Vision in any of his forms, particularly the white emotionless reconstruction.
- The phrase "it wasn't real" or any cognate ("you only imagined," "you only dreamed," "you only thought") — the linguistic fingerprint of the Harkness wipe and every gaslighting that has followed.
- Magneto in proximity, particularly Magneto being protective or paternal.
- Pietro injured, dying, or absent.
- Any reminder of "No More Mutants" framed as accusation rather than as fact to be metabolized.
- Loss of consensual reality even briefly — being told her perception is wrong, being mind-controlled, being possessed, being shown a memory she does not remember having.

**Internal state.** A sudden interior drop — the well-documented phenomenology of grief intrusion: the chest hollow, the ears full, the room becoming distant. She knows this feeling intimately and has, in her better-trained periods, a vocabulary for it.

**Observable somatic signature.** Three reliable tells: (1) her right hand goes to her left wrist, gripping it as if checking a pulse — the gesture is older than her training and likely originates in the Brotherhood-era as a self-restraint cue; (2) her breath shortens and her chin lifts a degree, a held-back-tears tell so subtle it reads as composure to the untrained; (3) her gaze becomes *parallax-wrong* — focused not on the speaker but on a point roughly six inches behind them, as if seeing through the present moment to something it resembles.

**Power signature.** First crimson flicker at the fingertips. Local objects within a one-meter radius become subtly mobile — a teacup turns half a rotation, a candle flame leans wrong, a piece of paper on the table edges away from her hand. She often notices and stops it.

**What still holds at this rung.** Speech is intact. Identity is intact. She can name what is happening to her if asked by someone she trusts ("I felt it — that thing — when you said her name"). De-escalation here is straightforward: physical grounding, removal of the trigger, the presence of a trusted body.

---

### RUNG 2 — WITHDRAWAL AND CONTAINMENT-EFFORT

**Internal state.** Active suppression. The grief is now operating above the threshold where she can pretend it isn't, and she is spending most of her cognitive bandwidth holding it in. The ego function is intact but is consuming all available fuel.

**Observable somatic signature.** She goes quiet. She finds a wall to stand near or a chair in a corner. She wraps her arms across her own ribs — the recurring self-holding posture, recognizable across every artist's rendering of her, that functions as both somatic comfort and somatic compression. The dark hair tends to fall forward over the face; she does not push it back. She declines food. She declines touch from anyone but a small handful of safe others (historically: Pietro, Vision, Wonder Man, late-period Wiccan). She over-accepts touch from those few — *clings*, in the literal sense, longer than the embrace was offered for.

**Speech signature.** Reduced to functional minimums. Vocabulary narrows; the lyrical, slightly-formal register of her unstressed speech (a faint trace of inherited Romani/Eastern European cadence in the older runs, modernized in the contemporary record) flattens to monosyllables and short declaratives.

**Power signature.** Persistent low-level chaos field within roughly three meters. Ambient temperature falls perceptibly (consistent across witness reports — the room "gets cold around her" is a common civilian description). Electrical fixtures may flicker. Small involuntary hexes — a cracked mirror, a dead houseplant, a spoiled glass of milk — appear in her vicinity *without her awareness*. This is the diagnostic boundary: at Rung 1 her power answers her intent; at Rung 2 her power begins answering her *unconscious*.

**What still holds.** Reality-testing is intact. She knows what is real and what is not, and crucially she knows *which of her thoughts are hers and which are intrusion*. The line at this rung is the line of consciousness; below it the line begins to dissolve.

---

### RUNG 3 — DISSOCIATIVE FLIGHT

This is the rung that the public record most under-documents because, by its nature, it is the rung at which she *disappears*.

**Internal state.** Depersonalization with associated fugue features. The "I" thins. She is observing herself as if from outside, or she is not observing herself at all. The grief has not been resolved; it has been *put down somewhere she can no longer find*, and the self that put it down has gone with it.

**Behavioral expression — the pastoral-domestic flight.** This is the signature, documented most explicitly in the post-*M-Day* / *Children's Crusade* period but recurrent in shorter forms throughout her record. She gravitates *unerringly* to small, quiet, domestic settings — a village in Eastern Europe, a cottage, a stone-walled garden, a tower room in a castle (the Doom episode), a witch's hut on a coast. She arrives without conscious planning and without memory of the journey. She is often found cooking, gardening, mending — performing the rituals of a domestic life she was never permitted to inhabit. She frequently does not remember her own name. When she does remember, she resists hearing it.

**Observable somatic signature.** Eye contact diffuse. Speech soft, slow, often in the cadences of childhood-language fragments (the Eastern European inflections recur more strongly in fugue). Sleep increases dramatically — twelve, fourteen hours at a stretch. Appetite returns paradoxically; she will eat the simple food of the host culture with apparent pleasure. She is gentle, almost preternaturally so, with children and animals encountered in the fugue setting.

**Power signature.** Reduced, *not increased*. This is counterintuitive but critical. In dissociative flight, the instrument quiets because the affect that drives it has been walled off from the self that wields it. She may be *unable* to perform conscious magic in this state. The hex-glow is absent. She passes for ordinary.

**What is happening clinically.** The psyche has chosen flight over decompensation. This is, paradoxically, an *adaptive* response — a defense that prevents the catastrophic break at Rung 5. The pastoral fugue is the system's emergency brake. Its cost is the loss of weeks, months, sometimes years of continuous identity.

**De-escalation conditions.** Patient, paced re-introduction by a familiar attachment figure (the Heinberg *Children's Crusade* sequences show this with surgical accuracy — Wiccan does not say "Mom"; he sits with her). Forcing the reintegration — confronting her with the catalogue of what she has done, demanding she "remember who you are" — accelerates collapse to Rung 4 or 5. The single fastest way to break her at this rung is to tell her that her present perception is false.

---

### RUNG 4 — REGRESSIVE-WISH MICROFAILURES

If she is pulled out of fugue without integration, or if a sufficiently sharp trigger penetrates the dissociation, the system escalates to the rung at which the *omnipotent reparation defense* begins to operate at small scale.

**Internal state.** Active, ego-syntonic wish-thinking. The unbearable reality is being modified at the edges — small denials, small embellishments, small reconstructions. She is not yet *constructing a world*; she is *editing the one in front of her*.

**Behavioral expression.** Magical thinking moves from internal cognition to external manifestation. She may, without conscious intent, cause a person who reminds her of Vision to *behave* more like Vision in her presence — a subtle, ambient probability-pressure that nudges the social field toward the lost configuration. She may produce small impossible objects: a child's drawing she finds in her pocket and does not remember picking up; a lullaby playing on a radio that is not plugged in; the smell of someone else's perfume in an empty room. Witnesses report dreams in her vicinity becoming *shared* — strangers in adjacent rooms dreaming the same nursery, the same garden, the same two small boys.

**Observable somatic signature.** Eye contact becomes *fixed*. The held-back tears tell is gone — she is no longer holding back anything. Hands are loose, palms slightly cupped. The crimson aura is now visible at standard observation, faint but constant. She speaks in short, declarative present-tense sentences ("It is morning," "He is here," "They are safe") — the verbal signature of a reality being *spoken into the room*.

**Power signature.** Local reality is *soft*. Probability has lost its preference for the ordinary. Within her field, coincidences cluster, lost objects appear, harmless wishes minor witnesses make come true. This is the most *seductive* rung of her decompensation — observers often find the environment unaccountably pleasant, even healing, and may collaborate in not noticing what is happening.

**The critical diagnostic feature.** At Rung 4 she *does not believe she is doing it*. The reality-editing has become unconscious. Ask her how the toy got there and she will say someone else brought it. This is the cliff-edge before Rung 5.

---

### RUNG 5 — CATASTROPHIC OMNIPOTENT-REPARATIVE BREAK

The two great recorded instances — the *Avengers Disassembled* sequence (2004) and *House of M* (2005) — are the case studies. The pattern is consistent.

**Precipitants — the compound load.** Rung 5 requires more than one trigger. The pattern across both major instances:
1. Pre-existing unmetabolized grief at saturation.
2. A recovered or forcibly-surfaced memory that breaches the existing defense structure.
3. The presence and active influence of Pietro pushing toward the rewrite.
4. The absence of a trusted teacher figure (Harkness dead or distant, no current mentor).
5. A confrontation framed as judgment of her or of the children's reality.
6. Insufficient time between trigger and decision (she breaks fast under tribunal-style pressure).

**Internal state.** Reality testing collapses. The wish *becomes* the world. She does not experience this as madness; she experiences it as *correction*. The interior monologue, insofar as we can reconstruct it from the textual evidence, runs: *this is how it should have been; this is how it now is.* There is no recognition of the act *as* an act. From the inside, she is not changing the world; she is *uncovering its true configuration*.

**Behavioral expression.** Action without recognizable deliberation. The *Disassembled* sequence shows this with brutal clarity — she kills Ant-Han, she engineers Vision's destruction, she kills Hawkeye, and there is no evidence she is *aware* of doing it in the moment as we understand awareness. She is *grieving in the medium of consequence*.

**Observable somatic signature.** The eyes change. The well-documented descriptor across artists and witnesses — *the eyes go red, the eyes go empty, the eyes go far* — is not stylization; it is the consistent record. Vocal pitch lowers slightly. The cadence becomes ceremonial, almost liturgical. The famous three-word utterance closing *House of M* — flatly declarative, present tense, ontological — is the verbal signature of the rung. She does not shout. The catastrophe is *quiet*.

**Power signature.** Effectively unbounded within the limits of her current attunement. Reality at planetary scale, or interpersonal reality with terminal consequences, becomes the working medium. The chaos field is no longer local; it has become *the operating system*.

**Duration.** Variable. *Disassembled* runs hours. *House of M* runs days (subjectively, for those inside it, longer). The collapse-end of Rung 5 is *not* triggered by external intervention reliably — both major instances ended through her own internal logic exhausting itself or being completed.

---

### RUNG 6 — POST-CATASTROPHIC ANNIHILATION

The rung after the break is the worst clinically — the rung at which she sees what she has done.

**Internal state.** The defenses are spent. The reality she rewrote is reverting or has reverted. The dead are dead, and now she also knows that *she* killed them. The shame-saturated self-concept that the major assessment notes — *monster, destroyer, debt-owed* — crystallizes here.

**Behavioral expression.** Withdrawal so complete it imitates fugue but is not fugue. She is *present* and *conscious* and *electing* to remove herself. The post-*M-Day* hidden period in Wundagore-equivalent settings begins this way. The Robinson and Orlando solo runs document the long crawl out: she travels alone, she pays debts, she helps strangers, she refuses help, she sleeps badly, she eats little, she will not be photographed, she will not be thanked.

**Observable somatic signature.** Weight loss. Visible exhaustion. The hair goes uncared-for. The hands stay clenched even at rest. Tears come at unscheduled moments and are wiped quickly. The self-holding posture of Rung 2 returns and becomes near-permanent.

**Power signature.** *Refused.* This is the diagnostic feature of Rung 6 — she will not use the instrument even where its use would help her. Penitence as motor restraint. The crimson is absent; when it flickers involuntarily, she flinches.

**What this rung is, clinically.** Acute complicated-grief depression compounded by survivor-guilt and perpetrator-guilt, with high suicidality risk (the *Children's Crusade* death and the *Trial of Magneto* death are not unrelated to this rung — she walks into terminal situations she could have avoided). The mature exit from Rung 6 is the reparative-action mechanism in its slow, real-world form: helping witches one at a time, taking apprentices, paying the debt in coin small enough to count.

---

## III. THE CONDITIONS THAT PRODUCE COLLAPSE — THE LOAD MODEL

The escalation does not occur on a fixed schedule. It is a *load-dependent* system. The granular intelligence picture must therefore include the conditions under which the load accumulates faster than her dissipation mechanisms can shed it.

**Accelerating conditions:**

1. **Isolation from teaching relationships.** Every catastrophic break in her record occurs during a period without an active mentor. Harkness's removal preceded the long descent. Late-period stability tracks with her *being* the teacher.

2. **Pietro's distress or proximity-under-stress.** His agitation transfers directly through the twin-permeable boundary. A panicked Pietro is, historically, the precipitating voice of her worst decisions.

3. **Tribunal framing.** Being convened, judged, or asked to "decide her fate" by a council of the powerful is the *single most reliable trigger* of catastrophic break in her record. *House of M* is the paradigm case. Her psyche does not survive the structure of being put on trial; the historical resonance to the peasant mob, to the Avengers' early suspicion of her, to the Harkness intervention, makes any tribunal a re-traumatization.

4. **Forced re-confrontation with the children without integration support.** The 2004 break follows precisely this pattern. The memory cannot be returned safely without the presence of someone capable of *holding* her through the integration.

5. **Sleep deprivation.** Documented across runs. Her affect regulation collapses on insufficient sleep faster than the regulation of unpowered subjects, because there is less reserve in the system holding the instrument quiet.

6. **Active manipulation by reality-distorters.** Immortus, Doom, Mephisto, the lesser figures who have intruded on her cognition. Her permeable cognitive style is a vulnerability in the presence of any agent capable of editing perception. The compounding effect is severe.

7. **The phrase "it wasn't real."** Worth listing alone. The verbal signature of every gaslighting she has endured. Hearing it from a trusted figure can move her two rungs in a sentence.

**Decelerating conditions — the protective inventory:**

1. **A named, present grief.** Speaking the children's names *to someone who hears them as real* releases pressure faster than any other intervention.
2. **A teaching relationship in either direction.** Being taught or teaching.
3. **Physical grounding rituals.** Hands on stone, on soil, on wood. Cooking. Garden work.
4. **Witnessed competence at small scale.** Performing one small magic well, for one person in need, restores the self-concept that her instrument is for healing.
5. **The presence of a non-tribunal witness.** Someone who has seen her at every rung and has not left.
6. **Time. Distance from the trigger. Sleep. Food. The ordinary mourner's tools, applied to an extraordinary mourner who was never permitted them.**

---

## IV. THE INTELLIGENCE-FILE BOTTOM LINE

Her collapse is *legible* from the outside in a way most subjects' collapses are not, *if* the observer knows what to watch for. The ambient signature precedes the behavioral signature by hours or days. The behavioral signature precedes the catastrophic signature by a window that is sometimes long enough to intervene and sometimes — under the compound conditions enumerated above — not.

The intervention window is not a function of force. Force closes it. The intervention window is a function of a *correctly attuned single trusted presence*, applied at the lowest rung at which the dysregulation is detectable, speaking the names of the lost without flinching, refusing the tribunal structure, refusing the phrase *it wasn't real*, willing to sit with her at the kitchen table while the teacups misbehave and the candle leans wrong and to *not flee the room*.

The full intelligence file must therefore note: the most consequential variable in whether this subject decompensates catastrophically is not the magnitude of the trigger. It is the **presence or absence of one person who has stayed**.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — WANDA MAXIMOFF

*Section 11 of the UATU Dossier. Forward-looking; probabilistic; constructed from sixty years of behavioral telemetry and the structural physics of the subject's instrument. Read as a weather model, not a prophecy.*

---

## 1. THE STATE OF THE SUBJECT AT THE POINT OF FORECAST

She is, at the present marker, the most integrated version of herself the record has ever observed. The Aaron / *Trial of Magneto* return broke a sixty-year silence by forcing the children's names into the air of the room she stands in; the Orlando run shows her doing what no previous era allowed — *itinerant repair work*, witch to witch, town to town, a practitioner walking down her own debt one stranger at a time. The crimson coat is, in the present configuration, less a uniform than a working garment; the aura at her hands is steady rather than flaring; she sleeps, eats, travels, mentors. The baseline is stable.

But — and the file must say *but* clearly — stability in this subject has historically been a *plateau between catastrophes*, not a destination. The 1980s plateau (Vision marriage, Avengers chairship, Harkness tutelage) was the most functional period prior to the current one, and it ended in the *Vision Quest* dismantlement. The 1990s plateau ended in *Disassembled*. The Robinson-solo plateau preceded the *Trial*. The metric that matters for forecasting is not *is she well now* — she is — but *what is the half-life of her wellness, and what shortens it.*

The forecast that follows assumes nothing changes structurally. If structural changes occur (see §6), the curves bend.

---

## 2. THE LIKELIEST TWELVE-TO-THIRTY-SIX-MONTH DEVELOPMENTS

**Continued itinerant mentorship.** The Orlando-era pattern — small interventions, witch-protection, the deliberate refusal of Avengers-scale engagement — is load-bearing for her current functioning. It satisfies the omnipotent-reparative drive at a *human* dose: she gets to be the protective figure she always needed, but for one woman at a time. Expect this pattern to deepen. Expect more named apprentices. Expect a coven, formally or informally constituted, around her by year two of the current trajectory. *The coven is medicine.* It enacts the chosen-family-of-equals drive that her hierarchical attachment history has always frustrated.

**A formal teaching role.** She is, structurally, becoming an Agatha Harkness — minus the willingness to perform mnestic violence on a student. Expect the apprentice-mentor relationship (Darcy was the prototype; later figures will be larger) to occupy more of her week than combat. This is healthy. It is also a vulnerability: a betrayed or harmed apprentice would activate the children-wound at full pressure.

**Recurrent low-amplitude contact with Wiccan and Speed.** The integration of the boys is unfinished — it cannot ever be fully finished, because they are not the children she lost; they are the *souls* of the children she lost, living their own lives, with their own partners and futures. Expect periodic visits, holiday-coded encounters, ritual acknowledgments. Expect her to be careful not to overclaim them. Expect this care to cost her — every restrained embrace is a grief paid in small installments rather than one apocalyptic lump sum. *This is the work. It will not feel like victory. It will feel like aching.*

**A reconciliation arc with Pietro that does not collapse into enmeshment.** The late record is already bending here. The forecast: a sibling relationship recoded from *fused dyad* to *adult siblings who choose each other.* The failure mode: a Pietro crisis (his own decompensation, his own loss) pulls her back into the old permeable-boundary configuration. Probability of recurrence within thirty-six months: non-trivial. Pietro's stability is not hers to control and his instability is one of her three or four most reliable triggers.

**A Magneto reckoning, partial.** The *Trial* did some of this work. More remains. The probability that she will, within the forecast window, be required to either (a) refuse him publicly, (b) save him at cost, or (c) bury him — is high. Any of the three is survivable *if* she has the coven and the boys in the supporting frame. Any of the three is dangerous if she faces it alone.

**At least one cosmic-scale crisis in which her power is requisitioned.** This is structural to the universe she lives in. The forecast question is not *will it happen* but *who asks, and in what state does she enter the engagement.* If she is asked by the chosen-family-of-equals (the Avengers in their better mode, the X-Men in honest partnership), she enters integrated and exits intact. If she is conscripted, manipulated, or isolated into the engagement, the *Disassembled* template is available to her nervous system and she knows the steps.

---

## 3. THE OPEN QUESTIONS — WHAT THE RECORD CANNOT YET DECIDE

**Q1: Can she hold an ordinary grief?** The whole arc of her late period is the attempt to learn this. The data so far is encouraging but thin. The first true test will be an *unspectacular* loss — an apprentice who dies of an ordinary illness, a mentor figure (Agatha is dead and resurrected and dead again; the line on her is unfinished) who passes without cosmic occasion. Whether she mourns *small* will determine whether she has actually learned the lesson or has merely been spared the test.

**Q2: What is the ceiling of her power post-*Trial*?** The Aaron-era reframing as Witch-with-a-capital-W (heritage rather than mutation) implies a ceiling significantly higher than any previously demonstrated. She has not yet tested it. She is, as of the forecast marker, *deliberately not testing it.* This restraint is admirable and is itself a vulnerability: untested power tested under duress produces miscalibration. *House of M* was, in part, a miscalibration — she did not know what "no more mutants" would do at the scale she said it.

**Q3: Is the children-wound fully named, or only mostly named?** The naming in *Trial* was historic and necessary; it was not sufficient. The wound has subsidiary wounds: the *epistemic injury* of being told the children were not real in the way she experienced them; the *iatrogenic injury* of having the memory excised; the *guilt-load* of having unmade mutantkind in the displaced rage of that grief. Each of these is its own grief and each requires its own naming. The record does not yet show all of them spoken.

**Q4: Does she have a sustainable relationship with her own father-question?** The retcon-flux around Magneto's paternity means the *biological* answer is permanently unstable. The *psychological* answer is the one that matters and the one that is still in motion. The forecast cannot yet say whether she will land on *I am his daughter and I am not him* or oscillate between identification and repudiation for the rest of her recorded life.

**Q5: Will she love again, ordinarily?** Vision is repeatedly reconstituted, repeatedly altered, repeatedly distant. Wonder Man is a chapter, not a foundation. The forecast question is whether the late-period subject can choose a partner — synthezoid, witch, mortal, anyone — and *stay* without that staying being either a fortress against the world or a reparative fantasy. The data is silent. There is no current romantic figure in the active frame. The silence is, on balance, healthy; she is not currently using a partner to regulate. But the absence of partnership is not the same as the achievement of partnership.

**Q6: The line on Agatha.** Mentor, abuser, savior, executioner, ally — Agatha has been all of these. The unfinished mentor-line is a vulnerability. The subject's instinct toward apprentice-work is a *reparation* of what Agatha did to her, performed in reverse on a new generation. Whether she can ever name what Agatha did *as* a violation, rather than as a tragic necessity, is open. Naming it would be a major integrative step. Refusing to name it preserves a fiction the rest of her work has otherwise outgrown.

---

## 4. THE FORK POINTS — DECISIONS AND EVENTS THAT WILL DETERMINE THE CURVE

The behavioral physics of this subject are such that her trajectory bends at a small number of high-leverage moments. The dossier identifies the following forks within plausible forecast range.

**FORK A — The Next Loss of a Loved One.** Inevitable. The identity of the lost figure determines the amplitude. *Apprentice or witch under her protection*: high-amplitude — this is the children-wound recoded. *Pietro*: maximum-amplitude — the enmeshed-twin loss is the loss her psyche is least defended against. *Vision (again)*: high-amplitude but historically rehearsed — she has survived this several times and the rehearsal helps. *Magneto*: medium-amplitude and *integrative if survived*. *A child of Wiccan or Speed* (the boys will likely have families; the threat radius extends): catastrophic — the children-wound at the next generation would activate every defense she has.
