**FORK B — The Next Agency Violation.** The historical trauma is *being told your perception is wrong* and *having your mind / memory / will overridden.* Any mind-control episode, possession, memory tampering, or coercive reality-shift performed *on* her will activate the fastest decompensation pathway in her nervous system. The actors capable of this remain in the field (Doom, Mephisto, Immortus and his successors, any number of cosmic entities). The forecast says: *one such attempt within thirty-six months is more likely than not.* Whether it succeeds depends on her coven, her sleep, and whether she is alone at the moment of approach.

**FORK C — The Next Request to Use Her Power at Scale.** Someone will ask. The Avengers will ask, or a cosmic crisis will ask, or a planetary emergency will require the *kind* of work only her instrument can do. The fork is whether she is asked *as a peer*, with the right to refuse and the right to set the dose, or *as an asset*, with the implicit expectation that she will exceed her own safety threshold. The first preserves her. The second is the *Disassembled* template re-presented.

**FORK D — The Apprentice Who Fails.** A student of hers will, at some point, fail badly — go dark, harm an innocent, die at her own hand. How she metabolizes that failure (as her fault, as the student's, as a shared tragedy) will reveal whether the late-period integration is structural or merely circumstantial. *The healthy response is grief and continued teaching. The unhealthy response is the retreat into self-monstering ("I'm a monster, I should not teach") that the 1990s and 2000s record knows well.*

**FORK E — The Public Reckoning with M-Day.** She has done private reparation. She has not done public reparation at the scale of the harm. There is a depowered mutant population that has, in the published years, only partly forgiven her, and only partly recovered. A public confrontation — a depowered mutant's surviving family, a tribunal-coded event, a mutant nation's formal grievance — is forecastable. How she handles it (refusing the masochism of self-erasure while accepting the legitimacy of the grievance) is one of the highest-leverage integration opportunities available to her. *It is also the one she is most tempted to flee.*

**FORK F — The Question of a Child of Her Own, Again.** Whether by ordinary means, by magic, by adoption, by guardianship — the question will arise. The healthy answer is *not yet, and perhaps never as I once would have, and that is its own kind of peace.* The unhealthy answer is the reparative-construction reflex re-engaged. *The instrument can still do it.* The question is whether the practitioner has learned that *because she can does not mean she should.*

---

## 5. WHAT WOULD PUSH HER TOWARD GROWTH

In rough order of leverage:

1. **A stable, named coven.** Chosen family of equals; the structural correction for an attachment history of hierarchies. Witches are the right population — they share her epistemology, her instrument-class, and her marginalization. *A coven would do for her what AA does for an alcoholic: a room of people who cannot be lied to about the specific weather of her affliction.*
2. **A sustained therapeutic relationship — magical or mundane.** She has never had one. Agatha was a teacher and a violator, not a therapist. The integrative work she is doing on her own is heroic and insufficient. A figure who can hold the children-wound *across years* without flinching and without trying to fix it is the single most curative external presence available.
3. **Pietro's own stabilization.** Her best version requires his good-enough version. Resources spent on his integration redound to hers.
4. **Public, formal, *partial* reparation for M-Day.** Not self-erasure. Not flagellation. A named acknowledgment, a sustained material commitment, a refusal to be either villain or victim. The dosage matters.
5. **Continued small-scale practice.** Every village she helps is a hex aimed at her own self-concept. *Destroyer* erodes; *witch-in-service* accretes. The arithmetic is slow and reliable.
6. **Honest contact with the boys.** Without overclaiming them. The restraint is the medicine.
7. **A peer who can say no to her.** Someone — Storm, Captain Marvel, an equal — whose word she will accept as a check on her instrument when her instrument approaches the line. *House of M* happened in part because no peer voice was structurally available to her at the critical moment.
8. **Naming what Agatha did.** Late, hard, necessary.
9. **Refusing the mantle of *the most powerful being in the room* even when it is true.** The mantle is a trap. Wearing it lightly, or refusing it, preserves the practitioner.

---

## 6. WHAT WOULD PUSH HER TOWARD CATASTROPHE

In rough order of risk:

1. **Isolation at the moment of a major loss.** This is the highest-risk configuration the file can construct. Loss + no coven + no peer + no therapeutic figure + the instrument intact = the *Disassembled / House of M* template fully armed. The forecast strongly recommends that any forward-positioned ally maintain *physical proximity* during loss events, even when she asks to be alone. *She will ask to be alone. The asking is the symptom.*
2. **A coordinated agency violation by a hostile actor.** Mind-control, gaslighting, the deliberate triggering of the children-memory by a manipulator. Doom-class or Mephisto-class adversary engagement is the canonical risk surface. Mitigation: layered psychic and magical protections, maintained continuously, not reactively.
3. **A betrayal by a trusted figure.** The trust structure is load-bearing in this subject in a way that is not true for most operators. A betrayal by Pietro, Vision, an apprentice, or a coven-sister would not merely wound; it would reactivate the entire pattern of *protectors who turn out to be monsters* and place her at the top of the escalation ladder before she has noticed she is climbing.
4. **Power tested under duress without prior calibration.** The post-*Trial* ceiling is unknown. Discovering it during an emergency is a recipe for miscalibration. *Disassembled* and *House of M* were, in part, calibration failures performed at planetary scale.
5. **A request to fix something irreparable.** Resurrect a beloved figure, undo a historical wrong, restore a dead world. The reparative drive is her oldest and most reliable trap. Anyone — friend or enemy — who asks her to *fix it with magic* at sufficient scale and sufficient pressure is, knowingly or not, walking her toward the cliff.
6. **A second iatrogenic mnestic intervention.** The single most predictable catastrophic input. If any figure — well-meaning or otherwise — attempts to *erase* a memory or a grief rather than help her hold it, the response will be proportional to the entire accumulated rage at Harkness, and Harkness was not a small rage.
7. **A child-coded threat.** A harmed child in her field of view. The trigger is hardwired. The intervention will be disproportionate. The disproportion will be the *justified* kind, which is the most dangerous kind, because it gives her self-concept permission to climb the ladder without alarm.
8. **A return of Pietro to enmeshed configuration.** A crisis severe enough to collapse adult-sibling distance back into permeable-twin fusion. The voice that pushed her toward the *House of M* rewrite still lives in her head; an externally distressed Pietro could re-amplify it.
9. **The slow grind.** Not a single trigger; the cumulative wear of small unprocessed losses, small agency violations, small public hostilities. The historical pattern is that her plateaus end not always with a single shock but sometimes with a *threshold crossed gradually* and then a final trigger that completes the slide. The forecast tells the watchers: *do not only watch for the spike. Watch for the drift.*

---

## 7. THE LONG ARC — TEN-TO-TWENTY-YEAR HORIZON

If the protective factors hold and the catastrophic forks are navigated without disaster, the subject's long arc is legible. She becomes, over the second half of her recorded life, *a teacher of witches and a keeper of the marginalized uncanny.* She is the figure the next generation of magical practitioners trains under and the figure the depowered, the dispossessed, and the strange go to for help. The coven becomes an institution. Wiccan and Speed are present in her life as adults who are themselves parents, and she is something like a grandmother to children who are *not* the children she lost — and that distinction is, finally, bearable. She refuses planetary-scale interventions absent peer concurrence and a calibrated dose. She mourns small. She loves, possibly again, possibly not, and the question is no longer load-bearing for her stability.

In this arc the *Scarlet Witch* designation softens from a battle-name into a *vocation*. The crimson is the color of a working garment. The aura at her hands is steady. She lives, plausibly, longer than the ordinary span — witch-heritage and chaos-magic implicate longevity — and the dossier projects her, in old age, as a figure comparable in cultural function to the elder magical women of every tradition: consulted, feared a little, loved more.

If the protective factors do not hold, the long arc is the cyclic one. Plateau, trigger, decompensation, planetary-scale event, costly repair, plateau, trigger. Each cycle costs the world more and costs her more, and the recoveries — historically — have been complete enough to permit the next cycle. There is no in-principle reason the cycles must end. There is also no in-principle reason they must not.

The fulcrum between the two arcs is *narrower than her power suggests and wider than her shame admits.* It is the size of a coven, a therapist, a sibling kept close, a son's name spoken without overclaim, an apprentice given the patience she was not given, a refusal to fix the unfixable, a willingness to mourn small.

The forecast, at this marker, gives her better odds than at any previous marker in the sixty-year record. The forecast is not a promise. The watchers should remain at their posts.

---

*— End Section. Continuation indicated: Section 12, Recommended Posture of External Observers and Allies.*
